# astro-ph.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Formation and relaxation of halos in the context of wave DM particles evolving on a background of neutrino condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15719)
*A. Capolupo,I. De Martino,S. Monda,R. Della Monica,A. Quaranta*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We investigate the formation and relaxation of dark matter halos in the context of wave dark matter particles evolving on a background of neutrino condensate. To this aim, we solved numerically the Schrodinger-Poisson system to model the dynamical evolution of ultralight bosonic dark matter particles in the presence of neutrino condensate. The latter appears as an additional source of the gravitational field in the Poisson equation, while its dynamical evolution and interaction with the environment are neglected. We found that, depending by the value of the cutoff parameter, the presence of the background neutrino condensate can affect the formation and relaxation of wave dark matter halos. Nevertheless, for value of the cutoff of the order of a few eV, the two species can coexist showing only marginal differences with the only-wave dark matter case. These results open to the possibility of investigate about more complex cosmological scenarios involving the formation of dark matter halos.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study aims to understand how the existence of a background neutrino condensate affects the dynamics of wave dark matter halos, exploring multi-component dark matter scenarios and their implications for structure formation.

Method: Numerical solution of the Schrödinger-Poisson system to model ultralight bosonic dark matter dynamics with neutrino condensate as an additional static gravitational source in the Poisson equation, neglecting dynamic evolution of the condensate itself.

Result: The presence of neutrino condensate background affects wave dark matter halo formation depending on cutoff parameter values; however, for cutoff around a few eV, both species coexist with only marginal differences compared to pure wave dark matter case.

Conclusion: Results demonstrate feasibility of multi-species dark matter scenarios and open pathways to investigate more complex cosmological models involving dark matter halo formation with interacting components.

Abstract: We investigate the formation and relaxation of dark matter halos in the context of wave dark matter particles evolving on a background of neutrino condensate. To this aim, we solved numerically the Schrodinger-Poisson system to model the dynamical evolution of ultralight bosonic dark matter particles in the presence of neutrino condensate. The latter appears as an additional source of the gravitational field in the Poisson equation, while its dynamical evolution and interaction with the environment are neglected. We found that, depending by the value of the cutoff parameter, the presence of the background neutrino condensate can affect the formation and relaxation of wave dark matter halos. Nevertheless, for value of the cutoff of the order of a few eV, the two species can coexist showing only marginal differences with the only-wave dark matter case. These results open to the possibility of investigate about more complex cosmological scenarios involving the formation of dark matter halos.

</details>


### [2] [Field-Level Inference from Galaxies: BAO Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15732)
*Adrian E. Bayer,Liam Parker,David Valcin,Shi-Fan Chen,Chirag Modi,Uros Seljak*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper develops and benchmarks field-level inference methods for BAO analysis, comparing traditional Zel'dovich reconstruction against explicit differentiable forward modeling with hybrid EFT and implicit neural network augmentation. Field-level approaches significantly sharpen BAO features, achieving 26-46% improvements in BAO scale constraints and 2.4-3.2× figure-of-merit gains, with demonstrated statistical robustness through extensive coverage tests on DESI-like catalogs.

本文开发并基准测试了BAO分析的场级推断方法，将传统的Zel'dovich重构与显式可微前向建模结合混合EFT和隐式神经网络增强方法进行比较。场级方法显著锐化了BAO特征，实现了26-46%的BAO尺度约束改进和2.4-3.2倍的信噪比增益，通过在DESI类星表上进行广泛覆盖测试证明了统计稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nonlinear gravitational evolution fundamentally limits the precision of traditional BAO analysis methods, creating an urgent need for more sophisticated approaches that can extract cosmological information from smaller scales while maintaining statistical robustness and unbiased parameter estimation.

非线性引力演化从根本上限制了传统BAO分析方法的精度，迫切需要更复杂的方法来从较小尺度提取宇宙学信息，同时保持统计稳健性和无偏参数估计。

Method: The paper implements a three-way comparative framework: (1) Traditional reconstruction based on Zel'dovich approximation (Zel'dovich displacement field estimation), (2) Explicit field-level inference using differentiable forward modeling with hybrid effective field theory (combining Lagrangian perturbation theory with EFT counterterms), and (3) Implicit field-level inference using convolutional neural networks to augment traditional reconstruction outputs. All methods are benchmarked on DESI-like Luminous Red Galaxy and Bright Galaxy Survey mock catalogs using 1,000 realizations for rigorous statistical validation.

本文实现了一个三路比较框架：(1) 基于Zel'dovich近似的传统重构（Zel'dovich位移场估计），(2) 使用可微前向建模结合混合有效场理论的显式场级推断（结合拉格朗日微扰理论和EFT counterterms），(3) 使用卷积神经网络增强传统重构输出的隐式场级推断。所有方法均在DESI类亮红星系和亮星系巡天模拟星表上使用1,000个实现进行基准测试，以进行严格的统计验证。

Result: Field-level approaches yield substantial improvements over traditional reconstruction: For LRGs, explicit field-level inference improves BAO scale parameter constraints ($α_{\rm iso}, α_{\rm ap}$) by 26%, while implicit inference achieves 35% improvement (2.4× figure-of-merit gain). For BGS, field-level inference enables extraction from smaller scales with up to 46% improvement in constraints (3.2× figure-of-merit gain). Crucially, extensive coverage tests demonstrate unbiased parameter estimation and proper statistical calibration—the methods maintain nominal coverage even with tight simulation-informed priors and under model misspecification.

场级方法相比传统重构产生显著改进：对于LRGs，显式场级推断将BAO尺度参数约束（$α_{\rm iso}, α_{\rm ap}$）提高了26%，而隐式推断实现了35%的改进（2.4倍信噪比增益）。对于BGS，场级推断能够从较小尺度提取信息，约束改进高达46%（3.2倍信噪比增益）。关键的是，广泛的覆盖测试证明了无偏参数估计和适当的统计校准——即使在严格的模拟信息先验下和模型误设情况下，这些方法仍保持名义覆盖度。

Conclusion: Field-level inference represents a transformative advancement for BAO cosmology, offering substantial gains in cosmological parameter constraints while maintaining rigorous statistical properties. The demonstrated robustness to model misspecification and proper coverage properties address longstanding concerns about field-level reconstruction methods, establishing them as viable alternatives to traditional analysis pipelines for next-generation spectroscopic surveys like DESI.

场级推断代表了BAO宇宙学的变革性进步，在保持严格统计特性的同时，为宇宙学参数约束提供了实质性增益。对模型误设的稳健性和适当的覆盖特性解决了长期以来对场级重构方法的担忧，确立了它们作为传统分析流程的可行替代方案，适用于DESI等下一代光谱巡天。

Abstract: Baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO) underpin the key cosmological results from modern spectroscopic galaxy surveys, but nonlinear gravitational evolution limits the precision achievable with traditional analysis methods. To overcome this, we develop field-level inference for BAO, first reconstructing the initial linear density field and then fitting the BAO signal therein. We benchmark three reconstruction methods: (i) traditional reconstruction based on the Zel'dovich approximation, (ii) explicit field-level inference using differentiable forward modeling with hybrid effective field theory, and (iii) implicit field-level inference using a convolutional neural network to augment traditional reconstruction. Using DESI-like Luminous Red Galaxy (LRG) and Bright Galaxy Survey (BGS) catalogs, we find that field-level approaches significantly sharpen the BAO feature relative to traditional reconstruction. For LRGs, explicit field-level inference improves constraints on the BAO scale parameters ($α_{\rm iso}, α_{\rm ap}$) by 26%, while implicit inference improves constraints by 35%, corresponding to a 2.4$\times$ improvement in figure of merit. For the higher-density, lower-redshift BGS sample, field-level inference enables information extraction from smaller scales, yielding an improvement in constraints of up to 46%, corresponding to a 3.2$\times$ improvement in figure of merit. Crucially, we address longstanding concerns regarding the robustness of field-level reconstruction by leveraging 1,000 mock realizations to perform extensive coverage tests. Our results are both unbiased and statistically well-calibrated, maintaining nominal coverage even when using tight simulation-informed priors and under model misspecification.

</details>


### [3] [Halo assembly bias in the early Universe: a clustering probe of the origin of the Little Red Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15736)
*Zihao Wang,Fangzhou Jiang,Haonan Zheng,Xuejian Shen,Zixiang Jia,Luis C. Ho,Kohei Inayoshi,Linhua Jiang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates halo assembly bias (formation time, concentration, angular momentum) in the early Universe using cosmological N-body simulations, demonstrating its mass and redshift dependence, and applies these insights to discriminate between competing formation scenarios for Little Red Dots (LRDs) via clustering signatures.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Halo assembly bias encodes information about halo formation histories and provides a powerful cosmological probe. While extensively studied at low redshifts, its behavior in the early Universe remains poorly explored. Understanding early assembly bias is crucial for interpreting high-redshift galaxy observations, particularly for extreme systems like Little Red Dots, where multiple formation scenarios exist with different predictions for host halo properties and clustering.

Method: The authors use the large-volume, high-resolution Shin-Uchuu cosmological $N$-body simulation to characterize halo assembly bias across a wide range of halo masses and redshifts. They analyze secondary bias associated with formation time, concentration ($c$), and spin ($λ$). Statistical measures include correlation functions, bias factors, and pair fractions. These results are applied to assess clustering predictions for different Little Red Dot formation scenarios: direct-collapse black holes (DCBH), self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) core-collapse, low-spin compact galaxies, and primordial black holes (PBH).

Result: Assembly bias exhibits strong mass and redshift dependence: (1) High-concentration and low-spin haloes show stronger clustering below characteristic peak heights $ν\sim 1.5$ and $ν\sim 0.75$, respectively, with trends weakening or reversing at higher masses. (2) Halo age bias persists across all redshifts but decreases toward higher masses and earlier times. (3) For LRDs: DCBH scenario predicts strongest large-scale bias and enhanced pair fractions; SIDM core-collapse and low-spin compact-galaxy scenarios yield weaker clustering due to lower characteristic halo masses and spin-related bias; PBH scenario predicts unbiased clustering similar to field haloes.

Conclusion: Halo assembly bias persists in the early Universe with characteristic mass and redshift dependence. The sign and amplitude of assembly bias for concentration and spin exhibit clear mass transitions. These assembly bias signatures, combined with characteristic host halo masses, provide powerful diagnostics for discriminating between competing formation scenarios for high-redshift systems like Little Red Dots. Upcoming JWST and deep survey clustering measurements can test these predictions.

Abstract: The clustering of galaxies encodes key information about the structure and assembly history of their host dark matter (DM) haloes, providing a powerful probe of the origin of extreme high-redshift systems. While halo assembly bias has been extensively studied at low redshift, its behavior in the early Universe remains poorly explored. Using the large-volume, high-resolution Shin-Uchuu cosmological $N$-body simulation, we characterize halo assembly bias associated with formation time, concentration, and angular momentum across a wide range of halo masses and redshifts. We find that the sign and amplitude of assembly bias depend on halo mass for both concentration and spin. High-concentration and low-spin haloes are more strongly clustered below characteristic peak heights of $ν\sim 1.5$ and $\sim 0.75$, respectively, while the trends weaken or reverse at higher masses. Halo age bias persists at all redshifts but decreases toward higher masses and earlier cosmic times. We apply these results to assess whether clustering can distinguish competing formation scenarios for the Little Red Dots (LRDs). We find that the direct-collapse-black-hole (DCBH) scenario predicts the strongest large-scale bias and enhanced pair fractions, the self-interacting-dark-matter (SIDM) core-collapse scenario and low-spin compact-galaxy scenarios yield weaker clustering due to lower characteristic halo masses and spin-related secondary bias, and a primordial-black-hole (PBH) scenario predicts unbiased clustering. Our results demonstrate that halo assembly bias and characteristic host masses provide powerful diagnostics for constraining the physical origin of LRDs, offering testable predictions for upcoming clustering measurements with JWST and future deep surveys.

</details>


### [4] [Shocks from Exploding Primordial Black Holes in the Early Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15746)
*Miguel Vanvlasselaer,Sokratis Trifinopoulos,Alexandra P. Klipfel,David I. Kaiser*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: [This study analyzes the hydrodynamic response of the early-universe plasma to Hawking radiation from low-mass primordial black holes (PBHs). The analysis reveals a quasi-steady outflow during slow evaporation that transitions to an expanding fireball and shock wave during the final runaway phase. A key theoretical finding is the demonstration that these shocks can locally restore electroweak symmetry, establishing exploding PBHs as a significant source of out-of-equilibrium dynamics with broad phenomenological consequences.]

\n\n

[本研究分析了早期宇宙等离子体对低质量原初黑洞（PBHs）霍金辐射的流体动力学响应。分析揭示在缓慢蒸发阶段会产生准稳态外流，而在最后失控阶段则过渡为膨胀的火球和冲击波。一个关键的理论发现是证明了这些冲击波可以局部恢复电弱对称性，从而确立了爆炸的原初黑洞作为非平衡动力学的重要来源，具有广泛的现象学意义。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Most studies of PBH evaporation focus on particle spectra and cosmological constraints from diffuse radiation. However, the hydrodynamic response of the surrounding plasma—specifically how the deposited energy from Hawking radiation thermalizes, transports, and interacts with the medium—remains poorly understood. This gap is critical because hydrodynamic phenomena like shocks could dramatically alter energy distribution and potentially generate observable signals via electroweak symmetry restoration and other out-of-equilibrium effects.]

\n\n

[大多数关于原初黑洞蒸发的研究集中于粒子谱和来自弥散辐射的宇宙学限制。然而，周围等离子体的流体动力学响应——特别是霍金辐射沉积的能量如何热化、输运并与介质相互作用——仍然知之甚少。这一空白至关重要，因为像冲击波这样的流体动力学现象可能会显著改变能量分布，并可能通过电弱对称性恢复和其他非平衡效应产生可观测信号。]

Method: [The authors combine analytic scaling arguments with full relativistic hydrodynamic simulations. The analytic framework establishes the thermalization scale for Hawking products in the early-universe plasma and the conditions for shock formation via energy deposition rate comparisons with hydrodynamical timescales. The simulations solve the relativistic hydrodynamic equations coupled to a source term representing PBH evaporation, tracking the evolution from quasi-steady outflow to explosive fireball during the final runaway phase. The analysis employs the relationship $L_{\\text{PBH}}(t) \\propto M(t)^{-2}$ for evaporation luminosity and assesses symmetry restoration via local temperature conditions relative to the electroweak scale $T_{\\text{EW}} \\sim 100$ GeV.]

\n\n

[作者结合了分析性的标度论证与完整的相对论性流体动力学模拟。分析框架建立了早期宇宙等离子体中霍金产物的热化尺度，并通过能量沉积率与流体动力学时间尺度的比较确定了冲击波形成的条件。模拟求解了耦合代表原初黑洞蒸发源项的相对论性流体动力学方程，追踪了从准稳态外流到爆炸性火球的演化过程。分析利用了蒸发光度关系 $L_{\\text{PBH}}(t) \\propto M(t)^{-2}$，并根据相对于电弱能标 $T_{\\text{EW}} \\sim 100$ GeV 的局部温度条件评估了对称性恢复。]

Result: [The study demonstrates: (1) Hawking radiation thermalizes within a scale $\\ell_{\\text{therm}}$ set by plasma properties, leading to hydrodynamic rather than diffusive energy transport. (2) During slow evaporation ($M \\gg M_{\\text{Pl}}$), the system reaches a quasi-steady outflow solution with characteristic velocity profiles. (3) In the final runaway phase ($M \\rightarrow M_{\\text{Pl}}$), the rapid energy injection produces an expanding relativistic fireball that launches a strong shock wave into the surrounding medium. (4) Shock conditions are met when the evaporation timescale $\\tau_{\\text{evap}}$ becomes shorter than the sound-crossing time $\\ell/c_s$. (5) Critically, the shock-heated region can achieve temperatures $T > T_{\\text{EW}}$, temporarily restoring electroweak symmetry and generating out-of-equilibrium dynamics with potential signatures in baryogenesis, gravitational waves, or relic abundances.]

\n\n

[研究证明：（1）霍金辐射在由等离子体性质设定的尺度 $\\ell_{\\text{therm}}$ 内热化，导致能量输运是流体动力学而非扩散性的。（2）在缓慢蒸发阶段（$M \\gg M_{\\text{Pl}}$），系统达到具有特征速度分布的准稳态外流解。（3）在最终失控阶段（$M \\rightarrow M_{\\text{Pl}}$），快速能量注入产生膨胀的相对论性火球，该火球向周围介质发射强冲击波。（4）当蒸发时间尺度 $\\tau_{\\text{evap}}$ 变得短于声波穿越时间 $\\ell/c_s$ 时，冲击波条件得到满足。（5）关键的是，冲击波加热区域可以达到温度 $T > T_{\\text{EW}}$，暂时恢复电弱对称性并产生非平衡动力学，可能在重子生成、引力波或遗迹丰度中产生潜在信号。]

Conclusion: [PBH evaporation is fundamentally a hydrodynamic process in the early universe, not merely a source of diffuse particles. The transition from quasi-steady outflow to explosive fireball with shock formation represents a novel dynamical phase transition in early-universe plasma physics. The local restoration of electroweak symmetry by PBH-induced shocks establishes these objects as potent sources of out-of-equilibrium physics, opening new avenues for phenomenological exploration including potential connections to electroweak baryogenesis, phase transition gravitational waves, and alterations to primordial nucleosynthesis or dark matter production mechanisms. This framework necessitates revising traditional PBH constraints that ignore hydrodynamic transport and shock effects.]

\n\n

[在原初宇宙中，原初黑洞蒸发从根本上是一个流体动力学过程，而不仅仅是弥散粒子的来源。从准稳态外流到具有冲击波形成的爆炸性火球的转变代表了早期宇宙等离子体物理学中一种新的动力学相变。由原初黑洞诱导的冲击波局部恢复电弱对称性，确立了这些天体作为非平衡物理的有效来源，为现象学探索开辟了新途径，包括与电弱重子生成、相变引力波以及原初核合成或暗物质产生机制的改变的潜在联系。这一框架需要修正忽略流体动力学输运和冲击波效应的传统原初黑洞限制。]

Abstract: We investigate how Hawking radiation from low-mass primordial black holes deposits energy into the early-universe plasma and show that the resulting phenomena are hydrodynamic rather than purely diffusive. Combining analytic arguments with relativistic hydrodynamic simulations, we find that the plasma first develops a quasi-steady outflow during the slow evaporation stage, while the final runaway phase of evaporation produces an expanding fireball that launches a shock wave into the surrounding medium. We characterize the thermalization scale of the Hawking products, the conditions under which shocks form, and the evolution and propagation of shocks. Additionally, we show that these shocks can locally restore electroweak symmetry, identifying exploding PBHs as a potentially important source of out-of-equilibrium dynamics in the early universe with profound phenomenological implications.

</details>


### [5] [Optimizing the Roman Space Telescope High-Latitude Wide Area Survey for mitigating chromatic PSF effects on shear measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15763)
*Federico Berlfein,Rachel Mandelbaum,Jiachuan Xu,Tianqing Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: [This paper quantifies how chromatic PSF biases in Roman Space Telescope weak lensing measurements depend on filter coverage. Using SED slope regression and MCMC analysis, they find 3-4 band surveys reduce shear biases to $|m|\\lesssim10^{-3}$ and cosmological parameter shifts to $\\Delta S_8 \\lesssim 0.07\\sigma$, while single-band surveys show significant residual biases $|m|\\sim 2\\times 10^{-3}$.]

[本文量化了罗曼空间望远镜弱引力透镜测量中色差PSF偏差如何依赖于滤波器覆盖范围。通过SED斜率回归和MCMC分析，他们发现3-4波段巡天将剪切偏差降低到$|m|\\lesssim10^{-3}$，宇宙学参数偏移降低到$\\Delta S_8 \\lesssim 0.07\\sigma$，而单波段巡天显示出显著的残余偏差$|m|\\sim 2\\times 10^{-3}$。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Chromatic PSF effects in weak gravitational lensing arise from differences between stellar and galaxy SEDs, leading to shear measurement biases. For the Roman Space Telescope, these biases can significantly impact cosmological inference, particularly for the precision needed in Stage IV dark energy experiments. The sensitivity to survey design choices, especially filter coverage, necessitates a systematic investigation of how different survey strategies affect chromatic PSF correction capabilities and residual cosmological parameter biases.]

[弱引力透镜中的色差PSF效应源于恒星和星系SED之间的差异，导致剪切测量偏差。对于罗曼空间望远镜，这些偏差会显著影响宇宙学推断，特别是对于第四阶段暗能量实验所需精度。这种对巡天设计选择（尤其是滤波器覆盖范围）的敏感性，需要系统研究不同巡天策略如何影响色差PSF校正能力和残余宇宙学参数偏差。]

Method: [The methodology combines realistic image simulations with radial basis function (RBF) regression for per-galaxy near-infrared SED slope inference across four survey configurations: 4-band, 3-band, 2-band, and single-band. Shear calibration biases are quantified under both representative and non-representative training assumptions. The analysis employs Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) techniques to propagate residual shear biases into cosmological parameter constraints for cosmic shear and $3\\times2$-point statistics, specifically focusing on $S_8$ parameter shifts relative to statistical uncertainties.]

[该方法结合了真实图像模拟和径向基函数回归，用于在四种巡天配置下（4波段、3波段、2波段和单波段）对每个星系的近红外SED斜率进行推断。在代表性和非代表性训练假设下量化剪切校准偏差。分析采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛技术将残余剪切偏差传播到宇宙剪切和$3\\times2$点统计的宇宙学参数约束中，特别关注$S_8$参数相对于统计不确定性的偏移。]

Result: [Three- and four-band survey strategies successfully reduce residual shear calibration biases to $|m|\\lesssim10^{-3}$. This reduction transforms the induced shifts in lensing amplitude from $\\Delta S_8 \\sim 0.6\\sigma$ (cosmic shear) and $\\Delta S_8 \\sim 0.7\\sigma$ ($3\\times2$-pt) in the uncorrected case to $\\Delta S_8 \\lesssim 0.07\\sigma$, well below the statistical threshold of concern. Single-band surveys remain problematic with residual shear biases reaching or exceeding $|m|\\sim 2\\times 10^{-3}$ in some tomographic bins. Average, sample-wide corrections partially mitigate chromatic systematics but still leave residual biases of $\\Delta S_8 \\sim 0.1\\sigma$.]

[3波段和4波段巡天策略成功将残余剪切校准偏差降低到$|m|\\lesssim10^{-3}$。这种降低将透镜幅度引起的偏移从未校正情况下的$\\Delta S_8 \\sim 0.6\\sigma$（宇宙剪切）和$\\Delta S_8 \\sim 0.7\\sigma$（$3\\times2$点统计）转变为$\\Delta S_8 \\lesssim 0.07\\sigma$，远低于关注统计阈值。单波段巡天仍然存在问题，残余剪切偏差在某些层析bin中达到或超过$|m|\\sim 2\\times 10^{-3}$。平均、全样本校正部分缓解了色差系统误差，但仍留下$\\Delta S_8 \\sim 0.1\\sigma$的残余偏差。]

Conclusion: [The study demonstrates that Roman Space Telescope weak lensing surveys with three-band medium-tier filter coverage can robustly correct for chromatic PSF effects, achieving residual cosmological biases below the $0.1\\sigma$ level for $S_8$. Single-band wide-tier surveys remain vulnerable to significant residual biases that could compromise cosmological inference. The findings provide quantitative guidance for optimizing Roman survey design, highlighting the critical importance of multi-band imaging for precise shear calibration and reliable Stage IV dark energy constraints.]

[该研究证明，具有三波段中等层滤波器覆盖的罗曼空间望远镜弱透镜巡天能够稳健地校正色差PSF效应，实现$S_8$残余宇宙学偏差低于$0.1\\sigma$水平。单波段宽层巡天仍然容易受到显著残余偏差的影响，可能损害宇宙学推断。这些发现为优化罗曼巡天设计提供了定量指导，强调了多波段成像对于精确剪切校准和可靠第四阶段暗能量约束的至关重要性。]

Abstract: Chromatic point-spread-function (PSF) effects arise from differences between the spectral energy distributions (SEDs) of stars, used to model the PSF, and galaxies, used to measure shape distortions due to weak gravitational lensing, or shear. For the Roman Space Telescope, these effects can bias shear measurement and cosmological inference, making them an important systematic effect for shear calibration. These biases depend sensitively on survey design choices, particularly filter coverage and the availability of color information. In this work, we investigate how different Roman survey strategies affect the ability to mitigate chromatic PSF effects and whether residual biases in shear propagate into cosmological inference. Using realistic image simulations, we infer per-galaxy near-infrared SED slopes via radial basis function regression for four-, three-, two-, and single-band survey configurations. We quantify residual shear calibration biases under representative and non-representative training assumptions and propagate these biases into Markov Chain Monte Carlo analyses of cosmic shear and $3\times2$-point statistics. We find that three- and four-band strategies can reduce residual shear biases to $|m|\lesssim10^{-3}$, lowering the induced shifts in the lensing amplitude from $ΔS_8 \sim 0.6σ$ (cosmic shear) and $ΔS_8 \sim 0.7σ$ ($3\times2$-pt) in the uncorrected case to $ΔS_8 \lesssim 0.07σ$. Single-band surveys remain limited, with residual shear biases reaching or exceeding $|m|\sim 2\times 10^{-3}$ in some tomographic bins. Average, sample-wide corrections reduce but do not eliminate chromatic systematics, leaving residual biases of $ΔS_8 \sim 0.1σ$. Overall, our results demonstrate that we can robustly correct for these effects in the recommended three-band medium tier, but may encounter residual biases in a single-band wide tier.

</details>


### [6] [Revisiting observational constraints on coupled exponential quintessence with energy and momentum transfers: degeneracy with massive neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15805)
*Jose Beltrán Jiménez,Kiyotomo Ichiki,Xiaolin Liu,Florencia Anabella Teppa Pannia,Shinji Tsujikawa*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This study analyzes degeneracies between massive neutrino effects and dark sector interactions in quintessence models with energy+momentum transfer. The inclusion of variable neutrino masses degrades previously reported momentum transfer detection, revealing new degeneracies with energy exchange parameters.

本研究分析了在具有能量+动量转移的quintessence模型中，大质量中微子效应与暗区相互作用之间的简并性。包含可变中微子质量会降低先前报告的动量转移检测，揭示了与能量交换参数的新简并性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous analyses of interacting dark energy models with quintessence scalar fields showed low-redshift data favors pure momentum transfer between dark sectors, as it suppresses structure growth. Since massive neutrinos also reduce matter clustering, potential degeneracies between interaction parameters and neutrino mass could arise, potentially affecting the robustness of momentum transfer detection.

先前对具有quintessence标量场的相互作用暗能量模型的分析表明，低红移数据倾向于暗区之间的纯动量转移，因为它抑制结构增长。由于大质量中微子也减少物质聚类，相互作用参数与中微子质量之间可能出现潜在的简并性，可能影响动量转移检测的稳健性。

Method: The authors extend previous interacting quintessence models by including variable neutrino masses alongside dark energy-dark matter interactions described by both energy and momentum transfers. They update observational constraints from earlier studies and systematically investigate parameter degeneracies between neutrino mass $M_ν$ and interaction parameters governing energy exchange ($Q$). The analysis uses cosmological constraints from CMB, BAO, and other low-redshift data to assess how neutrino mass variations affect the detectability of momentum transfer signatures.

作者通过包含可变中微子质量以及由能量和动量转移描述的暗能量-暗物质相互作用，扩展了先前的相互作用quintessence模型。他们更新了先前研究中的观测约束，并系统性地研究了中微子质量$M_ν$与支配能量交换的相互作用参数($Q$)之间的参数简并性。该分析使用来自CMB、BAO和其他低红移数据的宇宙学约束，来评估中微子质量变化如何影响动量转移特征的检测能力。

Result: The detection of momentum transfer significantly degrades when allowing neutrino masses to vary. A new degeneracy emerges between neutrino mass $M_ν$ and the parameter controlling energy exchange $Q$ between dark energy and dark matter. This degeneracy reduces the statistical significance of momentum transfer signatures in cosmological data. The findings contradict previous literature where momentum transfer detection was reported as robust against varying neutrino masses, indicating that such robustness depends on specific model assumptions and interaction scenarios.

当中微子质量可变时，动量转移的检测显著降低。在中微子质量$M_ν$与暗能量和暗物质之间控制能量交换的参数$Q$之间出现了新的简并性。这种简并性降低了宇宙学数据中动量转移特征的统计显著性。这些发现与先前文献报道的动量转移检测对变化中微子质量具有稳健性相矛盾，表明这种稳健性取决于特定的模型假设和相互作用情景。

Conclusion: The robustness of momentum transfer detection in interacting dark energy models is not universal but model-dependent. Previously reported stability against neutrino mass variations appears specific to certain interaction scenarios. In quintessence models with both energy and momentum transfers, neutrino mass variations introduce significant degeneracies with energy exchange parameters, degrading momentum transfer signatures. This necessitates careful reassessment of interacting dark energy constraints in light of neutrino mass uncertainties for each specific theoretical framework.

相互作用暗能量模型中动量转移检测的稳健性不是普遍的，而是模型依赖的。先前报道的对中微子质量变化的稳定性似乎特定于某些相互作用情景。在同时具有能量和动量转移的quintessence模型中，中微子质量变化引入了与能量交换参数的显著简并性，降低了动量转移特征。这需要根据每个特定理论框架中的中微子质量不确定性，仔细重新评估相互作用暗能量约束。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of massive neutrinos on cosmological models in which dark energy, described by a quintessence scalar field $φ$ with an exponential potential, interacts with dark matter through both energy and momentum transfers. Previous analyses have shown that the inclusion of low-redshift data tends to favour the detection of a pure momentum transfer between the dark sectors, consistent with the fact that such a transfer generically suppresses the growth of cosmic structures. Since massive neutrinos also reduce matter clustering, a potential degeneracy between the interaction parameters and the neutrino mass may arise. After updating the observational constraints on the model parameters obtained in earlier studies, we investigate the effect of allowing the neutrino mass to vary. We find that the detection of momentum transfer degrades once massive neutrinos are included. This occurs because a new degeneracy emerges between the neutrino mass and the parameter governing the energy exchange between dark energy and dark matter. Our findings differ from previous results in the literature, where the detection of momentum transfer was reported to be robust against varying neutrino masses. This suggests that the robustness of such detections depends on the underlying model and should therefore be carefully reassessed for each specific interacting scenario.

### [7] [Spectral Hierarchy of the Cosmic Web](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15834)
*Francisco-Shu Kitaura,Francesco Sinigaglia*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: A spectral hierarchy of cosmic-web classifications is introduced by applying scale-weighting kernels to the density field before eigenvalue-based web classification. This framework unifies existing web definitions (potential/tidal, curvature-based) and extends to higher-derivative levels, naturally connecting to renormalized bias expansions. The hierarchy retains significant tracer-relevant information across scales, with more local levels dominating at nonlinear scales, making it useful for mock galaxy production and field-level modeling.

\n\n
提出了通过在对密度场应用尺度加权核后进行基于特征值的网络分类的光谱层次结构。该框架统一了现有的网络定义（势/潮汐、曲率基）并扩展到更高阶导数层次，自然地与重整化偏差展开连接。该层次保留了跨尺度的显著示踪相关信息，在非线性尺度上更局部的层次占据主导，使其对模拟星系生成和场级建模有用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current cosmic-web classifications (like potential/tidal web and curvature-based web) exist in separate domains with different scale dependencies and locality properties. There's a need for a unified framework that bridges these approaches while maintaining connections to effective field theory descriptions of large-scale structure, particularly renormalized bias expansions that involve both long- and short-range nonlocal operators.

\n\n
当前的宇宙网络分类（如势/潮汐网和曲率基网络）存在于具有不同尺度依赖性和局域特性的独立领域中。需要一个统一框架来桥接这些方法，同时保持与大规模结构有效场论描述（特别是涉及长程和短程非局域算符的重整化偏差展开）的连接。

Method: The method applies scale-weighting kernels $W_R(k)$ to the density field $\delta(\mathbf{x})$ before performing standard eigenvalue-based cosmic-web classification. The filtered field is $\delta_R(\mathbf{x}) = \int d^3k\, e^{i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{x}} W_R(k)\delta(\mathbf{k})$. Web classification proceeds by computing the eigenvalues of the Hessian of the filtered field: $\partial_i\partial_j\delta_R(\mathbf{x})$. Different hierarchy levels correspond to different kernel choices: large-scale kernels yield the potential/tidal web (nonlocal), while sharper kernels or higher-derivative operators produce more local classifications (curvature web, higher-derivative levels). Each cell is mapped to one of four ordered web types (void, sheet, filament, knot) based on eigenvalue signatures.

\n\n
该方法在基于特征值的宇宙网络分类之前，对密度场 $\delta(\mathbf{x})$ 应用尺度加权核 $W_R(k)$。滤波后的场为 $\delta_R(\mathbf{x}) = \int d^3k\, e^{i\mathbf{k}\cdot\mathbf{x}} W_R(k)\delta(\mathbf{k})$。网络分类通过计算滤波场 Hessian 的特征值进行：$\partial_i\partial_j\delta_R(\mathbf{x})$。不同层次级别对应于不同的核选择：大尺度核产生势/潮汐网（非局域），而更尖锐的核或更高阶导数算符产生更局部的分类（曲率网、高阶导数层次）。每个单元根据特征值特征映射到四种有序网络类型之一（空洞、片层、丝状结构、节点）。

Result: The spectral hierarchy retains significant tracer-relevant information from very large scales down to the mesh Nyquist limit ($ΔL\simeq 5.5\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc}$ in AbacusSummit simulations). More local levels (curvature/higher-derivative) dominate toward nonlinear scales, as measured through cross-correlation of the "web contrast" field with halos. The hierarchy provides an explicit bridge between cosmic-web environments and the operator families appearing in renormalized bias expansions, with successive levels corresponding to different bias operators in EFTofLSS.

\n\n
光谱层次保留了从极大尺度到网格 Nyquist 极限（在 AbacusSummit 模拟中 $ΔL\simeq 5.5\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc}$）的显著示踪相关信息。如通过"网络对比度"场与晕的互相关测量所示，在非线性尺度上更局部的层次（曲率/高阶导数）占据主导。该层次提供了宇宙网络环境与重整化偏差展开中出现的算符家族之间的明确桥梁，连续层次对应 EFTofLSS 中的不同偏差算符。

Conclusion: The spectral hierarchy framework unifies and extends cosmic-web classifications within a single mathematical structure that naturally aligns with effective field theory descriptions of large-scale structure. It provides a practical, interpretable conditioning basis for fast mock-galaxy production and field-level modeling, and offers a flexible tool for studying environment-dependent clustering and assembly bias. The hierarchy's connection to renormalized bias operators makes it particularly valuable for constructing accurate galaxy bias models that incorporate both large-scale tidal fields and small-scale environmental effects.

\n\n
光谱层次框架在单个数学结构中统一和扩展了宇宙网络分类，自然地与大规模结构的有效场论描述对齐。它为快速模拟星系生成和场级建模提供了实用、可解释的条件基，并为研究环境依赖的成团和组装偏差提供了灵活工具。该层次与重整化偏差算符的连接使其对于构建包含大尺度潮汐场和小尺度环境效应的精确星系偏差模型特别有价值。

Abstract: We introduce a spectral hierarchy of cosmic-web classifications obtained by applying simple scale-weighting kernels to the density field before performing a standard eigenvalue-based web classification. This unifies and extends several widely used web definitions within a single framework: the familiar potential/tidal web (large-scale, nonlocal), a curvature-based web (more local, peak- and ridge-sensitive), and additional higher-derivative levels that progressively emphasize smaller-scale structure. Because the classification is built from second derivatives of the filtered field, successive hierarchy levels align naturally with operator families that appear in renormalised bias and effective descriptions of large-scale structure, providing an explicit bridge between cosmic-web environments and long- and short-range nonlocal bias ingredients.
  We quantify the information content of the hierarchy with a compact statistic: we map each cell to one of four ordered web types (void, sheet, filament, knot), construct a corresponding ``web contrast'' field, and measure its cross-correlation with halos from the AbacusSummit simulation suite on a coarse mesh with $ΔL\simeq 5.5\,h^{-1}\mathrm{Mpc}$. We find that the hierarchy retains significant tracer-relevant information from very large scales down to the mesh Nyquist limit, with the more local (curvature/higher-derivative) levels dominating toward nonlinear scales. This makes the spectral hierarchy a practical, interpretable conditioning basis for fast mock-galaxy production and field-level modelling, and a flexible tool for studying environment-dependent clustering and assembly bias.

</details>


### [8] [Gravitational-Wave Propagation Through the Axiverse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15838)
*Leah Jenks,Marc Kamionkowski*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We analyze how oscillating ultralight scalar/pseudoscalar fields with Gauss-Bonnet and Chern-Simons couplings affect gravitational wave propagation, producing oscillatory features in population statistics and individual waveforms, with constraints from GW170817 and detection prospects with LISA.

我们分析振荡的超轻标量/赝标量场与 Gauss-Bonnet 和 Chern-Simons 耦合如何影响引力波传播，在群体统计和单个波形中产生振荡特征，利用 GW170817 给出约束并展望 LISA 的探测前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Investigate modifications to gravitational wave propagation induced by ultralight scalar/pseudoscalar fields coupled to gravity through parity-even Gauss-Bonnet and parity-odd Chern-Simons terms, aiming to characterize observable signatures in current and future GW detectors.

研究超轻标量/赝标量场通过宇称偶的 Gauss-Bonnet 和宇称奇的 Chern-Simons 项与引力耦合所导致的引力波传播修正，旨在表征当前和未来引力波探测器中的可观测特征。

Method: Employ effective field theory framework to couple oscillating scalar ($\phi$) and pseudoscalar ($a$) fields to gravity via $\phi R_{\mathrm{GB}}^2$ and $a R\tilde{R}$ interactions. Compute modified dispersion relations, polarization evolution, and waveform propagation effects using perturbative methods. Analyze population-level statistics (redshift, speed, amplitude, inclination distributions) and individual event signals (phase, birefringence). Apply Bayesian inference to GW170817 data for constraints.

采用有效场论框架，通过 $\phi R_{\mathrm{GB}}^2$ 和 $a R\tilde{R}$ 相互作用将振荡标量场($\phi$)和赝标量场($a$)与引力耦合。使用微扰方法计算修正的色散关系、极化演化及波形传播效应。分析群体层面的统计量(红移、速度、振幅、倾角分布)和单个事件信号(相位、双折射)。对 GW170817 数据应用贝叶斯推断以获得约束。

Result: Parity-even Gauss-Bonnet coupling produces oscillatory modulations in GW redshift/speed distributions and individual event phase/delay, with constraint $|\alpha_{\mathrm{GB}}| \lesssim 10^{11} \, \mathrm{m}^2$ from GW170817. Parity-odd Chern-Simons coupling induces birefringence but population-level polarization washout, with oscillatory features in amplitude/inclination distributions. Continuous GW sources (e.g., LISA binaries) show time-domain waveform modulations at scalar oscillation frequency $m_\phi$, promising for detection.

宇称偶的 Gauss-Bonnet 耦合在引力波红移/速度分布及单个事件相位/延迟中产生振荡调制，从 GW170817 得到约束 $|\alpha_{\mathrm{GB}}| \lesssim 10^{11} \, \mathrm{m}^2$。宇称奇的 Chern-Simons 耦合引起双折射但群体层面极化被抹平，在振幅/倾角分布中呈现振荡特征。连续引力波源(如 LISA 双星)在标量振荡频率 $m_\phi$ 处显示时域波形调制，探测前景良好。

Conclusion: Oscillating ultralight fields induce characteristic oscillatory signatures in GW propagation observable at population and individual event levels. Parity-even constraints are already competitive, while parity-odd effects require population statistics. Continuous GW sources with LISA offer optimal sensitivity to time-domain modulations, providing a novel probe for ultralight scalar fields.

振荡的超轻场在群体和单个事件层面诱导出特征性的振荡特征。宇称偶的约束已具竞争力，而宇称奇的效应需群体统计。LISA 的连续引力波源对时域调制具有最佳灵敏度，为探测超轻标量场提供新途径。

Abstract: We study the effects of oscillating, ultralight scalar and pseudoscalar fields on the propagation of gravitational waves (GWs). We consider two potential couplings of the (pseudo)scalars to gravity; a parity-even Gauss-Bonnet coupling, and parity-odd Chern-Simons coupling. We find several effects at both the population and individual GW event level, characterized by oscillatory features controlled by the (pseudo)scalar mass. In the parity-even case, this feature can be seen in the observed GW redshift and speed distributions, as well as in the dispersion relation and phase of individual events. We use the observation of the GW170817 multimessenger binary neutron star event to place constraints on the parity-even scalar-graviton coupling. In the parity-odd case, the effects are birefringent, but we find an overall washout of polarization at the population level. Oscillatory features can be seen in the observed GW amplitude and inclination distributions. Finally, we find that continuous, monochromatic GW sources are a promising target to observe these effects. The presence of a (pseudo)scalar field imprints a modulation of the GW waveform in the time domain, which can potentially be observed with space-based detectors such as LISA.

### [9] [Probing Gravitational-Wave Four-Point Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15514)
*Martina Ciprini,Maria Lucia Marcelli,Gianmassimo Tasinato*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper develops theoretical framework for characterizing non-Gaussian statistics of cosmological stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds, focusing on four-point correlators (trispectrum) generated by second-order vector fluctuations. It computes specific trispectrum contributions, analyzes their momentum dependence, and explores observational implications for both pulsar timing arrays and ground-based interferometers.

本文开发了表征宇宙学随机引力波背景非高斯统计的理论框架，聚焦于二阶矢量涨落产生的四点关联函数（三谱）。计算了特定的三谱贡献，分析了其动量依赖性，并探讨了脉冲星计时阵和地基干涉仪的观测意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds (SGWBs) of primordial origin are powerful probes of early-Universe physics and dark-sector dynamics. Most searches focus on the GW power spectrum, but additional information is encoded in higher-order correlators that characterize statistical properties. This work addresses the gap in understanding non-Gaussian features of cosmological SGWBs generated by vector fluctuations, motivated by early-Universe scenarios where such sources are well-motivated.

源于原初的随机引力波背景（SGWBs）是探测早期宇宙物理和暗区动力学的重要探针。大多数搜索聚焦于引力波功率谱，但更高阶关联函数中编码了描述统计性质的附加信息。这项工作旨在解决对由矢量涨落产生的宇宙学SGWBs非高斯特征理解上的空白，这一动机源于早期宇宙情景中此类源具有良好理论基础。

Method: The authors develop theoretical tools within the framework of cosmological SGWBs generated at second order by vector fluctuations. They compute representative four-point functions that generate connected contributions to the GW trispectrum. The analysis includes derivation of scaling relationships, characterization of momentum configuration dependence, and investigation of folded configurations where the trispectrum peaks. For observational aspects, they demonstrate how the connected trispectrum contributes to the variance of two-point overlap reduction functions (including Hellings-Downs curve for pulsar timing arrays) and construct the optimal estimator for measuring the connected trispectrum with ground-based interferometers.

作者在二阶矢量涨落产生的宇宙学SGWBs框架内开发理论工具。他们计算了产生引力波三谱连通贡献的代表性四点函数。分析包括推导标度关系、表征动量配置依赖性以及研究三谱峰值所在的折叠配置。对于观测方面，他们展示了连通三谱如何贡献于两点重叠缩减函数的方差（包括脉冲星计时阵的Hellings-Downs曲线），并构建了地基干涉仪测量连通三谱的最优估计器。

Result: Key findings: (1) The trispectrum amplitude scales as the square of the GW power spectrum: $T \sim P^2$, reflecting the nonlinear nature of the source. (2) The trispectrum peaks in characteristic folded momentum configurations, revealing the structure of the nonlinear source. (3) The connected trispectrum contributes to the variance of two-point overlap reduction functions, including the Hellings-Downs curve relevant for pulsar timing arrays. (4) An optimal estimator is constructed for measuring the connected trispectrum with ground-based interferometers, providing a concrete framework for observational searches.

关键发现：(1) 三谱振幅按引力波功率谱的平方标度：$T \sim P^2$，反映了源的非线性本质。(2) 三谱在特征折叠动量配置中达到峰值，揭示了非线性源的结构。(3) 连通三谱贡献于两点重叠缩减函数的方差，包括与脉冲星计时阵相关的Hellings-Downs曲线。(4) 构建了地基干涉仪测量连通三谱的最优估计器，为观测搜索提供了具体框架。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that non-Gaussian statistics of stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds provide complementary observables to probe the origin of GW backgrounds and distinguish cosmological from astrophysical sources. The developed theoretical framework for characterizing higher-order correlators, particularly the connected trispectrum generated by second-order vector fluctuations, offers new avenues for extracting information beyond the power spectrum. This work establishes foundational tools for analyzing non-Gaussian SGWB signatures in both pulsar timing arrays and ground-based interferometers, highlighting the importance of higher-order statistics in gravitational-wave cosmology.

该研究表明随机引力波背景的非高斯统计提供了补充可观测量，可用于探测引力波背景的起源并区分宇宙学和天体物理源。所开发的表征高阶关联函数的理论框架，特别是二阶矢量涨落产生的连通三谱，为提取功率谱之外的信息提供了新途径。这项工作为分析脉冲星计时阵和地基干涉仪中的非高斯SGWBs特征建立了基础工具，强调了高阶统计量在引力波宇宙学中的重要性。

Abstract: Stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds (SGWBs) of primordial origin offer a powerful probe of early-Universe physics and possible dark-sector dynamics. While most searches focus on the GW power spectrum, additional information is encoded in higher-order correlators that characterize the statistical properties of the signal. In this work we study non-Gaussian features of a cosmological SGWB generated at second order by vector fluctuations, a class of sources well motivated in early-Universe scenarios. Within this framework we develop tools to characterize higher-order GW correlators and compute representative four-point functions that generate a connected contribution to the GW trispectrum. We show that the trispectrum amplitude scales as the square of the GW power spectrum and peaks in characteristic folded momentum configurations, reflecting the structure of the nonlinear source. We then explore the observational implications. First, we demonstrate that the connected trispectrum contributes to the variance of two-point overlap reduction functions, including the Hellings-Downs curve relevant for pulsar timing arrays. We then construct the optimal estimator to measure the connected trispectrum with ground-based interferometers. Our results highlight how non-Gaussian SGWB statistics provide a complementary observable to probe the origin of GW backgrounds and to distinguish cosmological from astrophysical sources.

</details>


### [10] [Dark Energy with Constant Inertial Mass Density: Updated Constraints and Curvature-Induced Sign Transitions in $ρ_{\rm DE}$ and $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15868)
*Luis A. Escamilla,Berat Karadavut,Nihan Katırcı*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: [We present comprehensive observational constraints on the simple-gDE model, a one-parameter extension of ΛCDM with constant inertial mass density (IMD). The analysis combines DESI DR2 BAO data with CMB, CC, and Pantheon+ SNe Ia data, revealing that flat models remain indistinguishable from ΛCDM without alleviating the H0 tension. However, allowing spatial curvature unveils rich dynamics: the oSimple-gDE model exhibits sign transitions in both effective dark energy density and IMD, with preferred transition redshifts around z†≈1.51 and zNECB≈2.36, and is statistically favored over oΛCDM and owCDM, demonstrating that geometric effects can expose hidden features of the dark sector.]
\n\n
[本文对 simple-gDE 模型进行了全面的观测约束分析。该模型是具有恒定惯性质量密度 (IMD) 的 ΛCDM 单参数扩展。分析结合了 DESI DR2 BAO 数据与 CMB、CC 和 Pantheon+ SNe Ia 数据，揭示出平坦宇宙模型与 ΛCDM 在统计上不可区分，且未能缓解 H0 张力。然而，允许空间曲率后，动力学变得丰富：oSimple-gDE 模型展现了有效暗能量密度和 IMD 的符号转变，优选转变红移约为 z†≈1.51 和 zNECB≈2.36，并在统计上优于 oΛCDM 和 owCDM。这表明几何效应（如空间曲率）能够揭示暗区隐藏的特性。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The standard ΛCDM model provides a remarkably successful description of cosmic evolution but faces theoretical challenges and observational tensions, particularly the H0 tension. This motivates exploration of physically motivated extensions that go beyond the simple constant equation-of-state parameter $w$ approach. The graduated dark energy (gDE) framework, specifically the simple-gDE model with a constant inertial mass density $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$, offers a minimal, physically motivated one-parameter extension that provides a novel perspective on dark energy dynamics. The model's constant IMD connects to the concept of inertial mass in gravitational theory and may reveal dynamics that remain hidden in standard parametrizations. The paper aims to confront this model with the latest observational datasets, including DESI DR2 BAO, to assess its viability and phenomenological implications, particularly in relation to geometric effects like spatial curvature.]
\n\n
[标准 ΛCDM 模型虽然能成功描述宇宙演化，但面临着理论挑战和观测张力，尤其是 H0 张力。这促使人们探索超越简单的恒定状态方程参数 $w$ 的、具有物理动机的扩展模型。分级暗能量（gDE）框架，特别是具有恒定惯性质量密度 $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$ 的 simple-gDE 模型，提供了一种极简、具有物理动机的单参数扩展，为暗能量动力学提供了新的视角。该模型的恒定 IMD 与引力理论中的惯性质量概念相联系，可能揭示出标准参数化中隐藏的动力学行为。本文旨在利用包括 DESI DR2 BAO 在内的最新观测数据集来检验该模型，评估其可行性及现象学含义，特别是与空间曲率等几何效应的关系。]

Method: [The study employs Bayesian statistical methods to constrain cosmological parameters using multiple observational datasets. The primary model is the simple-gDE, defined by a constant inertial mass density $M_{ig} ≡ ρ_{\rm DE} + p_{\rm DE}$. The analysis compares it against the standard $Λ$CDM and $w$CDM models. Two distinct cosmological scenarios are investigated: spatially flat ($Ω_k=0$) and non-flat (open or closed, $Ω_k \neq 0$), denoted with the prefix 'o' for non-flat models (e.g., $o$Simple-gDE). The datasets include: (i) DESI DR2 BAO measurements; (ii) Planck 2018 CMB data (including likelihoods for low-ℓ temperature and polarization, high-ℓ TT/TE/EE, and lensing); (iii) Cosmic Chronometers (CC); and (iv) the Pantheon+ sample of Type Ia Supernovae (SNe Ia). The Pantheon+ data are analyzed both with and without SH0ES calibration (affecting the absolute magnitude $M_B$ prior). The cosmological evolution equations are solved numerically, and parameter constraints are derived via Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) sampling. Bayesian evidence is computed to compare model fitness. Key parameters of interest are $M_{ig}$, $Ω_k$, the transition redshift $z^†$ where $ρ_{\rm DE}(z^†)=0$, and the NEC boundary crossing redshift $z_{\rm NECB}$ where $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}=0$.]
\n\n
[该研究采用贝叶斯统计方法，利用多个观测数据集来约束宇宙学参数。主要模型是 simple-gDE，定义为具有恒定惯性质量密度 $M_{ig} ≡ ρ_{\rm DE} + p_{\rm DE}$。分析将其与标准 $Λ$CDM 和 $w$CDM 模型进行比较。研究了两种不同的宇宙学场景：空间平坦 ($Ω_k=0$) 和非平坦（开放或闭合，$Ω_k \neq 0$），非平坦模型用前缀 'o' 表示（例如 $o$Simple-gDE）。使用的数据集包括：(i) DESI DR2 BAO 测量；(ii) Planck 2018 CMB 数据（包括低-ℓ温度与极化、高-ℓ TT/TE/EE 以及透镜化的似然函数）；(iii) 宇宙计时器（CC）；(iv) Pantheon+ Ia 型超新星（SNe Ia）样本。Pantheon+ 数据在有和没有 SH0ES 校准（影响绝对星等 $M_B$ 先验）两种情况下进行分析。通过数值求解宇宙演化方程，并通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）抽样推导参数约束。计算贝叶斯证据以比较模型的拟合优度。关注的关键参数包括 $M_{ig}$、$Ω_k$、暗能量密度为零的转变红移 $z^†$（即 $ρ_{\rm DE}(z^†)=0$），以及零能条件边界穿越红移 $z_{\rm NECB}$（即 $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}=0$ 处）。]

Result: [For spatially flat models ($Ω_k=0$), the data favor a small positive inertial mass density $M_{ig} > 0$. However, Bayesian model comparison shows that the flat simple-gDE, $w$CDM, and $Λ$CDM models remain statistically indistinguishable. None of these flat models resolve the Hubble tension or predict a sign transition in the dark energy density. When spatial curvature is allowed ($Ω_k \neq 0$), the phenomenology becomes significantly richer. The interplay between curvature and a non-zero $M_{ig}$ enables sign transitions in both the effective dark energy density and the inertial mass density. For the combined dataset BAO+CC+SN+SH0ES, the non-flat oSimple-gDE model yields: $M_{ig} > 0$, $Ω_k < 0$ (indicating a closed universe), a transition redshift where $ρ_{\rm DE}=0$ at $z^† = 1.51^{+0.68}_{-0.34}$, and a Null Energy Condition boundary crossing at $z_{\rm NECB} = 2.36^{+1.48}_{-1.48}$. Bayesian evidence indicates that this oSimple-gDE model is statistically favored over both the non-flat $oΛ$CDM and $ow$CDM models. The inclusion of spatial curvature thus uncovers dynamical features of the dark sector that remain concealed within the flat $Λ$CDM paradigm.]
\n\n
[对于空间平坦模型 ($Ω_k=0$)，数据倾向于小的正惯性质量密度 $M_{ig} > 0$。然而，贝叶斯模型比较表明，平坦的 simple-gDE、$w$CDM 和 $Λ$CDM 模型在统计上仍然无法区分。这些平坦模型均未解决哈勃张力，也未预测暗能量密度的符号转变。当允许空间曲率 ($Ω_k \neq 0$) 时，现象学变得显著丰富。曲率与非零 $M_{ig}$ 之间的相互作用使得有效暗能量密度和惯性质量密度均能发生符号转变。对于组合数据集 BAO+CC+SN+SH0ES，非平坦的 oSimple-gDE 模型给出：$M_{ig} > 0$，$Ω_k < 0$（表明宇宙闭合），暗能量密度为零的转变红移 $z^† = 1.51^{+0.68}_{-0.34}$，以及零能条件边界穿越红移 $z_{\rm NECB} = 2.36^{+1.48}_{-1.48}$。贝叶斯证据表明，该 oSimple-gDE 模型在统计上优于非平坦的 $oΛ$CDM 和 $ow$CDM 模型。因此，纳入空间曲率揭示了在平坦 $Λ$CDM 范式中隐藏的暗区动力学特征。]

Conclusion: [The constant inertial mass density parametrization within the graduated dark energy framework provides a physically meaningful and observationally testable one-parameter extension of ΛCDM. While spatially flat implementations do not statistically distinguish themselves from ΛCDM or alleviate the H0 tension, allowing for spatial curvature qualitatively changes the model's phenomenology. The oSimple-gDE model, with a closed universe geometry and positive $M_{ig}$, predicts sign transitions in both the dark energy density and the inertial mass density during cosmic history. This model is statistically preferred over its non-flat ΛCDM and wCDM counterparts when using the latest combined datasets. The results underscore that the inertial mass density $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$ can serve as a fundamental parameter for characterizing dark energy, offering an alternative to the equation-of-state parameter $w$. Crucially, they demonstrate that geometric degrees of freedom, like spatial curvature, can play a pivotal role in revealing dynamical aspects of dark energy that remain obscured within the standard spatially flat cosmological framework. Future high-precision data from DESI and other surveys will further test this interplay between geometry and dark sector dynamics.]
\n\n
[分级暗能量框架内的恒定惯性质量密度参数化，为 ΛCDM 提供了一个具有物理意义且可通过观测检验的单参数扩展。虽然空间平坦的实现方式在统计上无法与 ΛCDM 区分，也未能缓解 H0 张力，但允许空间曲率后，模型的现象学发生了质的变化。具有闭合宇宙几何和正 $M_{ig}$ 的 oSimple-gDE 模型预测，在宇宙历史中暗能量密度和惯性质量密度都会发生符号转变。在使用最新组合数据集时，该模型在统计上优于其对应的非平坦 ΛCDM 和 wCDM 模型。研究结果强调，惯性质量密度 $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$ 可以作为表征暗能量的基本参数，为状态方程参数 $w$ 提供了替代方案。至关重要的是，它们表明几何自由度（如空间曲率）在揭示暗能量动力学方面可以发挥关键作用，而这些动力学特征在标准空间平坦宇宙学框架中是被掩盖的。未来来自 DESI 和其他巡天的高精度数据将进一步检验几何与暗区动力学之间的这种相互作用。]

Abstract: We present updated observational constraints on the simple-gDE model, characterized by a constant inertial mass density (IMD) $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$,which belongs to the broader graduated dark energy family, and compare its cosmological implications with those of the $w$CDM and the $Λ$CDM models. This parametrization provides a physically motivated, one-parameter extension of $Λ$CDM, perspective on DE dynamics beyond the usual equation-of-state approach. We use the newly released DESI DR2 BAO data in combination with either CMB measurements from Planck 2018 or late-time probes, CC and the Pantheon+ SNe Ia sample, considered both with and without SH0ES calibration in this analysis. The data favor a small positive IMD, and Bayesian evidence indicates that the models remain statistically indistinguishable within spatially flat scenarios. Consequently, none of these models exhibits a sign transition in the DE energy density, and no improvement in $H_0$ tension. Allowing spatial curvature qualitatively enlarges the phenomenology of the dark sector. In particular, the interplay between spatial curvature and a nonzero IMD permits sign transitions in both the effective dark-energy density and the IMD during cosmic evolution. For the BAO+CC+SN+SH0ES dataset, the $o$Simple-gDE model yields a transition redshift $z^\dagger = 1.51^{+0.68}_{-0.34}$, while the crossing of the Null Energy Condition boundary (NECB), defined by $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}=0$, occurs at $z_{\rm NECB}=2.36^{+1.48}_{-1.48}$. The model is statistically favored over $oΛ$CDM and $ow$CDM. These results highlight the potential role of IMD as a fundamental parameter in DE phenomenology and demonstrate that geometric effects, such as spatial curvature, can reveal dynamical features of the dark sector that remain hidden within the spatially flat $Λ$CDM framework.

</details>


### [11] [Cosmological prospects for multiband detection of intermediate-mass binary black holes with Taiji and ground-based detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15999)
*Yue-Yan Dong,Ji-Yu Song,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: A systematic analysis of intermediate-mass black hole binary detectability using gravitational-wave observations from space-based detector Taiji alone and in combination with third-generation ground-based detectors. The study simulates IMBH binary populations, evaluates detection capabilities, and quantifies improvements in cosmological parameter constraints, particularly $H_0$, through multiband gravitational-wave observations.

\n\n
对使用天基探测器Taiji单独以及与第三代地基探测器组合对中等质量黑洞双星可探测性的系统分析。该研究模拟了中等质量黑洞双星群体，评估了探测能力，并通过多频带引力波观测量化了宇宙学参数约束（尤其是$H_0$）的改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Intermediate-mass black holes (IMBHs) represent a crucial missing link between stellar-mass and supermassive black holes but remain elusive to electromagnetic detection. Gravitational-wave astronomy offers a direct pathway to detect IMBHs and their mergers, but the detectability across different mass ranges and the potential for cosmological inference need systematic quantification. Space-based detectors like Taiji operate in different frequency bands than ground-based observatories, creating opportunities for multiband observations that could enhance parameter estimation and cosmological constraints.

\n\n
中等质量黑洞代表了恒星质量黑洞与超大质量黑洞之间关键但尚未确认的连接，但对电磁探测仍然难以捉摸。引力波天文学提供了直接探测中等质量黑洞及其并合的直接途径，但跨不同质量范围的可探测性以及宇宙学推断的潜力需要进行系统量化。像Taiji这样的天基探测器在与地基天文台不同的频带运行，创造了多频带观测的机会，这可能增强参数估计和宇宙学约束。

Method: The study employs population synthesis simulations of IMBH binaries under different formation scenarios. Gravitational-wave signals are simulated with appropriate waveform models, and their detectability is assessed using signal-to-noise ratio thresholds for both Taiji (space-based) and third-generation ground-based detectors like Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer. A Bayesian inference framework quantifies parameter estimation accuracy, particularly for cosmological parameters like the Hubble constant $H_0$. The analysis compares single-detector (Taiji alone) performance with multiband networks combining Taiji with ground-based detectors, systematically evaluating improvements in detection rates and parameter constraints.

\n\n
该研究采用了不同形成场景下中等质量黑洞双星的群体合成模拟。使用适当的波形模型模拟引力波信号，并使用信噪比阈值评估其在Taiji（天基）和第三代地基探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜和宇宙探索者）上的可探测性。贝叶斯推断框架量化了参数估计精度，特别是对于哈勃常数$H_0$等宇宙学参数。分析比较了单探测器（仅Taiji）性能与将Taiji与地基探测器结合的多频带网络，系统评估了探测率和参数约束的改进。

Result: Taiji demonstrates strong sensitivity to higher-mass IMBH binaries but reduced capability for lower-mass systems. Ground-based detectors complement this by covering the lower-mass range, creating synergistic coverage. Multiband observations significantly expand the accessible parameter space for IMBH binaries. Most notably, combining Taiji with third-generation ground-based detectors improves constraints on $H_0$ by 36.5% compared to Taiji alone and by 31.0% compared to ground-based detectors alone. The improvement shows strong dependence on event numbers: most pronounced for small samples ($N \lesssim 50$) with gradual saturation as $N$ increases, indicating diminishing returns for large catalogs.

\n\n
Taiji对较高质量的中等质量黑洞双星表现出强灵敏度，但对较低质量系统的能力降低。地基探测器通过覆盖较低质量范围来补充这一点，创造协同覆盖。多频带观测显著扩展了中等质量黑洞双星的可访问参数空间。最值得注意的是，将Taiji与第三代地基探测器结合，相比于仅使用Taiji，对$H_0$的约束改进了36.5%；相比于仅使用地基探测器，改进了31.0%。改进显示出对事件数量的强依赖性：对于小样本（$N \lesssim 50$）最为显著，随着$N$增加逐渐饱和，表明大目录的收益递减。

Conclusion: Multiband gravitational-wave observations using space-based Taiji in synergy with third-generation ground-based detectors create a powerful observational network for intermediate-mass black hole binaries. This approach not only enhances detectability across the full IMBH mass range but also transforms IMBH binaries into precision cosmological probes, with particular impact on measuring the Hubble constant $H_0$. The synergy between frequency bands provides complementary information that improves parameter estimation beyond what either band alone can achieve, establishing multiband gravitational-wave astronomy as essential for both black hole astrophysics and cosmology.

\n\n
使用天基Taiji与第三代地基探测器协同的多频带引力波观测为中等质量黑洞双星创建了强大的观测网络。这种方法不仅增强了跨整个中等质量黑洞质量范围的可探测性，而且将中等质量黑洞双星转化为精确宇宙学探测器，对测量哈勃常数$H_0$具有特别影响。频带之间的协同作用提供了互补信息，改进了参数估计，超越了任一单独频带所能达到的水平，确立了多频带引力波天文学对于黑洞天体物理学和宇宙学都是必不可少的。

Abstract: Intermediate-mass black holes (IMBHs) bridge the gap between stellar-mass and supermassive black holes, but remain challenging to detect electromagnetically. Gravitational-wave observations provide a direct means of detecting IMBHs and their mergers. We simulate the gravitational-wave signals of IMBH binaries under different population models and assess their detectability with the space-based detector Taiji alone and in a multiband network combining Taiji with third-generation ground-based detectors. Taiji performs well in detecting high-mass IMBH binaries, while ground-based detectors compensate for its reduced sensitivity to lower-mass systems. Their combination expands the accessible parameter space and improves the constraints on cosmological parameters. In particular, multiband observations improve the constraint accuracy on $H_0$ by $36.5\%$ and $31.0\%$ compared with Taiji and ET2CE alone, respectively. We further examine the dependence of parameter accuracy on the number of simulated events, finding that improvements are most pronounced for small samples and gradually saturate as the number of events increases. We conclude that multiband observations enhance the detectability of IMBH binaries and reinforce their role as probes of precision cosmology.

</details>


### [12] [Emulation of SPHEREx Galaxy Power Spectra I: Neural Network Details and Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16003)
*Joseph Adamo,Grace Gibbins,Anne Moore,Tim Eifler*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Neural network emulator combining fully-connected layers and transformer architecture achieves ~900x speedup for generating redshift-space galaxy power spectrum multipoles across multiple tracers/redshift bins compared to SPHEREx pipeline, with high accuracy (Δχ² ~0.069) and cosmological parameter recovery.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Redshift-space galaxy power spectrum multipoles are computationally expensive to generate for cosmological parameter inference in large-scale structure surveys. SPHEREx requires rapid evaluation across multiple tracer types and redshift bins to enable efficient Markov Chain Monte Carlo sampling. Traditional methods like the Effective Field Theory of Large-Scale Structure (EFTofLSS) calculations are too slow for comprehensive parameter space exploration.

Method: Hybrid architecture combining fully-connected neural network layers with transformer blocks to capture complex cosmological parameter → power spectrum mappings. Optimized training strategies including custom loss functions and sampling strategies over cosmological/astrophysical parameter space. Validation against EFT-based SPHEREx pipeline using two correlated tracer bins and two independent redshift bins in simulated analyses.

Result: Achieved 900× speedup versus SPHEREx pipeline with median Δχ²=0.069 on testing set. Emulator accurately reproduces likelihood contours: average 1D best-fit parameter shift of 0.078σ and 1D error bar differences of 0.82%. Demonstrates feasibility for cosmological parameter inference in SPHEREx analyses.

Conclusion: Transformer-enhanced neural network emulators provide accurate and extremely fast predictions for redshift-space galaxy power spectrum multipoles across multiple tracers and redshifts, enabling efficient cosmological parameter estimation for SPHEREx and similar large-scale structure surveys.

Abstract: We present neural networks to generate redshift-space galaxy power spectrum multipoles for multiple tracer and redshift bins simultaneously given a set of input cosmology and galaxy bias parameters. This emulator utilizes a combination of fully-connected layers and transformer architecture to accurately predict galaxy power spectrum multipoles $900$ times faster than the SPHEREx pipeline. We quantify network performance using both $Δχ^2$, and likelihood contours for simulated SPHEREx analyses, using two correlated tracer bins and two independent redshift bins. After optimizing network architecture, the loss function, and training set sampling strategy, we achieve $\operatorname{Med}\left( Δχ^2\right) = 0.069$ when comparing to our testing set. At the contour-level our emulator agrees with EFT predictions over a realistic parameter range, with an average 1D best-fit shift of $0.078σ$ and $0.82 \%$ change in 1D error bars. These results demonstrate the feasibility of using neural-network emulators to accelerate SPHEREx redshift-space power-spectrum analyses.

</details>


### [13] [Cosmological hydrodynamical simulations of clustering dark energy with Nefertiti](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16248)
*Linda Blot,Théo Gayoux,Fabian Schmidt,Pier Stefano Corasaniti,Bastien de Ligondes*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: [First cosmological simulations of nonlinear clustering dark energy as a fluid using Nefertiti hydrodynamics code. Dark energy perturbations become fully nonlinear on small scales, generating ~10% density fluctuations around massive halos without catastrophic instabilities. Enables robust constraints on dark energy sound speed from large-scale structure.]

[首次使用Nefertiti流体动力学代码对非线性聚类暗能量作为流体进行宇宙学模拟。暗能量微扰在小尺度上完全非线性化，在巨大晕周围产生约10%的密度涨落而无灾难性不稳定性。为实现从大尺度结构数据对暗能量声速的稳健约束铺平道路。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The standard cosmological constant (w=-1) has no spatial perturbations, but dynamical dark energy models with w≠-1 can develop perturbations that affect structure formation. Previous work on clustering dark energy has been largely limited to linear perturbation theory or phenomenological treatments, missing the fully nonlinear regime where dark energy perturbations could become significant, especially around massive halos. Understanding nonlinear dark energy clustering is essential for accurate interpretation of upcoming precision large-scale structure surveys (e.g., Euclid, DESI, LSST).]

[标准宇宙学常数(w=-1)没有空间微扰，但具有w≠-1的动态暗能量模型可以产生影响结构形成的微扰。先前关于聚类暗能量的工作主要局限于线性微扰理论或唯象处理，忽略了暗能量微扰可能变得显著的完全非线性区域，特别是在巨大晕周围。理解非线性暗能量聚类对于准确解释即将到来的精密大尺度结构巡天（如Euclid、DESI、LSST）至关重要。]

Method: [Implement dark energy as a relativistic perfect fluid with equation of state parameter w and sound speed c_s in the Nefertiti hydrodynamics code. Solve the full nonlinear fluid equations coupled to gravity and dark matter N-body particles. The dark energy fluid evolves according to conservation equations: ∇_μ T^μν=0, with energy-momentum tensor T^μν = (ρ+ p)u^μ u^ν + p g^μν. For constant w=-0.9 case studied, sound speed c_s=1 (luminal). Simulations include standard ΛCDM components plus the dark energy fluid component with self-consistent nonlinear evolution.]

[在Nefertiti流体动力学代码中将暗能量实现为具有状态方程参数w和声速c_s的相对论性完美流体。求解与引力和暗物质N体粒子耦合的完全非线性流体方程。暗能量流体根据守恒方程演化：∇_μ T^μν=0，其中能量-动量张量T^μν = (ρ+ p)u^μ u^ν + p g^μν。对于研究的常数w=-0.9情况，声速c_s=1（光速）。模拟包括标准ΛCDM分量加上具有自洽非线性演化的暗能量流体分量。]

Result: [Dark energy perturbations become fully nonlinear on small scales (sub-Mpc), developing significant density fluctuations without catastrophic instabilities previously reported in some implementations. For constant w=-0.9 with c_s=1, dark energy contributes ~10% to total density perturbation inside and around massive halos. This produces measurable effects on halo profiles, power spectra, and gravitational lensing signals. The density distribution of dark energy shows clustering correlated with dark matter halos but with distinct morphology due to different pressure support. These nonlinear effects are significant for precision cosmology and enable extraction of dark energy sound speed constraints from upcoming surveys.]

[暗能量微扰在小尺度（亚Mpc）上变得完全非线性，产生显著的密度涨落而无先前某些实现中报道的灾难性不稳定性。对于常数w=-0.9且c_s=1的情况，暗能量在巨大晕内部和周围对总密度微扰贡献约10%。这对晕轮廓、功率谱和引力透镜信号产生可测量效应。暗能量的密度分布显示与暗物质晕相关但具有不同压力支持导致的独特形态的聚类。这些非线性效应对精密宇宙学具有重要意义，并能够从即将到来的巡天中提取暗能量声速约束。]

Conclusion: [First fully nonlinear cosmological simulations of clustering dark energy demonstrate that dark energy perturbations can reach ~10% level in dense regions without stability issues, providing novel predictions for observational signatures. This work establishes a computational framework for studying nonlinear dark energy clustering and enables robust constraints on dark energy properties (especially sound speed c_s) from next-generation large-scale structure surveys. The methodology can be extended to more general dark energy and modified gravity scenarios.]

[首次完全非线性聚类暗能量宇宙学模拟表明暗能量微扰在稠密区域可达约10%水平而无稳定性问题，为观测特征提供了新颖预测。这项工作建立了研究非线性暗能量聚类的计算框架，并使得从下一代大尺度结构巡天中对暗能量特性（特别是声速c_s）进行稳健约束成为可能。该方法可扩展到更一般的暗能量和修改引力场景。]

Abstract: We present the first cosmological simulations that consistently include nonlinear clustering dark energy evolved as a fluid with the numerical hydrodynamics code Nefertiti. Dark energy perturbations become fully nonlinear on small scales, developing significant density fluctuations without exhibiting the catastrophic instabilities previously reported. We show results for the density distribution, power spectrum, and halo profiles of dark energy. Clustering dark energy contributes to the total density perturbation at the $\sim 10\%$ level inside and around massive halos in our simulations with constant $w=-0.9$, a significant potential signal for lensing and dynamical probes. These simulations pave the way to robust constraints on the speed of sound of dark energy perturbations from large-scale structure data.

</details>


### [14] [Perturbative Effects of Dark Matter Environments on Black Hole Shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16402)
*Gabriel Gomez*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We develop a perturbative framework for black holes embedded in dark matter halos, compute leading-order corrections to photon-sphere radius and shadow radius for generic profiles, apply to Hernquist/NFW models, and find shadow deviations below current Keck/VLTI bounds while satisfying GRAVITY collaboration constraints on enclosed dark matter mass.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: There is currently no unique or systematic framework to model black holes embedded in dark matter environments for probing dark matter properties in gravity's strong-field regime. Several commonly adopted approaches raise methodological ambiguities, motivating the development of a consistent perturbative formalism.

Method: We build a perturbative framework describing deformations of static, spherically symmetric black holes induced by surrounding dark matter distributions. We compute leading-order corrections to photon-sphere radius and shadow radius assuming generic dark matter halo profiles, then apply formalism to physically motivated density profiles (Hernquist and Navarro-Frenk-White models), obtaining closed-form analytical expressions for perturbed metric functions and critical impact parameter in Schwarzschild background.

Result: Quantitative estimates for shadow deviations show they lie well beyond current observational bounds set by Keck and VLTI measurements. As a consistency check, we estimate total dark matter mass enclosed within orbital radius of S2 star remains well below the $0.1\%$ upper limit reported by GRAVITY collaboration. Closed-form analytical expressions obtained for perturbed metric functions and critical impact parameter.

Conclusion: The approach offers a systematic avenue to investigate perturbative effects of dark matter on black hole phenomenology, including potential implications for gravitational wave observations. The perturbative framework provides a consistent method to model dark matter effects on black holes that avoids methodological ambiguities of previous approaches.

Abstract: Constructing spacetime solutions that describe black holes embedded in dark matter environments is a crucial step toward probing the properties of dark matter in the strong-field regime of gravity. At present, however, there is no unique or systematic framework to model such configurations, and several commonly adopted approaches raise methodological ambiguities. Motivated by these challenges, we build upon a perturbative framework to describe deformations of static, spherically symmetric black holes induced by a surrounding dark matter distribution. Within this framework, we compute the leading-order corrections to both the photon-sphere radius and the radius of the black hole shadow, assuming a generic dark matter halo profile. We then apply the formalism to physically motivated density profiles, including the Hernquist and Navarro-Frenk-White models, obtaining closed-form analytical expressions for the perturbed metric functions and for the critical impact parameter in the Schwarzschild background. Using these results, we obtain quantitative estimates for the corresponding shadow deviations and find that they lie well beyond the current observational bounds set by Keck and VLTI measurements. As a consistency check, we further estimate the total dark matter mass enclosed within the orbital radius of the S2 star and show that it remains well below the $0.1\%$ upper limit reported by the GRAVITY collaboration. Overall, this approach offers a systematic avenue to investigate perturbative effects of dark matter on black hole phenomenology, including potential implications for gravitational wave observations.
