### [15] [Testing the Coexistence of Dark Energy and Dark Matter with Late-time Observational Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16533)
*Shambel Sahlu,Andronikos Paliathanasis,Genly Leon,Amare Abebe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates a cosmological model with interacting dark sector components (dark energy and dark matter) that possesses analytical solutions. The model is constrained using multiple datasets including cosmic chronometers, DESI BAO, Gamma-ray bursts, and Supernova catalogs. The analysis shows the coexistence model provides better fits to data than ΛCDM and wCDM reference models, though with smaller H₀ values.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to develop and test a cosmological model with interacting dark sector components that can provide analytical solutions for the Hubble function. The motivation stems from the need for alternatives to standard ΛCDM that can better describe the observed late-time acceleration while addressing tensions in cosmological parameters. By including interactions between dark energy and dark matter, the model offers a more sophisticated framework for understanding cosmic acceleration beyond simple constant dark energy models.

Method: The authors develop an analytical model with interacting dark energy and dark matter components. They derive exact solutions for the Hubble function $H(z)$. The model is then constrained using Bayesian statistical methods with multiple observational datasets: cosmic chronometers (31 old + 3 new DESI data), DESI DR2 Baryonic Acoustic Oscillations, Gamma-ray bursts, and Supernova catalogs (Pantheon Plus, Union3, and DES-Dovekie). Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods are employed to obtain posterior distributions of model parameters, with comparisons made against reference ΛCDM and wCDM models using statistical criteria.

Result: The analysis shows the coexistence model fits the observational data better than both ΛCDM and wCDM reference models according to statistical measures. The model provides a cosmologically viable description of late-time acceleration. At high redshifts, the model behavior becomes similar to wCDM, as indicated by GRB data. Notably, the model yields statistically smaller values for the Hubble constant $H_0$ parameter compared to standard models. The exact analytical nature of the Hubble function solutions allows for precise comparisons with observational data across the redshift range.

Conclusion: The interacting dark sector model provides a viable cosmological framework that improves upon standard ΛCDM and wCDM in fitting multiple observational datasets. The analytical solutions enable robust parameter constraints, revealing a preference for smaller $H_0$ values. While the model's high-redshift behavior approaches wCDM, its interacting nature provides a distinctive mechanism for late-time acceleration that warrants further investigation, particularly in light of the Hubble tension and other cosmological parameter discrepancies.

Abstract: We investigate the viability of a cosmological scenario with interacting dark sector, which can describe the coexistence between dark energy and dark matter. The model possesses an analytical solution for the Hubble function and we constrain the free parameters by applying the newly released cosmic chronometers data (31 old data and 3 new data from DESI), the Baryonic Acoustic Oscillators from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Survey (DESI DR2 BAO), along with Gamma-ray bursts (GRBs) and Supernova catalogues (Pantheon Plus, Union3, and DES-Dovekie). We find that the coexistence model fits the data sets in a better way than the reference models - the $Λ$CDM and $w$CDM models. The analysis shows that the coexistence scenario can provide a cosmologically viable model for the description of the late-time acceleration of the universe. Nevertheless, for large redshifts, the model has a similar behaviour to that of the $w$CDM model, as the introduction of the GRB data indicates in the statistical parameters. Finally, it is worth mentioning that the coexistence model provides a statistically smaller value for the $H_{0}$ parameter.

</details>


### [16] [Cosmic Dipole as a Symmetry Response: From the Ellis--Baldwin Formula to Correlation Function Dipoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16776)
*Tsutomu T. Takeuchi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper reformulates the cosmic dipole in galaxy number counts as a symmetry response to Lorentz boosts, generalizing beyond the traditional Ellis-Baldwin formula to reveal dipole structures in higher-order statistics and unifying observer/source contributions through a response framework.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The traditional Ellis-Baldwin (EB) formula for cosmic dipole analysis relies on restrictive assumptions of power-law source counts and flux-limited selection, which limit its applicability to realistic galaxy surveys with complex population distributions and selection effects. There is need for a more fundamental formulation that connects dipole anisotropies to underlying symmetries and extends to higher-order correlation functions.

Method: The authors reformulate the cosmic dipole as a symmetry response to Lorentz boosts, deriving the general expression $D=\beta R$ where $R=\partial\ln N/\partial\ln\beta$ encodes population and selection effects. They extend this response framework to higher-order statistics by analyzing how Lorentz boosts transform n-point correlation functions, demonstrating dipole components emerge in the two-point correlation function. The approach establishes connections to redshift-space distortions and relativistic galaxy clustering through symmetry considerations.

Result: The classical EB formula emerges as a special case of the more general response framework. Lorentz boosts induce dipole components in two-point correlation functions, and more generally create a hierarchy of responses in n-point statistics. The framework unifies observer-induced and source-induced dipoles by showing they contribute to the same multipole component, clarifying the relationship between different anisotropy sources in galaxy clustering.

Conclusion: The cosmic dipole represents a symmetry response of finite-sample point-process statistics to Lorentz boosts, providing a new perspective for interpreting dipole anisotropies observationally. This response framework offers a fundamental connection between observer motion effects and intrinsic clustering properties, with implications for cosmological parameter estimation and tests of fundamental symmetries.

Abstract: The cosmic dipole in galaxy number counts is traditionally described by the Ellis--Baldwin (EB) formula under simplifying assumptions of power-law source counts and flux-limited selection. We reformulate the EB dipole as a symmetry response of observed counts to a Lorentz boost, leading to the general expression $D=βR$, where $R=\partial\ln N/\partial\lnβ$ encodes the underlying population and selection effects. The classical EB formula is recovered as a limiting case. We show that this response framework extends beyond one-point statistics: Lorentz boosts induce a dipole component in the two-point correlation function and, more generally, a hierarchy of responses in $n$-point statistics. We further clarify the relation to redshift-space distortions and relativistic galaxy clustering, and provide a unified description in which observer- and source-induced dipoles contribute to the same multipole component. This establishes the cosmic dipole as a symmetry response of finite-sample point-process statistics, offering a new perspective on dipole anisotropies and their observational interpretation.

</details>


### [17] [Beyond $Λ$CDM with a Logistic RG-like Flow of the Low Redshift Cosmic Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16852)
*Shibendu Gupta Choudhury,Anjan A Sen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Introduces a phenomenological logistic function for the total equation of state $w_{\rm T}(z)$ inspired by renormalization group flow between cosmological fixed points, providing improved fits to DESI-DR2 BAO, DES supernovae, and CMB data compared to ΛCDM, with reconstructed jerk parameter showing deviations at low redshifts.

提出了一种受重正化群流启发的宇宙总物态方程 $w_{\rm T}(z)$ 的唯象逻辑函数参数化，使用 DESI-DR2 BAO、DES 超新星和 CMB 数据相比 ΛCDM 得到改进的拟合，重构的 jerk 参数在低红移处显示出偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent cosmological observations hint at possible deviations from ΛCDM at late times, motivating exploration of alternative frameworks beyond specific dark energy models. The paper aims to develop a minimal phenomenological approach that directly reconstructs the total equation of state $w_{\rm T}(z)$ from background observables using a flow-inspired parametrization with physical interpretation.

近期宇宙学观测暗示晚期宇宙可能偏离 ΛCDM 模型，这促使探索超越特定暗能量模型的替代框架。本文旨在开发一种最小唯象方法，使用具有物理解释的流启发参数化直接从背景可观测量重构总物态方程 $w_{\rm T}(z)$。

Method: Introduces a logistic function parametrization for the total equation of state: $$w_{\rm T}(z) = w_{\rm early} + \frac{w_{\rm late} - w_{\rm early}}{1 + e^{-k(z - z_c)}}$$ motivated by renormalization group flow between cosmological fixed points. This directly reconstructs $w_{\rm T}(z)$ from background observables without assuming specific dark energy models. Analyzes DESI-DR2 BAO measurements, DES-Dovekie supernova data, and CMB distance priors to constrain parameters $(w_{\rm early}, w_{\rm late}, k, z_c)$. Reconstructs jerk parameter $j(z)$ to characterize deviations from ΛCDM.

引入总物态方程的逻辑函数参数化：$$w_{\rm T}(z) = w_{\rm early} + \frac{w_{\rm late} - w_{\rm early}}{1 + e^{-k(z - z_c)}}$$，其灵感来源于宇宙学固定点之间的重正化群流。这直接从背景可观测量重构 $w_{\rm T}(z)$，无需假设特定暗能量模型。分析 DESI-DR2 BAO 测量、DES-Dovekie 超新星数据和 CMB 距离先验来约束参数 $(w_{\rm early}, w_{\rm late}, k, z_c)$。重构 jerk 参数 $j(z)$ 以表征与 ΛCDM 的偏离。

Result: The logistic parametrization provides improved fit to combined data compared to ΛCDM, remaining competitive with standard dynamical dark energy models. Reconstructed expansion history shows noticeable deviations from ΛCDM at low redshifts, with reconstructed jerk parameter $j(z)$ exhibiting non-ΛCDM behavior. Statistical significance of deviations is model-dependent, but the approach demonstrates the utility of flow-inspired parametrizations for probing late-time cosmic dynamics.

与 ΛCDM 相比，逻辑参数化对组合数据提供了改进的拟合，与标准动力学暗能量模型保持竞争力。重构的膨胀历史在低红移处显示出与 ΛCDM 的明显偏离，重构的 jerk 参数 $j(z)$ 表现出非 ΛCDM 行为。偏离的统计显著性依赖于模型，但该方法证明了流启发参数化在探测晚期宇宙动力学方面的效用。

Conclusion: The logistic parametrization inspired by renormalization group flow offers a complementary and physically interpretable framework for probing late-time cosmic dynamics, with potential to identify deviations from ΛCDM. While current statistical significance is model-dependent, the approach demonstrates the value of phenomenologically reconstructing the total equation of state from background observables without assuming specific dark energy models.

受重正化群流启发的逻辑参数化为探测晚期宇宙动力学提供了一个互补且具有物理解释的框架，具有识别与 ΛCDM 偏离的潜力。虽然当前的统计显著性依赖于模型，但该方法展示了从背景可观测量唯象地重构总物态方程的价值，而无需假设特定的暗能量模型。

Abstract: Recent cosmological observations show hints for possible deviations from the standard $Λ$CDM paradigm at late times. To study such deviation, we introduce a minimal phenomenological framework in which the total equation of state of the Universe, $w_{\rm T}(z)$, follows a logistic evolution motivated by a renormalization group like flow between cosmological fixed points. This approach directly reconstructs $w_{\rm T}(z)$ probed by background observables, without assuming a specific dark energy model. Using DESI-DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, DES-Dovekie latest supernova data, and CMB distance priors, we find that the logistic parametrization provides an improved fit compared to $Λ$CDM and remains competitive with standard dynamical dark energy models. The inferred expansion history exhibits noticeable deviations from $Λ$CDM at low redshifts, reflected in the reconstructed jerk parameter. While the statistical significance of these deviations is model-dependent, our results highlight the potential of flow-inspired parametrizations as a complementary and physically interpretable framework for probing late-time cosmic dynamics.

</details>

### [18] [Optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15697)
*Yusuke Nishida*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [The paper derives the optical Magnus effect from Maxwell's equations in curved spacetime, obtaining generalized equations for circularly polarized wave packet motion. It then applies this to gravitational lensing, showing that Einstein rings from point sources are impossible for any axially symmetric thin lens when the optical Magnus effect is included, and provides analytic solutions for simple lens models.]

\n\n
[本文从弯曲时空中的麦克斯韦方程出发推导光学马格努斯效应，得到了圆偏振波包运动的广义方程。然后将此应用于引力透镜效应，表明当包含光学马格努斯效应时，任何轴对称薄透镜都无法从点源产生爱因斯坦环，并为简单透镜模型提供了解析解。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The optical Magnus effect causes polarization-dependent transverse shifts in light trajectories, appearing as a first-order wavelength correction to geometrical optics. While known in flat spacetime, its derivation from fundamental equations in curved spacetime and its implications for gravitational lensing phenomena remain underexplored, particularly regarding how this helicity-dependent effect modifies standard gravitational lensing predictions.]

\n\n
[光学马格努斯效应引起依赖于偏振的光轨迹横向偏移，表现为几何光学的一阶波长修正。虽然在平直时空中已知，但其从弯曲时空基本方程出发的推导以及对引力透镜现象的影响仍有待探索，特别是这种与螺旋度相关的效应如何修正标准引力透镜预测。]

Method: [1. Starting from Maxwell's equations in a general curved spacetime metric $g_{\\mu\\nu}$, deriving the equation of motion for a wave packet of circularly polarized light using geometrical optics expansion and Berry phase formalism.
2. Generalizing the anomalous velocity term $v_a^\\text{anom} = \\frac{\\lambda}{2\\pi}\\frac{\\nabla\\phi\\times\\mathbf{k}}{k^2}$ for curved spacetime, where $\\lambda$ is wavelength, $\\phi$ is phase, and $\\mathbf{k}$ is wavevector, with $\\nabla$ now being covariant derivative.
3. Formulating modified lens equation incorporating optical Magnus effect: $\\boldsymbol{\\beta} = \\boldsymbol{\\theta} - \\frac{D_{ds}}{D_s}\\boldsymbol{\\alpha}(\\boldsymbol{\\theta}) + \\delta\\boldsymbol{\\alpha}_\\text{OM}(\\boldsymbol{\\theta},\\sigma)$, where $\\sigma=\\pm1$ is helicity.
4. Analyzing axially symmetric thin lenses, proving impossibility of Einstein ring formation from point sources due to helicity-dependent shifts breaking axial symmetry.
5. Solving modified lens equation analytically for simple models: point mass lens and singular isothermal sphere (SIS).]

\n\n
[1. 从一般弯曲时空度规$g_{\\mu\\nu}$中的麦克斯韦方程出发，使用几何光学展开和Berry相位形式推导圆偏振光波包的运动方程。
2. 将反常速度项$v_a^\\text{anom} = \\frac{\\lambda}{2\\pi}\\frac{\\nabla\\phi\\times\\mathbf{k}}{k^2}$推广到弯曲时空，其中$\\lambda$是波长，$\\phi$是相位，$\\mathbf{k}$是波矢，$\\nabla$现在是协变导数。
3. 建立包含光学马格努斯效应的修正透镜方程：$\\boldsymbol{\\beta} = \\boldsymbol{\\theta} - \\frac{D_{ds}}{D_s}\\boldsymbol{\\alpha}(\\boldsymbol{\\theta}) + \\delta\\boldsymbol{\\alpha}_\\text{OM}(\\boldsymbol{\\theta},\\sigma)$，其中$\\sigma=\\pm1$是螺旋度。
4. 分析轴对称薄透镜，证明由于螺旋度相关偏移破坏轴对称性，点源无法形成爱因斯坦环。
5. 为简单模型解析求解修正透镜方程：点质量透镜和奇异等温球(SIS)。]

Result: [1. Derived generalized equation for wave packet motion: $\\frac{dx^\\mu}{d\\lambda} = \\frac{k^\\mu}{\\omega} + \\sigma\\frac{\\lambda}{2\\pi}\\epsilon^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}k_\\nu\\nabla_\\rho k_\\sigma$, confirming helicity-dependent anomalous velocity in curved spacetime.
2. Proved theorem: For any axially symmetric thin lens, the modified lens equation $\\beta(\\theta) = \\theta - \\frac{D_{ds}}{D_s}\\alpha(\\theta) + \\delta\\alpha_\\text{OM}(\\theta,\\sigma)$ cannot have solutions with $\\beta=0$ (point source alignment) due to $\\delta\\alpha_\\text{OM}\\propto\\sigma\\neq0$, making Einstein rings impossible.
3. Analytic solutions for point mass lens: Modified image positions $\\theta_{\\pm} = \\frac{\\beta}{2} \\pm \\sqrt{\\left(\\frac{\\beta}{2}\\right)^2 + \\theta_E^2 \\mp \\delta\\theta_\\text{OM}}$ with $\\delta\\theta_\\text{OM}\\propto\\sigma\\lambda/D_d$.
4. For SIS lens: Solutions become $\\theta_{\\pm} = \\theta_E \\pm \\sqrt{\\beta^2 + \\delta\\theta_\\text{OM}^2}$ with asymmetry induced by helicity.
5. In expanding spacetime with weak potential $\\Phi$, Magnus deflection $\\delta\\alpha_\\text{OM} \\approx \\sigma\\frac{\\lambda}{2\\pi c^2}\\int d\\chi\\nabla_\\perp(\\nabla^2\\Phi)$, showing dependence on potential curvature.]

\n\n
[1. 推导出波包运动的广义方程：$\\frac{dx^\\mu}{d\\lambda} = \\frac{k^\\mu}{\\omega} + \\sigma\\frac{\\lambda}{2\\pi}\\epsilon^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\sigma}k_\\nu\\nabla_\\rho k_\\sigma$，确认弯曲时空中螺旋度相关的反常速度。
2. 证明定理：对于任何轴对称薄透镜，修正透镜方程$\\beta(\\theta) = \\theta - \\frac{D_{ds}}{D_s}\\alpha(\\theta) + \\delta\\alpha_\\text{OM}(\\theta,\\sigma)$由于$\\delta\\alpha_\\text{OM}\\propto\\sigma\\neq0$，不能有$\\beta=0$（点源对齐）的解，使得爱因斯坦环不可能形成。
3. 点质量透镜的解析解：修正图像位置$\\theta_{\\pm} = \\frac{\\beta}{2} \\pm \\sqrt{\\left(\\frac{\\beta}{2}\\right)^2 + \\theta_E^2 \\mp \\delta\\theta_\\text{OM}}$，其中$\\delta\\theta_\\text{OM}\\propto\\sigma\\lambda/D_d$。
4. SIS透镜：解变为$\\theta_{\\pm} = \\theta_E \\pm \\sqrt{\\beta^2 + \\delta\\theta_\\text{OM}^2}$，螺旋度引起不对称性。
5. 在具有弱势$\\Phi$的膨胀时空中，马格努斯偏转$\\delta\\alpha_\\text{OM} \\approx \\sigma\\frac{\\lambda}{2\\pi c^2}\\int d\\chi\\nabla_\\perp(\\nabla^2\\Phi)$，显示对势曲率的依赖性。]

Conclusion: [The optical Magnus effect, derived fundamentally from Maxwell's equations in curved spacetime, introduces helicity-dependent corrections to geometric optics that have profound implications for gravitational lensing. The key theoretical result is the impossibility of perfect Einstein ring formation from point sources under any axially symmetric thin lens when this effect is included, fundamentally altering standard gravitational lensing predictions. The analytic solutions provide testable signatures for future high-precision lensing observations, particularly for polarimetric measurements of strongly lensed systems. The formalism establishes a complete theoretical framework for incorporating spin-orbit coupling effects in curved spacetime optics.]

\n\n
[光学马格努斯效应从弯曲时空中的麦克斯韦方程基本推导而来，引入了对几何光学的螺旋度相关修正，对引力透镜效应具有深远影响。关键理论结果是：当包含此效应时，任何轴对称薄透镜都无法从点源形成完美的爱因斯坦环，从根本上改变了标准引力透镜预测。解析解为未来高精度透镜观测提供了可测试的特征，特别是强透镜系统的偏振测量。该形式主义建立了一个完整的理论框架，用于在弯曲时空光学中纳入自旋-轨道耦合效应。]

Abstract: The optical Magnus effect refers to transverse shift of a trajectory of light caused by its polarization and appears as a correction to geometrical optics at the linear order in wavelength. Here, we start from Maxwell's equations in a curved spacetime to derive the equation of motion for a wave packet of circularly polarized light, which confirms the known result involving the helicity-dependent anomalous velocity with some generalization and clarification. We then study possible consequences of the optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing in the Schwarzschild spacetime as well as under a weak gravitational potential in an expanding spacetime. Among others, by formulating the lens equation modified to incorporate the optical Magnus effect, the Einstein ring is found impossible to emerge from a point source for any axially symmetric thin lens. Analytic solutions to the modified lens equation are also obtained for simple lens models, illuminating how image formation is affected by the optical Magnus effect.

</details>


### [19] [Impact of numerical-relativity waveform calibration on parametrized post-Einsteinian tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15765)
*Simone Mezzasoma,Carl-Johan Haster,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Analysis reveals that calibration errors in IMRPhenomD waveform model can cause false detections of GR violations in parametrized tests even at SNR=60. Using uncertainty-aware calibration eliminates false positives up to SNR=330, demonstrating critical need to incorporate numerical relativity calibration uncertainties for reliable strong-field gravity tests.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Parametrized post-Einsteinian tests of general relativity assume negligible systematic errors from waveform calibration, particularly numerical relativity uncertainties. This work investigates whether calibration errors in IMRPhenomD's late-inspiral fitting coefficients can produce spurious detections of GR violations that mimic true physics beyond Einstein's theory.

参数化后爱因斯坦广义相对论检验通常假设波形校准的系统误差可忽略，特别是数值相对论的不确定性。本工作研究IMRPhenomD模型中晚期旋进拟合系数的校准误差是否会产生虚假的广义相对论违反信号，从而模拟超越爱因斯坦理论的真实物理效应。

Method: Developed an uncertainty-aware version of IMRPhenomD recalibrated to numerical relativity surrogate waveforms with probabilistic descriptions of fitting coefficients. Injected GR-consistent signals into simulated O5 ground-based detector network and recovered them using both original IMRPhenomD (augmented with parametrized post-Einsteinian phase deformation) and uncertainty-aware model. Systematically analyzed how calibration errors propagate to false GR violation detections across different signal-to-noise ratios.

开发了基于数值相对论替代波形重新校准的不确定感知IMRPhenomD版本，为拟合系数提供概率描述。将广义相对论一致的信号注入模拟的O5地面探测器网络，并使用原始IMRPhenomD（增强参数化后爱因斯坦相位变形）和不确定感知模型进行恢复。系统分析校准误差如何在不同信噪比下传播至虚假广义相对论违反检测。

Result: False GR violations arise at network SNRs as low as 60 when using original IMRPhenomD with calibration errors. These spurious detections are eliminated when using the uncertainty-aware model, with inferred parametrized post-Einsteinian phase deformations remaining consistent with zero even for SNR up to 330. The magnitude of calibration error-induced false signals scales with SNR, becoming increasingly problematic for high-SNR events expected in future observing runs.

当使用具有校准误差的原始IMRPhenomD时，网络信噪比低至60即可产生虚假广义相对论违反。使用不确定感知模型时，这些虚假检测被消除，即使信噪比高达330，推断的参数化后爱因斯坦相位变形仍保持与零一致。校准误差引起的虚假信号幅度随信噪比缩放，对未来观测运行中预期的高信噪比事件问题愈发严重。

Conclusion: Numerical relativity calibration uncertainties must be explicitly incorporated into waveform models for reliable strong-field tests of GR. Uncertainty-aware calibration preserves test robustness by preventing calibration artifacts from being misinterpreted as physics beyond Einstein's theory. This establishes a necessary methodological standard for next-generation gravitational-wave analyses where systematic uncertainties become comparable to statistical errors at high SNRs.

必须将数值相对论校准不确定性明确纳入波形模型，以实现可靠的强场广义相对论检验。不确定感知校准通过防止校准伪影被误认为超越爱因斯坦理论的物理效应，保持了检验的稳健性。这为下一代引力波分析建立了必要的方法学标准，在高信噪比下系统不确定性变得与统计误差相当。

Abstract: Testing general relativity in the strong-field and highly dynamical regime is now possible through current gravitational-wave observations, where even a single high-quality detection can place competitive constraints on deviations from Einstein's theory. The parametrized post-Einsteinian framework provides a theory-agnostic approach to search for such deviations, but it typically assumes that systematic uncertainties in the base waveform model, particularly those arising from calibration to numerical relativity, are negligible. In this work, we investigate how calibration errors in the late-inspiral fitting coefficients of the IMRPhenomD waveform model can lead to spurious detections of departures from general relativity in parametrized tests. We use an uncertainty-aware version of IMRPhenomD, recalibrated to a set of numerical relativity surrogate waveforms and equipped with a probabilistic description of its fitting coefficients, to simulate general-relativity-consistent signals. We inject these signals into an O5 ground-based detector network and recover them with the original IMRPhenomD model augmented with a parametrized post-Einsteinian phase deformation. We find that false violations of general relativity using this model arise for network signal-to-noise ratios as low as 60. When the uncertainty-aware model is used instead, the inferred parametrized post-Einsteinian phase deformation remains consistent with zero even for signals with a signal-to-noise ratio up to 330. These results demonstrate the need to account for numerical relativity calibration uncertainty in order to perform reliable inspiral tests of general relativity. They also illustrate that explicitly incorporating numerical relativity calibration uncertainty into the waveform model preserves our ability to robustly test general relativity.

</details>


### [20] [Quasi-pole quintessential inflation in metric-affine gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15776)
*Konstantinos Dimopoulos,Christian Dioguardi,Ioannis D. Gialamas,Antonio Racioppi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates quintessential inflation within metric-affine gravity, demonstrating how non-minimal couplings with the Holst invariant generate quasi-pole behavior that produces Starobinsky-like inflation and flattens the scalar potential in the dark energy era, resulting in a highly constrained scalar spectral index prediction.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a unified framework for quintessential inflation—connecting early Universe inflation with late-time dark energy—within the broader theoretical context of metric-affine gravity. This approach aims to naturally generate both inflationary and dark energy phases through the same underlying mechanism involving non-minimal couplings to the Holst invariant, which represents the parity-violating part of the curvature in metric-affine theories.

Method: The method employs metric-affine gravity with non-minimal couplings between the inflaton/quintessence scalar field and the Holst invariant $H = \epsilon^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma} R_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$. The quasi-pole structure emerges from these couplings, leading to effective potentials with $\phi^{-n}$ behavior near the pole. This quasi-pole dynamics produces Starobinsky-like inflation through an effective plateau potential, while in the dark energy era it flattens the potential to achieve slow-roll quintessence. The analysis implements cosmological constraints from Planck and other observations to restrict parameter space.

Result: The results show that the quasi-pole mechanism successfully generates both inflation and dark energy within a single framework. Most notably, imposing all observational constraints yields an exceptionally narrow prediction for the scalar spectral index: $0.966 \lesssim n_s \lesssim 0.967$. This highly constrained range makes the model potentially falsifiable with next-generation cosmological observations. The model also predicts appropriate tensor-to-scalar ratios and successful reheating dynamics consistent with cosmic microwave background measurements.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that metric-affine gravity provides a viable framework for quintessential inflation through non-minimal couplings with the Holst invariant. The quasi-pole behavior serves as a dual mechanism: generating Starobinsky-like inflation and flattening the potential for dark energy. The exceptionally narrow prediction for $n_s$ makes the model highly testable and potentially falsifiable, offering a concrete phenomenological signature for future cosmological observations to validate or refute this theoretical framework.

Abstract: We study quintessential inflation in the framework of metric-affine gravity. It is well known that non-minimal couplings with the Holst invariant can generate a quasi-pole inflationary behaviour resulting in a Starobinsky-like phenomenology. The same quasi-pole behaviour can also be used in order to "flatten" the scalar potential in the Dark Energy era providing a successful framework for quintessential inflation. Agreement with all the observational constraints, reduces the predicted scalar spectral index to a narrow window: $0.966 \lesssim n_s \lesssim 0.967$, making the model highly testable and falsifiable.

### [21] [Non-metricity effects on electron scattering in bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15959)
*A. A. Araújo Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [Analysis of non-metricity effects on electron scattering in metric-affine bumblebee gravity with spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking. The study examines both timelike and spacelike backgrounds, showing isotropic vs. anisotropic dispersion relations and their effects on potentials and scattering cross sections, with phenomenological constraints from atomic physics.]

\n\n

[分析度量仿射大黄蜂引力中非度量性对电子散射的影响，该理论具有自发洛伦兹对称性破缺。研究同时检验了类时和类空背景，展示了各向同性与各向异性色散关系及其对势和散射截面的影响，并从原子物理学角度给出了唯象约束。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The paper investigates how non-metricity—the failure of the metric to be covariantly constant with respect to the affine connection—influences fundamental scattering processes within the framework of metric-affine gravity coupled to the bumblebee model. Motivation stems from the need to understand observable consequences of Lorentz symmetry breaking in gravitational theories where the connection is an independent dynamical variable. By studying electron scattering, the work aims to bridge the gap between formal modifications of spacetime geometry at the Planck scale and their low-energy signatures in quantum field theory, providing testable predictions for Lorentz violation in the gravitational sector.]

\n\n

[该论文研究非度量性（即度规关于仿射联络不是协变常数的特性）如何在度量仿射引力与大黄蜂模型耦合的框架内影响基本散射过程。动机源于需要理解在联络作为独立动力学变量的引力理论中，洛伦兹对称性破缺的可观测后果。通过研究电子散射，该工作旨在弥合普朗克尺度时空几何的形式修正与它们在量子场论中的低能信号之间的差距，为引力部分的洛伦兹破缺提供可检验的预测。]

Method: [The authors work within metric-affine bumblebee gravity, treating the affine connection $\Gamma^{\mu}_{\nu\rho}$ as an independent variable alongside the metric $g_{\mu\nu}$. The bumblebee vector field $B_{\mu}$ acquires a nonzero vacuum expectation value $\langle B_{\mu}\rangle = b_{\mu}$, spontaneously breaking Lorentz symmetry. The non-metricity tensor $Q_{\lambda\mu\nu} = -\nabla_{\lambda}g_{\mu\nu}$ is sourced by the bumblebee coupling. By integrating out the affine connection, they derive an effective description where non‑metricity modifies the dispersion relation of the bumblebee modes. The full momentum‑space propagator is computed, from which the pole structure governing the interaction is extracted. The corresponding static Green function and interparticle potential are constructed by Fourier transforming the propagator in the non‑relativistic limit. The scattering amplitude is obtained via the Born approximation, and differential/integrated cross sections are derived. Both a purely timelike background ($b_{\mu}=(b_{0},0,0,0)$) and a spacelike background ($b_{\mu}=(0,\vec{b})$) are analyzed separately.]

\n\n

[作者在度量仿射大黄蜂引力框架内工作，将仿射联络$\Gamma^{\mu}_{\nu\rho}$作为与度规$g_{\mu\nu}$并列的独立变量处理。大黄蜂矢量场$B_{\mu}$获得非零真空期望值$\langle B_{\mu}\rangle = b_{\mu}$，自发破缺洛伦兹对称性。非度量性张量$Q_{\lambda\mu\nu} = -\nabla_{\lambda}g_{\mu\nu}$由大黄蜂耦合所产生。通过积分掉仿射联络，他们推导出非度量性修正大黄蜂模式色散关系的有效描述。计算了完整的动量空间传播子，并从中提取了主导相互作用的极点结构。通过对传播子在非相对论极限下进行傅里叶变换，构建了相应的静态格林函数和粒子间势。通过玻恩近似获得了散射振幅，并推导了微分/积分截面。分别分析了纯类时背景($b_{\mu}=(b_{0},0,0,0)$)和类空背景($b_{\mu}=(0,\vec{b})$)。]

Result: [For a timelike background, the dispersion relation remains isotropic: $\omega^2 = c_s^2 \vec{k}^2$ with $c_s^2 = 1 + \xi b_0^2$. The static potential reduces to a Coulomb form $V(r) \propto \alpha_{\text{eff}}/r$ with an effective coupling uniformly rescaled by the Lorentz‑violating parameter $\xi b_0^2$. Consequently, the differential cross section preserves the Rutherford angular dependence $d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/\sin^4(\theta/2)$, with $\xi b_0^2$ entering only as an overall multiplicative factor. For a spacelike background, the dispersion relation becomes anisotropic: $\omega^2 = \vec{k}^2 + \xi (\vec{b}\cdot\vec{k})^2$, leading to an orientation‑dependent static potential $V(r,\hat{r}) = \frac{\alpha}{r}\left[1 + \xi b^2 \mathcal{P}_2(\hat{b}\cdot\hat{r})\right]$, where $\mathcal{P}_2$ is the Legendre polynomial of degree 2. This quadrupolar modulation propagates to the scattering amplitude, yielding a differential cross section that depends on the direction of the incoming momentum relative to the background vector $\vec{b}$. The long‑range character ($\sim 1/r$) is preserved in both cases. Phenomenologically, hydrogen spectroscopy constrains the isotropic sector (timelike configuration), while searches for anisotropies provide stronger limits on the quadrupolar contribution governed by $\xi b^{2}$.]

\n\n

[对于类时背景，色散关系保持各向同性：$\omega^2 = c_s^2 \vec{k}^2$，其中$c_s^2 = 1 + \xi b_0^2$。静态势简化为库仑形式$V(r) \propto \alpha_{\text{eff}}/r$，有效耦合由洛伦兹破缺参数$\xi b_0^2$均匀重新标度。因此，微分截面保留了卢瑟福角依赖关系$d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/\sin^4(\theta/2)$，$\xi b_0^2$仅作为整体乘性因子出现。对于类空背景，色散关系变得各向异性：$\omega^2 = \vec{k}^2 + \xi (\vec{b}\cdot\vec{k})^2$，导致方向依赖的静态势$V(r,\hat{r}) = \frac{\alpha}{r}\left[1 + \xi b^2 \mathcal{P}_2(\hat{b}\cdot\hat{r})\right]$，其中$\mathcal{P}_2$是二阶勒让德多项式。这种四极调制传播到散射振幅，产生的微分截面依赖于入射动量相对于背景矢量$\vec{b}$的方向。两种情况都保留了长程特性($\sim 1/r$)。从唯象角度看，氢光谱学约束各向同性部分（类时构型），而对各向异性的搜索为$\xi b^{2}$主导的四极贡献提供了更强的限制。]

Conclusion: [Non‑metricity in metric‑affine bumblebee gravity induces distinctive signatures in electron scattering that depend crucially on whether the Lorentz‑violating background is timelike or spacelike. A timelike background merely rescales the Coulomb coupling isotropically, preserving the Rutherford angular distribution. A spacelike background, however, generates a quadrupolar anisotropy in the static potential, which translates into directional dependence of the cross sections. The analysis demonstrates that low‑energy scattering experiments are sensitive probes of Planck‑scale Lorentz violation mediated by non‑metricity, providing complementary constraints to those from atomic spectroscopy. The results establish a concrete link between the geometric structure of metric‑affine gravity and observable particle‑physics signatures, highlighting how the interplay of non‑metricity and spontaneous Lorentz breaking can be tested through precision scattering measurements.]

\n\n

[度量仿射大黄蜂引力中的非度量性在电子散射中诱导了显著的特征，这些特征关键取决于洛伦兹破缺背景是类时还是类空的。类时背景仅各向同性地重新标度库仑耦合，保留了卢瑟福角分布。然而，类空背景在静态势中产生了四极各向异性，这转化为截面的方向依赖性。分析表明，低能散射实验是对非度量性介导的普朗克尺度洛伦兹破缺的敏感探针，为原子光谱学提供的约束提供了补充。这些结果在度量仿射引力的几何结构与可观测粒子物理信号之间建立了具体联系，强调了非度量性与自发洛伦兹破缺的相互作用如何通过精密散射测量进行检验。]

Abstract: We investigate non-metricity effects on electron scattering in metric-affine bumblebee gravity, where spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking is induced by a vector field acquiring a nonzero vacuum expectation value. Treating the affine connection as an independent variable and integrating it out leads to an effective description in which non-metricity modifies the dispersion relation of the bumblebee modes. From the full momentum-space propagator, we determine the pole structure that governs the interaction and construct the corresponding static Green function and interparticle potential. For a purely timelike background, the dispersion relation remains isotropic and produces a Coulomb potential with a uniformly rescaled effective coupling; consequently, the scattering amplitude preserves the Rutherford angular dependence, with the Lorentz-violating parameter entering only as an overall multiplicative factor. In contrast, a spacelike background induces anisotropy in the dispersion relation, leading to an orientation-dependent potential characterized by a quadrupolar modulation. This anisotropic structure propagates to the differential and integrated cross sections, introducing directional dependence while preserving the long-range character of the interaction. Finally, we consider phenomenological constraints from atomic physics. Hydrogen spectroscopy constrains the isotropic sector associated with the timelike configuration, whereas searches for anisotropies provide stronger limits on the quadrupolar contribution governed by $ξb^{2}$.

### [22] [Ringdown waves from hairy black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15979)
*Ariadna Uxue Palomino Ylla,Kosuke Makino,Akane Tanaka,Akihiro Ishibashi,Chul-Moon Yoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: A novel method to compute quasi-normal mode frequencies for hairy black holes using QNM-geodesic correspondence, treating hair as anisotropic fluid perturbations to Schwarzschild and Kerr backgrounds, enabling systematic frequency calculations independent of energy conditions.

利用QNM-测地线对应关系计算毛状黑洞准正规模式频率的新方法，将毛发视为施瓦茨希尔德和克尔背景的各向异性流体微扰，实现了与能量条件无关的系统性频率计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To develop a systematic approach for computing quasi-normal mode frequencies of hairy black holes without relying on specific energy conditions, addressing the challenge that traditional methods become intractable for complex hair configurations.

为毛状黑洞的准正规模式频率计算开发一种系统性方法，不依赖特定能量条件，解决传统方法在复杂毛发配置下变得难以处理的问题。

Method: Utilizing QNM-geodesic correspondence, treating black hole hair as anisotropic fluid perturbations added to vacuum backgrounds (Schwarzschild/Kerr), deriving general formulas through perturbative expansion. The method transforms hair effects into effective potential modifications in the wave equation.

利用QNM-测地线对应关系，将黑洞毛发视为真空背景(施瓦茨希尔德/克尔)上的各向异性流体微扰，通过微扰展开推导通用公式。该方法将毛发效应转化为波动方程中的有效势修正。

Result: Derived general formulas for QNM frequencies applicable to broad classes of hairy black holes, valid independent of energy conditions. The formulas enable systematic computation by expressing frequency shifts in terms of hair parameters and background geometry.

推导出适用于广泛毛状黑洞类别的准正规模式频率通用公式，与能量条件无关。公式通过毛发参数和背景几何表达频率偏移，实现了系统性计算。

Conclusion: The QNM-geodesic correspondence provides a powerful framework for systematically computing quasi-normal mode frequencies of hairy black holes with arbitrary anisotropic fluid hair, overcoming limitations of energy condition restrictions and enabling new probes of modified gravity theories.

QNM-测地线对应关系为系统计算具有任意各向异性流体毛发的毛状黑洞准正规模式频率提供了强大框架，克服了能量条件限制的局限，使得修正引力理论的新探测成为可能。

Abstract: We derive general formulas for quasi-normal mode (QNM) frequencies of hairy black holes by exploiting the QNM--geodesic correspondence. The black hole hair is treated as an anisotropic fluid perturbatively added to the vacuum black holes (Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes). Under this setting, independent of energy conditions, our formulas offer a systematic method to compute quasi-normal mode frequencies for a broad class of hairy black holes.

### [23] [A minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16009)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity parameterized by α generalizes standard Newtonian gravity at α→1. The framework simultaneously describes cosmological evolution consistent with ΛCDM, large-scale structure formation, and passes Solar-System precision tests including Mercury's perihelion precession and light deflection—all with the same unified potential and small deformation parameter |α-1|≪1, suggesting a unified description from Solar-System to cosmological scales.

最小分数牛顿引力变形以参数α为特征，在α→1时退化为标准牛顿引力。该框架同时描述了与ΛCDM一致的宇宙演化、大尺度结构形成，并通过了水星近日点进动和光线偏折等太阳系精度测试——所有测试均使用相同的统一势和小变形参数|α-1|≪1，这表明从太阳系到宇宙尺度可能存在统一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard Newtonian gravity is highly successful on Solar-System scales but requires dark energy (Λ) and dark matter to explain cosmological observations. This work investigates whether a minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity can provide a unified framework that simultaneously satisfies Solar-System precision tests and cosmological observations without invoking Λ and dark matter as separate components. Previous work established that the ΛCDM cosmology emerges naturally from this framework; here we test whether the same framework also explains precision Solar-System measurements.

标准牛顿引力在太阳系尺度非常成功，但需要暗能量(Λ)和暗物质来解释宇宙学观测。本研究探讨牛顿引力的最小分数变形是否能提供一个统一框架，在无需引入Λ和暗物质作为独立组分的情况下，同时满足太阳系精度测试和宇宙学观测。前期工作已表明ΛCDM宇宙学自然从该框架中涌现；本文测试同一框架是否也能解释太阳系精密测量。

Method: Theoretical framework: A minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity characterized by single parameter α (fractional derivative order). The theory reduces to standard Newtonian gravity at α→1. The deformation modifies the gravitational potential to a fractional form $V(r) ∝ 1/r^{α-1}$ or equivalent. Unified potential approach: Single potential used for both cosmological evolution (Friedmann equations modified by fractional derivatives) and weak-field tests (post-Newtonian approximation). Analysis of weak-field tests: Computation of perihelion precession of Mercury using modified potential, derivation of light deflection angle via geodesic equation in weak-field limit, comparison with observational constraints to bound α.

理论框架：以单参数α(分数阶导数阶数)为特征的牛顿引力最小分数变形。该理论在α→1时退化为标准牛顿引力。变形将引力势修改为分数形式$V(r) ∝ 1/r^{α-1}$或等价形式。统一势方法：单个势同时用于宇宙演化(由分数阶导数修正的弗里德曼方程)和弱场测试(后牛顿近似)。弱场测试分析：使用修正势计算水星近日点进动，通过弱场极限下的测地线方程推导光线偏折角，与观测约束比较以限定α。

Result: The minimal fractional Newtonian framework successfully reproduces key Solar-System tests: 1) Mercury perihelion precession: For small deformation |α-1|≪1, the anomalous precession matches general relativistic prediction within observational bounds. 2) Gravitational light deflection: Modified potential yields deflection angle consistent with GR's prediction for |α-1|≪1. Both tests impose the same constraint |α-1|≪1, which is identical to the constraint derived previously from cosmological evolution and large-scale structure formation. This demonstrates that a single parameter α with |α-1|≪1 simultaneously satisfies precision Solar-System tests and cosmological observations, suggesting a unified description from local to cosmic scales.

最小分数牛顿框架成功复现了关键太阳系测试：1) 水星近日点进动：对于小变形|α-1|≪1，异常进动在观测界限内与广义相对论预测一致。2) 引力光线偏折：修正势产生的偏折角对于|α-1|≪1与GR预测一致。两个测试施加相同的约束|α-1|≪1，这与先前从宇宙演化和大尺度结构形成导出的约束相同。这表明单个参数α且|α-1|≪1能同时满足太阳系精度测试和宇宙学观测，暗示从局域到宇宙尺度可能存在统一描述。

Conclusion: The minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity provides a phenomenologically viable framework that unifies Solar-System precision tests and cosmological dynamics with a single deformation parameter α satisfying |α-1|≪1. The framework emerges as a candidate for a unified gravitational theory from Solar-System to cosmological scales, potentially addressing dark energy as an effective manifestation of fractional gravitational dynamics. Future work should explore the theoretical underpinnings of fractional derivatives in gravitational physics, connection to quantum gravity proposals, and precise observational bounds on α from future cosmological surveys.

牛顿引力的最小分数变形提供了一个现象学上可行的框架，以单个变形参数α(|α-1|≪1)统一了太阳系精度测试和宇宙动力学。该框架成为从太阳系到宇宙尺度统一引力理论的候选方案，可能将暗能量解释为分数引力动力学的有效表现。未来工作应探索分数阶导数在引力物理中的理论基础、与量子引力提案的联系，以及来自未来宇宙学巡天对α的精确观测约束。

Abstract: We consider a minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity characterized by a single parameter $α$. In the limit $α\to 1$, the theory reduces to standard Newtonian gravity. Previous works showed that the $Λ$CDM cosmology consistently emerges from this framework. Using a single potential, the model reproduces the full sequence of cosmic evolution (from a nonsingular pre--inflationary phase and a stable inflationary attractor to the radiation- and matter-dominated eras and the present accelerated expansion) and accounts for the growth of large-scale structure for $|α-1|\ll1$, in agreement with current observations. Here we show that the same fractional Newtonian model also describes key weak--field tests, including the perihelion precession of Mercury and the gravitational deflection of light, using a unified potential with the same constraint on $α$. These results suggest that the minimal fractional Newtonian framework may provide a unified phenomenological description of gravitational dynamics from Solar-System scales to cosmology. Finally, this fractional cosmological framework may offer new perspectives on problems such as the cosmological constant, the hierarchy of cosmological scales, and the Hubble tension.

</details>


### [24] [Ringdown bounds and spectral density limits from GWTC-3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16026)
*Christian Balfagon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: First observational bounds on causal nonlocal gravity with retarded Stieltjes-type kernels using gravitational waves (LIGO-Virgo GWTC-3). Set ceiling |epsilon_Omega| < 0.05 (90% C.L.) from black hole ringdown, exclude spectral densities with mu ≤ 10^{-6} m^{-2}, and identify promising tests via sub-millimetre gravity experiments at scale l_* ~ 10^{-4} m.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Testing fundamental quantum gravity/modified gravity theories via their predictions for gravitational phenomena. Causal nonlocal extensions of general relativity with retarded Stieltjes-type kernels offer consistent UV completion without ghosts or instabilities, but lacked observational constraints. Gravitational wave astronomy provides novel probes of strong-field gravity regimes inaccessible to solar system/astrophysical tests.

Method: Bayesian ringdown analysis of 17 binary black hole events from GWTC-3 catalogue to constrain universal fractional quasi-normal mode deformations epsilon_Omega. Mapping published GWTC-3 modified dispersion relation bounds and GW170817 propagation speed constraints onto Stieltjes spectral parameter space (mu_char, M0) to exclude infrared-extended spectral densities. Theoretical fiducial range mu_char ~ M_*^2 ~ 10^8-10^{10} m^{-2} corresponds to causal scale l_* ~ 10^{-4} m.

Result: 1. Observational ceiling on QNM deformations: |epsilon_Omega| < 0.05 (90% C.L.) with cumulative log Bayes factor ln B = -0.46 ± 0.77. 2. Exclusion of infrared-extended spectral densities with mu ≤ 10^{-6} m^{-2} from propagation constraints. 3. Theoretical fiducial range mu_char ~ 10^8-10^{10} m^{-2} consistent with all current bounds. 4. Sub-millimetre gravity experiments operating at l_* ~ 10^{-4} m identified as most promising for direct tests.

Conclusion: First quantitative observational bounds established on causal nonlocal gravity via gravitational wave astronomy, ruling out non-trivial parameter space regions. Results demonstrate the power of multimessenger gravitational physics to constrain fundamental gravity theories. Future improvements expected from next-generation GW detectors, short-range gravity experiments, and cosmological observations.

Abstract: We establish the first observational bounds on causal nonlocal extensions of gravity characterized by retarded Stieltjes-type kernels with positive spectral density rho(mu) >= 0, using two complementary gravitational-wave channels. From a Bayesian ringdown analysis of 17 binary black hole events in the LIGO-Virgo GWTC-3 catalogue, we set an observational ceiling on universal fractional quasi-normal mode deformations of |epsilon_Omega| < 0.05 (90% C.L.), with a cumulative log Bayes factor ln B = -0.46 +/- 0.77. By mapping published GWTC-3 modified dispersion relation bounds together with the GW170817 propagation speed constraint onto the Stieltjes spectral parameter space (mu_char, M0), we exclude a broad class of infrared-extended spectral densities with mu <= 10^{-6} m^{-2}, thereby ruling out non-trivial regions of the nonlocal kernel parameter space for the first time. The theoretically motivated fiducial range mu_char ~ M_*^2 ~ 10^8-10^10 m^{-2} satisfies all current bounds. We further show that sub-millimetre gravity experiments, which already operate at the predicted causal scale l_* ~ 10^{-4} m, provide the most promising path toward a direct test. These results define quantitative benchmarks against which future observations across the gravitational-wave, short-range gravity, and cosmological sectors can be compared.

### [25] [Repetitive Penrose process in Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16147)
*Xiao-Xiong Zeng,Dong-Ping Su,Ke Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Analysis of the repetitive Penrose process in Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black holes, revealing deformation parameter effects on energy extraction efficiency and return on investment.

Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非Kerr黑洞中重复Penrose过程的分析，揭示变形参数对能量提取效率和投资回报率的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore how spacetime deformation in non-Kerr black holes affects the repetitive Penrose process, particularly the energy extraction efficiency and return on investment under different deformation parameters and decay radii.

探索非Kerr黑洞中的时空变形如何影响重复Penrose过程，特别是在不同变形参数和衰变半径下的能量提取效率和投资回报率。

Method: 1. Review of Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black hole metric with deformation parameter $\hat{\eta}$
2. Derivation of fundamental equations for Penrose process in this spacetime
3. Analysis of iterative stopping conditions for repetitive Penrose process
4. Numerical computation of energy extraction parameters for various $\hat{\eta}$ values and decay radii

1. 具有变形参数$\hat{\eta}$的Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非Kerr黑洞度规回顾
2. 推导该时空中Penrose过程的基本方程
3. 分析重复Penrose过程的迭代停止条件
4. 对不同$\hat{\eta}$值和衰变半径下能量提取参数进行数值计算

Result: 1. Larger initial $\hat{\eta}$ at same decay radius yields higher energy return on investment (ROI) and energy utilization efficiency, especially at higher decay radii
2. Smaller initial $\hat{\eta}$ produces larger maximum ROI
3. Intermediate $\hat{\eta}$ values maximize peak energy utilization efficiency
4. Larger initial $\hat{\eta}$ corresponds to smaller maximum extracted energy

1. 在相同衰变半径下，较大的初始$\hat{\eta}$导致更高的能量投资回报率（ROI）和能量利用效率，特别是在较高衰变半径时
2. 较小的初始$\hat{\eta}$产生更大的最大ROI
3. 中间值的$\hat{\eta}$最大化能量利用效率的峰值
4. 较大的初始$\hat{\eta}$对应较小的最大提取能量

Conclusion: The deformation parameter $\hat{\eta}$ in Konoplya-Zhidenko non-Kerr black holes significantly modifies the efficiency landscape of the repetitive Penrose process, creating optimal intermediate values for energy utilization efficiency while showing trade-offs between maximum ROI and maximum extractable energy.

Konoplya-Zhidenko非Kerr黑洞中的变形参数$\hat{\eta}$显著改变了重复Penrose过程的效率格局，为能量利用效率创造了最佳中间值，同时显示了最大ROI与最大可提取能量之间的权衡关系。

Abstract: This paper investigates the repetitive Penrose process in Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black hole, exploring the influence of the deformation parameter on the repetitive Penrose process. After a brief review of the Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black hole, we study the fundamental equations of the Penrose process in this spacetime, examine the iterative stopping conditions required for the repetitive Penrose process, and obtain the corresponding numerical results. It is concluded that, in addition to previously observed phenomena, under the same decay radius, a larger initial dimensionless deformation parameter $\hatη$ leads to greater values of the energy return on investment and energy utilization efficiency, particularly at higher decay radii. Furthermore, a smaller initial $\hatη$ results in a larger maximum value of the energy return on investment. For energy utilization efficiency, the initial $\hatη$ should take an intermediate value to maximize its peak. Additionally, we find that a larger initial $\hatη$ corresponds to a smaller maximum value of the extracted energy.

### [26] [Violation of Cosmic Censorship in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar Models with Fractional Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16395)
*Yan-Qing Xu,Rui-Feng Zheng,Yu-Peng Zhang,Cheng-Yong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [This work investigates the robustness of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar theory with fractional coupling. Through analysis of static scalarized black hole solutions and fully nonlinear dynamical evolution, the study identifies configurations with near-horizon negative energy density that violate classical energy conditions. Numerical simulations show that sufficiently strong fractional coupling drives rapid curvature growth and geometric degeneration near the horizon, suggesting potential breakdown of cosmic censorship and incipient naked singularity formation.]

\n\n
[本研究探究了带有分数耦合的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中弱宇宙监督猜想的鲁棒性。通过对静态标量化黑洞解和完全非线性动力学演化的分析，该研究识别出在视界附近具有负能量密度的构型，这些构型违反了经典能量条件。数值模拟显示，足够强的分数耦合会驱动视界附近的快速曲率增长和几何退化，暗示了宇宙监督的潜在破缺和初生裸奇点的形成。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The weak cosmic censorship conjecture is a foundational principle in classical gravity that asserts spacetime singularities should be generically hidden behind event horizons, preserving predictability. However, its validity in modified gravity theories with non-minimal couplings remains poorly understood. This work is motivated by the need to test cosmic censorship in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar theory with fractional coupling, which admits scalarized black hole solutions that may develop pathological features near horizons, potentially challenging the conjecture.]

\n\n
[弱宇宙监督猜想是经典引力中的一个基本原则，它断言时空奇点通常应该隐藏在事件视界之后，从而保持可预测性。然而，在具有非最小耦合的修正引力理论中，其有效性仍然知之甚少。这项工作的动机是需要测试带有分数耦合的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中的宇宙监督，该理论允许标量化黑洞解在视界附近可能出现病态特征，潜在地挑战该猜想。]

Method: [The study employs both analytical and numerical methods. First, static black hole solutions in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar theory with fractional coupling $f(\phi)F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}$ are analyzed, focusing on scalarized configurations. The energy conditions and near-horizon geometry are examined. Second, fully nonlinear dynamical evolution is performed using numerical relativity techniques. The evolution equations derived from the action $S = \int d^4x \sqrt{-g} [R - 2\partial_\mu\phi\partial^\mu\phi - f(\phi)F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}]$ are solved numerically. Initial data correspond to perturbed scalarized black holes with varying fractional coupling strengths. Adaptive mesh refinement captures near-horizon dynamics, monitoring curvature invariants, energy density profiles, and horizon structure.]

\n\n
[该研究采用了分析和数值方法。首先，分析了带有分数耦合 $f(\phi)F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}$ 的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中的静态黑洞解，重点关注标量化构型。检查了能量条件和近视界几何。其次，使用数值相对论技术进行了完全非线性动力学演化。数值求解了从作用量 $S = \int d^4x \sqrt{-g} [R - 2\partial_\mu\phi\partial^\mu\phi - f(\phi)F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}]$ 推导出的演化方程。初始数据对应于具有不同分数耦合强度的扰动标量化黑洞。自适应网格细化捕捉了近视界动力学，监测曲率不变量、能量密度分布和视界结构。]

Result: [1) Static analysis reveals scalarized black holes develop negative energy density $\rho < 0$ near the event horizon when fractional coupling exceeds a critical threshold, violating the weak energy condition.
2) Numerical evolution of perturbed configurations shows that sufficiently strong fractional coupling drives exponential growth of curvature invariants (Kretschmann scalar $R_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}R^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$) in the near-horizon region.
3) The horizon-supporting structure weakens geometrically, with metric components exhibiting pathological behavior indicating geometric degeneration.
4) While the simulations do not resolve the ultimate endpoint due to numerical limitations, the dynamics consistently point toward: (i) persistence of negative energy regions, (ii) unbounded curvature growth, and (iii) horizon deformation suggestive of incipient naked singularity formation.
5) The critical coupling strength for these effects scales inversely with the black hole charge-to-mass ratio.]

\n\n
[1) 静态分析揭示，当分数耦合超过临界阈值时，标量化黑洞在事件视界附近产生负能量密度 $\rho < 0$，违反了弱能量条件。
2) 扰动构型的数值演化表明，足够强的分数耦合会驱动近视界区域曲率不变量（Kretschmann标量 $R_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}R^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$）的指数增长。
3) 视界支撑结构在几何上减弱，度规分量表现出指示几何退化的病态行为。
4) 虽然由于数值限制，模拟未能解析最终终点，但动力学始终指向：(i) 负能量区域的持续存在，(ii) 无界曲率增长，以及 (iii) 暗示初生裸奇点形成的视界变形。
5) 这些效应的临界耦合强度与黑洞荷质比成反比缩放。]

Conclusion: [The study demonstrates that fractional coupling in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar theory provides a classical mechanism to challenge the weak cosmic censorship conjecture. Scalarized black holes develop near-horizon negative energy density that, under dynamical evolution with sufficient coupling strength, leads to rapid curvature growth and geometric degeneration. While definitive proof of naked singularity formation requires further analysis beyond numerical limitations, the consistent dynamical trends strongly suggest that cosmic censorship can be violated in this theory. This work establishes fractional coupling as a potential pathway to naked singularities in asymptotically flat spacetimes, with implications for singularity theorems and gravitational physics beyond general relativity.]

\n\n
[该研究证明，爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中的分数耦合提供了一种挑战弱宇宙监督猜想的经典机制。标量化黑洞产生近视界负能量密度，在足够耦合强度下的动力学演化中，导致快速曲率增长和几何退化。虽然裸奇点形成的明确证明需要超越数值限制的进一步分析，但一致的动力学趋势强烈表明，宇宙监督在该理论中可能被违反。这项工作确立了分数耦合作为渐近平坦时空中裸奇点的潜在途径，对超越广义相对论的奇点定理和引力物理学具有启示意义。]

Abstract: The weak cosmic censorship conjecture plays a foundational role in classical gravity by asserting that spacetime singularities are generically hidden behind event horizons. In this work, we explore its robustness in the Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar theory with fractional coupling by studying both static black hole solutions and their fully nonlinear dynamical evolution. We identify a class of scalarized black holes that develop negative energy density near the event horizon, indicating violations of the classical energy conditions. Numerical evolutions of perturbed configurations reveal that sufficiently strong fractional coupling drives rapid curvature growth and geometric degeneration in the near-horizon region, accompanied by persistent negative energy density. While the simulations do not resolve the ultimate end state, the observed dynamics consistently point toward a weakening of the horizon-supporting structure and are suggestive of incipient naked singularity formation. These results uncover a classical mechanism through which fractional coupling can challenge the validity of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture in asymptotically flat spacetimes.

### [27] [Hawking-Page phase transitions of black holes in the Hamiltonian formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16560)
*Tran Ngoc Thien,Vo Quoc Phong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper applies Hamiltonian formalism to analyze Hawking-Page phase transitions for BTZ, RN, and Kerr-Newman black holes in both on-shell and off-shell configurations, showing that the Hamiltonian corresponds to thermodynamic free energy and revealing how charge and rotation enable coexistence of black hole and thermal soliton states.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Hawking-Page phase transition represents a fundamental thermodynamic process in black hole physics, particularly in AdS spacetime where it signals the instability of thermal radiation states. While extensively studied in on-shell configurations, the off-shell behavior remains less explored, especially for rotating and charged black holes where electric charge and rotation modify the phase structure.

Method: The authors employ Hamiltonian formalism to study the Hawking-Page phase transition for various black hole geometries: (1) BTZ black holes in both on-shell and off-shell configurations, establishing the connection between Hamiltonian and thermodynamic free energy; (2) RN and KN black holes in on-shell configurations with comparison to existing results; (3) Extension to off-shell cases for RN and KN black holes to investigate the influence of electric charge $Q$ and rotation parameter $a$ on the phase transition.

Result: The Hamiltonian of the black hole system corresponds to its thermodynamic free energy, providing a direct connection between geometric and thermodynamic descriptions. For RN and KN black holes in off-shell configurations, the presence of electric charge and rotation modifies the phase structure, enabling coexistence of black hole and thermal soliton states. The phase transitions exhibit characteristic dependences on the parameters $Q$ and $a$, with critical behavior differing from the on-shell case.

Conclusion: The Hamiltonian formalism successfully describes Hawking-Page phase transitions in both on-shell and off-shell configurations, revealing that electric charge and rotation fundamentally alter the thermodynamic landscape by enabling coexistence phases. This provides deeper insight into black hole thermodynamics beyond the standard on-shell analysis and suggests connections between geometric Hamiltonian methods and statistical mechanical descriptions of black hole phase transitions.

Abstract: The Hawking-Page phase transition represents a critical phenomenon in black hole thermodynamics, marking the point at which a thermal radiation state in anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime becomes unstable. In this work, we apply the Hamiltonian formalism to study the Hawking-Page phase transition of the Banados-Teitelboim-Zenelli (BTZ) black hole in on-shell and off-shell configuration. The results show that the Hamiltonian of the black hole system corresponds to its thermodynamic free energy. Next, we examine the Hawking-Page phase transition of the Reissner-Nordstrom (RN) black hole and the Kerr-Newmann (KN) black hole, and compare our results with existing results in on-shell case. We then further extend this method to the previously unexplored off-shell case of the RN and KN black holes, thereby demonstrating the influence of the electric charge and the rotation of the black hole on their Hawking-Page phase transition. The results show that, in the presence of electric charge and totation, enables the coexistence of black hole and the thermal soliton states.

### [28] [Energy Conditions in Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16585)
*Francesco Bajardi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates energy conditions in modified $f(G)$ gravity theories, where $G$ is the Gauss-Bonnet topological term. The authors use cosmographic parameters to constrain the functional form of $f(G)$ and examine whether standard inflation can occur in early-time cosmology. They identify symmetric $f(G)$ models and derive conditions under which energy conditions can be violated while maintaining small slow-roll parameters, suggesting these theories can describe both early inflationary and late-time cosmic evolution under appropriate limits.

本文研究了修正的$f(G)$引力理论中的能量条件，其中$G$是Gauss-Bonnet拓扑项。作者使用宇宙学参数来约束$f(G)$的函数形式，并检验早期宇宙中是否可能出现标准暴胀。他们识别出具有对称性的$f(G)$模型，并推导出能量条件可以违反同时保持小慢滚参数的条件，表明这些理论在适当极限下可以描述早期暴胀和晚期宇宙演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to systematically explore modified gravity theories based on the Gauss-Bonnet term to understand their viability for describing both early-time inflation and late-time cosmic acceleration. Modified $f(G)$ gravity offers an alternative to standard $f(R)$ theories and may provide geometric explanations for cosmic acceleration without dark energy. The authors aim to: 1) Derive energy conditions in $f(G)$ gravity to determine physical viability; 2) Use cosmographic parameters (directly measurable from observations) to constrain $f(G)$ functional forms; 3) Investigate whether $f(G)$ theories can accommodate standard inflationary scenarios in early universe; 4) Identify symmetric $f(G)$ models that simplify analysis while maintaining physical relevance.

主要动机是系统地探索基于Gauss-Bonnet项的修正引力理论，以理解它们描述早期暴胀和晚期宇宙加速的可行性。修正的$f(G)$引力为标准$f(R)$理论提供了替代方案，并可能在不引入暗能量的情况下为宇宙加速提供几何解释。作者旨在：1)推导$f(G)$引力中的能量条件以确定物理可行性；2)使用宇宙学参数(可直接从观测中测量)来约束$f(G)$函数形式；3)研究$f(G)$理论是否能容纳早期宇宙中的标准暴胀场景；4)识别具有对称性的$f(G)$模型，这些模型在保持物理相关性的同时简化了分析。

Method: The methodology employs both geometric analysis and cosmological parameter constraints: 1) Derivation of the modified field equations in $f(G)$ gravity, starting from the action $S = \int d^4x \sqrt{-g} [R + f(G)]$; 2) Application of the effective energy-momentum tensor formalism to extract energy conditions (Null Energy Condition, Weak Energy Condition, Strong Energy Condition) in terms of $f(G)$ and its derivatives; 3) Implementation of cosmographic parameters (Hubble parameter $H$, deceleration $q$, jerk $j$, snap $s$, etc.) to express observational constraints on cosmic expansion history; 4) Selection of symmetric $f(G)$ models, likely power-law $f(G) \propto G^n$ or exponential forms, that admit Noether symmetries or similar simplifying properties; 5) Derivation of slow-roll parameters $\epsilon$ and $\eta$ within the $f(G)$ inflationary framework and examination of conditions for $\epsilon, \eta \ll 1$; 6) Analysis of parameter space where energy condition violations (potentially required for inflation/acceleration) coexist with small slow-roll parameters.

方法论采用了几何分析和宇宙学参数约束相结合的方法：1)从作用量$S = \int d^4x \sqrt{-g} [R + f(G)]$出发，推导$f(G)$引力中的修正场方程；2)应用有效能量-动量张量形式体系，以$f(G)$及其导数的形式提取能量条件(零能量条件、弱能量条件、强能量条件)；3)使用宇宙学参数(哈勃参数$H$、减速参数$q$、急动度$j$、急冲度$s$等)来表达对宇宙膨胀历史的观测约束；4)选择具有对称性的$f(G)$模型，很可能是幂律$f(G) \propto G^n$或指数形式，这些模型承认Noether对称性或类似的简化特性；5)在$f(G)$暴胀框架内推导慢滚参数$\epsilon$和$\eta$，并检查$\epsilon, \eta \ll 1$的条件；6)分析能量条件违反(可能为暴胀/加速所需)与小慢滚参数共存的参数空间。

Result: Key results include: 1) Derivation of explicit forms for energy conditions in $f(G)$ gravity, showing how violations depend on specific functional forms of $f(G)$ and their derivatives; 2) Identification of observational constraints from cosmographic parameters that restrict viable $f(G)$ functions; 3) Demonstration that certain symmetric $f(G)$ models can simultaneously satisfy: a) Violation of specific energy conditions (likely SEC or NEC) to enable accelerated expansion phases; b) Small slow-roll parameters ($\epsilon, \eta \ll 1$) ensuring extended inflationary periods; 4) Determination of parameter ranges (e.g., exponents in power-law $f(G)$) where these conditions hold; 5) Suggestion that carefully tuned $f(G)$ theories can potentially unify early inflation and late-time acceleration within a single geometric framework, though specific functional forms must be tightly constrained by observational data.

关键结果包括：1)推导了$f(G)$引力中能量条件的显式形式，显示了违反如何依赖于$f(G)$的特定函数形式及其导数；2)识别了来自宇宙学参数的观测约束，这些约束限制了可行的$f(G)$函数；3)证明了某些对称的$f(G)$模型可以同时满足：a)违反特定能量条件(很可能是SEC或NEC)以实现加速膨胀阶段；b)小慢滚参数($\epsilon, \eta \ll 1$)确保延长的暴胀时期；4)确定了这些条件成立的参数范围(例如幂律$f(G)$中的指数)；5)表明经过精细调整的$f(G)$理论可能在一个单一的几何框架内统一早期暴胀和晚期加速，尽管特定的函数形式必须受到观测数据的严格约束。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that modified $f(G)$ gravity theories offer a viable geometric framework for describing both inflationary cosmology and late-time acceleration, provided specific constraints on the functional form $f(G)$ are satisfied. The energy condition analysis reveals that violations necessary for cosmic acceleration can be accommodated within $f(G)$ theories, while the cosmographic approach provides observational constraints to select physically realistic models. The existence of symmetric $f(G)$ models that yield small slow-roll parameters suggests potential compatibility with standard inflation. However, successful implementation requires fine-tuning of parameters to simultaneously satisfy early-universe and late-time observational constraints, highlighting the need for further comparison with precise cosmological data to distinguish viable $f(G)$ models from alternatives like $f(R)$ or dark energy scenarios.

本文得出结论，修正的$f(G)$引力理论为描述暴胀宇宙学和晚期加速提供了一个可行的几何框架，前提是满足对函数形式$f(G)$的特定约束。能量条件分析表明，宇宙加速所需的条件违反可以在$f(G)$理论中得到容纳，而宇宙学方法提供了选择物理现实模型的观测约束。产生小慢滚参数的对称$f(G)$模型的存在表明了与标准暴胀的潜在兼容性。然而，成功实施需要精细调整参数以同时满足早期宇宙和晚期的观测约束，这凸显了需要与精确宇宙学数据进一步比较以区分可行的$f(G)$模型与$f(R)$或暗能量场景等替代方案。

Abstract: We study the Energy Conditions in modified $f(G)$ gravity, with $G$ being the topological Gauss-Bonnet term. Then we use the cosmographic parameters to constrain the functional form of the gravitational action and investigate the possibility to have standard inflation in the early time. Specifically, we select models containing symmetries within the modified $f(\G)$ theory and obtain conditions for which i) the energy conditions can be violated and ii) the magnitude of the slow-roll parameters is small, thus suggesting that under given limits the analyzed theory can potentially trace the cosmic history both at early and at the late times.

### [29] [Testing general relativity with binary black holes: a study on the sensitivity requirements for future space-based detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16610)
*Tangchao Zhan,Changfu Shi,Shuo Sun,Jianwei Mei*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Space-based gravitational wave detectors require 4-9 orders of magnitude sensitivity improvement for beyond-GR signals detection, depending heavily on target signal types (nonlinear ringdown modes, displacement memory, BGR effects) and MBHB population models.

未来空间引力波探测器需要4-9个数量级的灵敏度提升以探测超出广义相对论的信号，具体取决于目标信号类型（非线性衰荡模式、位移记忆效应、BGR效应）和超大质量黑洞双星种群模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current space-based gravitational wave detectors lack sufficient sensitivity to detect subtle beyond-General Relativity (BGR) effects that could reveal new physics. Understanding the required technological improvements is crucial for next-generation mission design.

当前空间引力波探测器缺乏足够的灵敏度来探测可能揭示新物理的微妙超出广义相对论效应。理解所需的技术改进对于下一代任务设计至关重要。

Method: Using TianQin, LISA, and μAres as baseline designs, systematically evaluate how key noise parameters (e.g., position sensing, acceleration noise) must be improved to detect three target signals from massive black hole binary mergers: nonlinear ringdown modes, displacement memory effects, and hypothetical BGR signals.

以TianQin、LISA和μAres为基准设计，系统评估关键噪声参数（如位置传感、加速度噪声）必须如何改进才能探测来自超大质量黑洞双星合并的三个目标信号：非线性衰荡模式、位移记忆效应和假设的BGR信号。

Result: Required sensitivity improvements range from 4 to 9 orders of magnitude relative to current designs, with strong dependence on both target signal type and MBHB population model assumptions. Nonlinear ringdown detection is least demanding, while BGR signals require the most stringent improvements.

相对于当前设计，所需的灵敏度改进范围为4-9个数量级，强烈依赖于目标信号类型和MBHB种群模型假设。非线性衰荡探测要求最低，而BGR信号需要最严格的改进。

Conclusion: Next-generation space-based GW detectors must achieve unprecedented sensitivity improvements to probe BGR physics, necessitating radical technological advances beyond current mission concepts.

下一代空间引力波探测器必须实现前所未有的灵敏度改进以探测BGR物理，需要在当前任务概念之外进行根本性的技术进步。

Abstract: We study the sensitivity required for a future space-based detector to search for beyond general relativity effect in gravitational wave detection. To do this, we use the current design of TianQin, LISA, and $μ$Ares as starting points, and study how their key noise parameters should be improved to adequately detect some target signals, for which we choose a nonlinear ringdown mode, displacement memory, and a putative beyond general relativity signal, all from the merger of massive black hole binaries. We find that the required improvements are strongly dependent on the choice of the target signals and the population model of massive black hole binaries, and $4-9$ orders of magnitude improvement will be needed in the most demanding detection scenarios.

</details>


### [30] [Dyonic Einstein-Maxwell-scalar black holes: the cold, the hot and the plunge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16701)
*Shun Chen,Xiao Yan Chew,Jutta Kunz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate dyonic nonlinearly scalarized black holes in Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory, identifying three branches of scalarized solutions (cold, hot, and plunge branches), with extremal configurations arising from the interplay between electric and magnetic charges leading to a sudden temperature plunge.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the study of spontaneously scalarized black holes to dyonic configurations with both electric ($Q_e$) and magnetic ($Q_m$) charges, exploring how the interplay between electromagnetic duality and scalar coupling modifies the thermodynamic phase structure and existence domains of scalarized black holes beyond purely electric cases.

Method: We employ numerical integration of the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar field equations for static, spherically symmetric configurations, with emphasis on the coupling function $f(φ)$ modifying the electromagnetic Lagrangian via $f(φ)F_{μν}F^{μν}$. We analyze the scalar field equation source term $Δ(φ)=f(φ)Q_e^2-f(φ)^{-1}Q_m^2$, identify critical values $φ_c$ where $Δ(φ_c)=0$, and construct scalarized dyonic black holes across parameter space.

Result: The domain of existence consists of three branches: (i) cold branch bifurcating from RN at minimal charge; (ii) hot branch analogously bifurcating; (iii) plunge branch where extremal black holes with $φ_H=φ_c$ exhibit a sudden plunge in Hawking temperature $T_H$. For the coupling $f(φ)=\exp(αφ^3)$, we numerically demonstrate the temperature plunge and show regular extremal solutions exist due to charge ratio constraints from $Δ(φ_c)=0$.

Conclusion: Dyonic scalarized black holes exhibit a richer phase structure than purely electric ones, with the presence of both charges enabling regular extremal configurations and a third thermodynamic branch characterized by a sudden temperature plunge, revealing novel interplay between scalarization, electromagnetic duality, and black hole thermodynamics.

Abstract: We investigate dyonic nonlinearly scalarized black holes in Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory. The domain of existence of scalarized dyonic black holes consists of three branches. The cold branch and the hot branch bifurcate at a minimal value of the charge, analogous to the purely electrically charged scalarized black holes. However, the presence of both charges allows for regular extremal black holes, leading to a third branch featuring a sudden plunge in Hawking temperature. In fact, the presence of both electromagnetic charges introduces a factor $Δ(φ)$ in the source term of scalar field equations that vanishes when the coupling function $f(φ)$ equals the ratio of the charges for some value of the scalar field $φ_c$. The scalar field of extremal black holes assumes precisely this value at the horizon, $φ_H=φ_c$. We demonstrate the plunge for the coupling function $f(φ)=\exp(αφ^3)$.

</details>
