### [31] [Baryon Asymmetry of the Universe from Preon Confinement and Supersymmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15694)
*Risto Raitio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Supersymmetric preon confinement at Λ_cr~10¹⁴ GeV generates BAU via anomaly inflow from Chern-Simons term induced by preon integration, with SUSY breaking from differential fermion/boson condensation providing out-of-equilibrium conditions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The baryon asymmetry of the universe requires a viable mechanism beyond Standard Model electroweak baryogenesis. Most models either assume topological structures or rely on statistical departures from equilibrium. This paper aims to derive BAU from first principles in a supersymmetric preon model, where confinement itself provides both the topological structure (via anomaly inflow) and the departure from equilibrium (via differential condensation).

Method: The model builds on a supersymmetric preon theory with U(1)×SU(3) internal symmetry. At confinement scale Λ_cr ~ 10¹⁴ GeV, integrating out massive preons generates a Chern-Simons term in the effective gauge action through the Callan-Harvey anomaly inflow mechanism. Confinement triggers supersymmetry breaking intrinsically due to asymmetric condensation of fermionic and bosonic preon composites, providing the necessary departure from thermal equilibrium. The time-varying CS coefficient sources net topological charge, converted to baryon number via anomaly equation. Electroweak sphalerons are out of equilibrium at Λ_cr, protecting asymmetry.

Result: The mechanism produces observed baryon-to-entropy ratio η ~ 8.7×10⁻¹⁰, constraining the fermion/boson condensation asymmetry to ε ≃ 0.022, consistent with one-loop origin. The BAU generation is structural (derived from anomaly inflow) rather than statistical, and operates independently of electroweak phase transition.

Conclusion: Supersymmetric preon confinement provides a novel, first-principles mechanism for BAU generation where topological structure emerges from anomaly inflow and departure from equilibrium arises intrinsically from differential condensation. The mechanism is structurally robust and bypasses electroweak sphaleron washout while matching observed asymmetry with reasonable parameters.

Abstract: We propose a mechanism for generating the baryon asymmetry of the universe (BAU) within a supersymmetric preon model based on $U(1)\times SU(3)$ internal symmetry. Integrating out massive preons at the confinement scale $Λ_{cr} \sim 10^{14}$ GeV induces a Chern-Simons (CS) term in the effective gauge action via the Callan-Harvey anomaly inflow mechanism, deriving rather than assuming the topological structure required for the model. The confinement transition, at which supersymmetry breaks intrinsically through the differential condensation of fermionic and bosonic preon composites, provides the necessary departure from thermal equilibrium. The time-varying CS coefficient sources a net topological charge, which the anomaly equation converts directly into baryon number. Electroweak sphalerons are out of equilibrium at $Λ_{cr}$, protecting the asymmetry from immediate washout. Matching the observed baryon-to-entropy ratio $η\sim 8.7\times 10^{-10}$ constrains the fermion/boson condensation asymmetry to $ε\simeq 0.022$, a value consistent with a one-loop origin. This mechanism is structural rather than statistical, and the electroweak phase transition plays no role.

</details>


### [32] [A Special $E_6\to G(2) \times SU(3)_A$ Embedding for Standard Model and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15710)
*Nicolò Masi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A novel $E_6$ grand unification with a special embedding yielding $E_6 \\to G(2) \\times SU(3)_A$. The model produces the Standard Model via sequential breaking while generating a hidden confining $G(2)$ dark sector. It suppresses proton decay, unifies gauge couplings, and provides a secluded dark matter candidate.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard grand unified theories (GUTs) based on regular embeddings often face proton decay constraints, require ad-hoc scalar sectors, and lack natural dark matter candidates. The motivation is to construct a minimal $E_6$-based framework that (1) naturally suppresses dangerous proton decay operators, (2) provides a self-contained dark sector via exceptional group structure, (3) achieves gauge coupling unification without excessive fine-tuning, and (4) maintains consistency with cosmological observations including inflation and topological defects.

标准大统一理论（GUTs）基于常规嵌入，通常面临质子衰变限制、需要特殊标量场、并缺乏自然的暗物质候选者。本研究的动机是构建一个基于$E_6$的最小框架，能够(1)自然地抑制危险的质子衰变算符，(2)通过例外群结构提供一个自包含的暗物质区，(3)在没有过度微调的情况下实现规范耦合常数统一，(4)保持与宇宙学观测（包括暴胀和拓扑缺陷）的一致性。

Method: The core mathematical innovation is the use of a special (non-regular) embedding of $E_6$ that yields the breaking chain $E_6 \\to G(2) \\times SU(3)_A$. The exceptional subgroup $G(2)$ serves as the hidden confining dark sector, while $SU(3)_A$ is the progenitor of the electroweak gauge group $SU(2)_L \\times U(1)_Y$. Hypercharge $Y$ is defined as $Y = \\sqrt{3}\\,t_{8}^{(A)}$, where $t_{8}$ is the diagonal generator of $SU(3)_A$. The Standard Model Higgs is identified within a larger exceptional representation ($\\mathbf{27}$ of $E_6$). The scalar potential involves three Higgs sectors corresponding to the different symmetry-breaking steps. Gauge coupling unification is verified via one-loop renormalization group equations (RGEs) across intermediate scales $M_{G(2)}$ and $M_A$. Exotic states from the $\\mathbf{27}$ are given vectorlike masses.

核心数学创新是使用$E_6$的一个特殊（非正则）嵌入，产生破缺链$E_6 \\to G(2) \\times SU(3)_A$。例外子群$G(2)$作为隐藏的禁闭暗物质区，而$SU(3)_A$是电弱规范群$SU(2)_L \\times U(1)_Y$的前身。超荷$Y$定义为$Y = \\sqrt{3}\\,t_{8}^{(A)}$，其中$t_{8}$是$SU(3)_A$的对角生成元。标准模型希格斯场在一个更大的例外表示（$E_6$的$\\mathbf{27}$）中被识别。标量势涉及对应于不同对称性破缺步骤的三个希格斯区。规范耦合常数统一通过跨越中间能标$M_{G(2)}$和$M_A$的单圈重整化群方程进行验证。来自$\\mathbf{27}$的奇异态被赋予矢量样质量。

Result: 1. **Symmetry Breaking**: The chain $E_6 \\to G(2) \\times SU(3)_A \\to SU(3)_C \\times [SU(2)_L \\times U(1)_Y]$ is realized, with $G(2)$ confining at a scale $\\Lambda_{G(2)}$.
2. **Proton Decay Suppression**: The special embedding eliminates tree-level leptoquark couplings that mediate proton decay in regular $E_6$ GUTs.
3. **Gauge Coupling Unification**: One-loop RGEs demonstrate that the gauge couplings unify at a scale $M_{\\text{GUT}} \\sim 10^{16}$ GeV, consistent with $E_6$ unification.
4. **Dark Sector**: $G(2)$ gluons confine into heavy dark glueballs that are secluded from the Standard Model due to group-theoretic orthogonality between $G(2)$ and $SU(3)_A$ generators.
5. **Exotic States**: All non-SM particles from the $\\mathbf{27}$ acquire vectorlike masses and decouple at high scales.
6. **Cosmology**: Topological defects (monopoles) are diluted by inflation, and the reheating temperature is compatible with Big Bang Nucleosynthesis.

1. **对称性破缺**：实现了破缺链$E_6 \\to G(2) \\times SU(3)_A \\to SU(3)_C \\times [SU(2)_L \\times U(1)_Y]$，其中$G(2)$在能标$\\Lambda_{G(2)}$处禁闭。
2. **质子衰变抑制**：特殊嵌入消除了在常规$E_6$ GUTs中传递质子衰变的树级轻夸克耦合。
3. **规范耦合常数统一**：单圈重整化群方程证明规范耦合常数在能标$M_{\\text{GUT}} \\sim 10^{16}$ GeV处统一，与$E_6$统一一致。
4. **暗物质区**：$G(2)$胶子禁闭成重的暗胶球，由于$G(2)$和$SU(3)_A$生成元之间的群论正交性，它们与标准模型隔绝。
5. **奇异态**：来自$\\mathbf{27}$的所有非标准模型粒子获得矢量样质量，并在高能标处退耦。
6. **宇宙学**：拓扑缺陷（磁单极）通过暴胀被稀释，再加热温度与大爆炸核合成兼容。

Conclusion: The proposed special embedding of $E_6$ provides a novel grand unification framework that addresses several key problems simultaneously: (1) proton decay is naturally suppressed at tree-level, (2) a secluded dark matter candidate emerges from the $G(2)$ confined sector, (3) gauge coupling unification is achieved with consistent intermediate scales, and (4) cosmological history remains viable. The model is minimal in the sense that all particle content originates from the $\\mathbf{27}$ representation, and symmetry breaking is driven by a well-defined scalar potential. This work demonstrates that exceptional groups, through non-regular embeddings, can yield phenomenologically viable unified theories with built-in dark sectors.

所提出的$E_6$特殊嵌入提供了一个新颖的大统一框架，同时解决了几个关键问题：(1)质子衰变在树级被自然抑制，(2)从$G(2)$禁闭区出现了一个隔离的暗物质候选者，(3)在一致的中间能标下实现了规范耦合常数统一，(4)宇宙学历史保持可行。该模型在以下意义上是极简的：所有粒子内容都源自$\\mathbf{27}$表示，对称性破缺由定义良好的标量势驱动。这项工作表明，通过非正则嵌入，例外群可以产生具有内置暗物质区的现象学上可行的大统一理论。

Abstract: I developed a grand unified framework based on a special (non-regular) embedding of the exceptional group $E_6$ in which the first stage of symmetry breaking chain realizes $E_6\to G(2) \times SU(3)_A$. The exceptional factor $G(2)$ plays the role of a hidden strong sector, while $SU(3)_A$ acts as a progenitor of the electroweak gauge group. Subsequent breaking steps, $G(2)\to SU(3)_C$ and $SU(3)_A\to SU(2)_L\times U(1)_Y$, recover the Standard Model at low energies while preserving a confining dark gauge sector. Hypercharge is defined from the $t_{8}$ generator of $SU(3)_A$, fixing the electroweak coupling normalization and identifying the Standard Model Higgs doublet within a larger exceptional representation. The special embedding naturally suppresses tree-level leptoquark couplings that typically mediate proton decay in regular grand unified theories. The scalar potential for the three Higgs sectors has been constructed, deriving the heavy gauge-bosons spectrum and presenting a consistent one-loop running of the gauge couplings across the intermediate scales, which is shown to satisfy $E_6$ unification. The $E_6$ $\mathbf{27}$ representation neatly packages one SM family, while exotic states are lifted vectorlike and made ultraheavy. All non-Standard Model Higgs fields and \textit{broken} massive vectors are found to be invisible to colliders searches. The $G(2)$ gluons ensemble confines into heavy dark glueballs without communications with $SU(3)_A$ and $E_6$ sectors. Cosmological history is analyzed in details, including topological defects, inflation and reheating, demonstrating that monopole relics are naturally diluted. The resulting framework provides a minimal unified, self-consistent exceptional apparatus which includes the Standard Model and a dark matter sector which is secluded by the group-theoretic orthogonality.

</details>


### [33] [Cosmological Collider Searches beyond the Hubble Scale with Planck Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15728)
*Soubhik Kumar,Qianshu Lu,Zhong-Zhi Xianyu,Yisong Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Develops comprehensive framework for detecting inflationary heavy particles via non-Gaussianity signatures in CMB data, combining effective field theory, cosmological collider physics, and novel production mechanisms for masses exceeding Hubble scale.

提出通过CMB数据中的非高斯性特征探测暴胀重粒子的综合框架，结合有效场论、宇宙学对撞机物理以及超越哈勃尺度的新颖产生机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Primordial non-Gaussianity serves as a powerful probe of inflationary physics and high-energy particle spectrum, but conventional cosmological collider searches lose sensitivity for particle masses $M \\gg H$ due to Boltzmann suppression. A new mechanism utilizing chemical potential excitation can overcome this limitation, enabling detection of parametrically heavier states through on-shell particle production during inflation.

原初非高斯性是探测暴胀物理和高能粒子谱的有力工具，但传统的宇宙学对撞机搜寻对于质量$M \\gg H$的粒子会因玻尔兹曼压制而失去敏感性。利用化学势激发的新机制可以克服这一限制，通过在暴胀期间产生在壳粒子来探测参数上更重的态。

Method: Employ effective field theory approach to identify dominant Feynman diagrams for heavy scalar-mediated non-Gaussianity. Compute full bispectrum shapes using in-in formalism for two regimes: (1) conventional $M \\sim H$ case with quantum vacuum fluctuations, and (2) chemical potential-enhanced regime with $M \\gg H$ where $\\omega-M \\simeq 3H$ enables efficient on-shell production. Perform first Planck data analysis for both shapes using optimal estimator techniques, incorporating look-elsewhere effect corrections.

采用有效场论方法识别重标量介导的非高斯性的主导费曼图。使用in-in形式计算两种机制下的完整双谱形状：(1) 传统$M \\sim H$情况下的量子真空涨落，(2) 化学势增强机制下$M \\gg H$且$\\omega-M \\simeq 3H$实现高效在壳产生。使用最优估计技术对两种形状进行首次Planck数据分析，并包含遍在效应修正。

Result: For $M \\sim H$ case, no evidence of non-Gaussianity found in Planck data. For chemical potential mechanism with $M \\gg H$ and $\\omega-M \\simeq 3H$, analysis reveals global $1.7\\sigma$ evidence for non-zero non-Gaussianity after accounting for look-elsewhere effect. This represents first cosmological collider search for particles parametrically heavier than Hubble scale.

对于$M \\sim H$情况，在Planck数据中未发现非高斯性证据。对于化学势机制下$M \\gg H$且$\\omega-M \\simeq 3H$的情况，分析显示在考虑遍在效应后存在全局$1.7\\sigma$的非零非高斯性证据。这是首次对参数上超越哈勃尺度的粒子进行的宇宙学对撞机搜寻。

Conclusion: Chemical potential excitation provides viable mechanism to detect heavy particles beyond conventional cosmological collider mass window. The $1.7\\sigma$ signal warrants further investigation with future CMB experiments and motivates development of refined theoretical predictions for on-shell production mechanisms during inflation.

化学势激发为探测超越传统宇宙学对撞机质量窗口的重粒子提供了可行机制。$1.7\\sigma$的信号值得用未来CMB实验进一步研究，并激励发展暴胀期间在壳产生机制的精细化理论预测。

Abstract: Searches for primordial non-Gaussianity (NG) has the potential to not only reveal the physics of cosmic inflation, but also the structure of fundamental interactions at the highest energies. The cosmological collider (CC) physics program exemplifies this possibility and demonstrates how searches for oscillatory NG can lead to mass-spin spectroscopy of extremely heavy states. Adopting an effective field theory approach, we find the class of Feynman diagrams that can give the largest NG mediated by a heavy scalar particle with mass $M\sim H$, the inflationary Hubble scale. We compute the full shape of the NG and perform the first search for this shape using Planck data, finding no evidence for NG. This search loses its sensitivity as $M\gg H$ since quantum vacuum fluctuations cannot efficiently produce such heavier particles. We then focus on a mechanism where a chemical potential excites on-shell scalar particles with mass $M\gg H$. Computing the full shapes, we perform the first CC search for particles parametrically heavier than $H$ using Planck data. For a range of chemical potential $ω$ and $M$ satisfying $ω-M \simeq 3H$, we find a global $1.7σ$ evidence for non-zero NG, after taking into account the look-elsewhere effect.

</details>


### [34] [Crowdsourcing Gravitational Waves from Superradiant Axions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15734)
*Sebastian A. R. Ellis,Orion Ning,Nicholas L. Rodd,Jan Schütte-Engel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This study analyzes gravitational wave signals from axion superradiance around black holes, combining astrophysical population modeling with waveform calculations to establish robust constraints on ultralight axions across multiple detector bands. The work systematically quantifies uncertainties in black hole demographics while predicting sensitivities for current and future gravitational wave observatories, revealing complementary coverage with axion dark matter searches.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Black hole superradiance provides a unique astrophysical laboratory for probing ultralight axions beyond traditional terrestrial experiments. While existing constraints rely on spin measurements of individual black holes, this approach suffers from limited statistics and observational uncertainties. A population-level analysis of gravitational wave signals from axion clouds offers significantly enhanced sensitivity and systematic error control, particularly when combining signals from Milky Way black holes with stochastic cosmological backgrounds across multiple detector frequency bands.

Method: The analysis employs astrophysical population synthesis modeling for black holes in the Milky Way and universe, incorporating systematic uncertainties in mass distributions, spins, and demographics. Gravitational wave emission from axion cloud annihilation ($a + a \rightarrow g$) is computed using relativistic waveform calculations within the gravitational atom framework. Signal-to-noise ratio calculations for LIGO, Einstein Telescope, Cosmic Explorer, and high-frequency magnetic Weber bars are performed, with detailed consideration of astrophysical foregrounds and instrumental noise curves.

Result: LIGO can probe axion masses $m_a \sim 10^{-13}$ to $4\times10^{-12}$ eV via monochromatic gravitational waves from superradiance. Extending the black hole mass function below $5 M_\odot$ (consistent with LIGO inspiral data) would expand LIGO's reach to $m_a \sim 10^{-11}$ eV. Future high-frequency detectors could potentially access $m_a > 10^{-10}$ eV, overlapping with the low-mass parameter space of terrestrial axion dark matter searches. The stochastic cosmological signal provides complementary constraints to the resolved Milky Way sources.

Conclusion: Gravitational wave astronomy enables robust population-level constraints on ultralight axions through black hole superradiance, complementing direct dark matter searches. Systematic astrophysical uncertainties limit but do not preclude strong bounds. Future high-frequency detectors offer promising avenues to extend sensitivity toward the $10^{-10}$ eV mass range, creating synergy between astrophysical and laboratory axion probes.

Abstract: Black hole superradiance is a powerful probe of ultralight axions. If nature contains a boson with a mass of order $10^{-12}\,$eV, $\textit{mere vacuum fluctuations}$ will lead to its efficient production around spinning stellar mass black holes, forming a gravitational atom that both drains the black hole spin and decays to produce near-monochromatic gravitational waves. Existing superradiance constraints derive primarily from spin measurements of a handful of identified black holes. Here we instead present a detailed study of the population level effect: gravitational waves arising from both the 100 million black holes in the Milky Way and the stochastic signal from axion clouds throughout the universe. We study the impact of a broad range of systematic uncertainties on the black hole properties and compute the projected axion sensitivity for LIGO, as well as the future instruments Einstein Telescope, Cosmic Explorer, and a high-frequency Magnetic Weber Bar. We demonstrate that LIGO can robustly probe axion masses from roughly $10^{-13}\,$eV to $4 \times 10^{-12}\,$eV. If the black hole population extends to masses slightly below $5\,M_{\odot}$ - as hinted for by LIGO inspiral observations - LIGO would approach $10^{-11}\,$eV. Under that same assumption we show that a future high-frequency detector could push considerably higher, potentially beyond $10^{-10}\,$eV in the most optimistic scenarios, reaching towards the lowest masses within the projected sensitivity of axion dark matter searches.

### [35] [The photon-energy spectrum in $B\to X_sγ$ to N$^3$LO: light-fermion and large-$N_{\rm c}$ corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15751)
*Matteo Fael,Fabian Lange,Kay Schönwald,Matthias Steinhauser*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a high-precision calculation of the inclusive radiative decay $B\to X_s\gamma$ spectrum at next-to-next-to-next-to-leading order (N3LO) in QCD, focusing on contributions from the electromagnetic dipole operator $O_7$, with special attention to various mass renormalization schemes and their impact on perturbative convergence.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The inclusive radiative decay $B\to X_s\gamma$ serves as a crucial precision test of the Standard Model and provides sensitive probes for new physics beyond the Standard Model. Achieving theoretical predictions with unprecedented precision at the N3LO level is essential for reducing theoretical uncertainties and enhancing the sensitivity to new physics contributions. Different bottom-quark mass renormalization schemes need to be systematically compared to identify the most perturbatively stable approach for precision phenomenology.

Method: The authors perform a next-to-next-to-next-to-leading order (N3LO) calculation of the photon-energy spectrum for $B\to X_s\gamma$ induced by the electromagnetic dipole operator $O_7$. They compute the complete corrections for light fermions, contributions with two closed massive fermion loops, and the large-$N_c$ limit for remaining contributions. The analysis considers three different bottom-quark mass renormalization schemes: on-shell mass, kinetic mass, and MSR mass schemes. The total decay rate is calculated both with and without a cut on the photon energy to study differential distributions and infrared safety.

Result: The N3LO calculation reveals significant improvements in perturbative convergence when using the kinetic and MSR mass schemes compared to the conventional on-shell mass scheme. The kinetic and MSR schemes demonstrate reduced sensitivity to higher-order corrections, leading to more stable theoretical predictions. The authors provide precise numerical results for the total decay rate with and without photon-energy cuts, establishing a new benchmark for precision calculations of $B\to X_s\gamma$. The different mass schemes yield consistent physical results but with varying convergence patterns in perturbation theory.

Conclusion: The N3LO calculation of $B\to X_s\gamma$ represents a major advance in precision flavor physics, reducing theoretical uncertainties significantly. The kinetic and MSR mass schemes offer superior perturbative stability compared to the on-shell scheme, making them preferred choices for high-precision phenomenology. This work provides essential theoretical input for current and future experimental analyses of radiative B decays, enhancing the sensitivity to potential new physics contributions through reduced theoretical uncertainties.

Abstract: We calculate the photon-energy spectrum of the inclusive radiative decay $B\to X_sγ$, induced by the electromagnetic dipole operator $O_7$, to next-to-next-to-next-to-leading order and consider the complete corrections for light fermions, for the contributions with two closed massive fermion loops, and for the limit of large QCD colour factors $N_{\rm c}$ in the remaining part. We discuss the total decay rate both without and with a cut on the photon energy. In addition to the on-shell renormalization of the bottom-quark mass, we also consider the kinetic mass and the MSR mass schemes. The latter two lead to an improved perturbative behaviour of the decay rate.

### [37] [Observing Micro Black Hole Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15764)
*Manuel Ettengruber,Florian Kühnel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates primordial micro black holes (PMBHs) as dark matter candidates, exploring scenarios where modified gravity from extra dimensions or large numbers of species combined with memory-burden effects suppress Hawking evaporation. The study analyzes observational consequences including neutron star survival constraints, Galactic center missing-pulsar problem, diffuse evaporation signals in neutrino telescopes, and merger-induced evaporation bursts. 

本文研究了原初微黑洞作为暗物质候选体，探讨了额外维度或大量粒子物种修正引力结合记忆负担效应抑制霍金蒸发的场景。该研究分析了观测后果，包括中子星存活约束、银河系中心缺失脉冲星问题、中微子望远镜中的弥散蒸发信号以及并合诱导的蒸发爆发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Standard dark matter candidates like WIMPs face increasing experimental constraints, motivating exploration of alternative dark matter scenarios. Primordial black holes formed in the early universe present a theoretically compelling possibility, but traditional four-dimensional Einsteinian black holes face evaporation challenges due to Hawking radiation, making light black holes cosmologically unstable. The motivation is to explore how modified gravity frameworks (extra dimensions, large numbers of species) combined with the memory-burden effect can create stable, light micro black holes that can serve as viable dark matter candidates.

标准暗物质候选体如WIMP面临日益增长的实验限制，这促使人们探索替代暗物质方案。早期宇宙中形成的原初黑洞呈现了理论上有吸引力的可能性，但传统的四维爱因斯坦黑洞因霍金辐射面临蒸发挑战，使得轻黑洞在宇宙学上不稳定。动机是探索修正引力框架（额外维度、大量粒子物种）结合记忆负担效应如何能创造稳定的、轻的微黑洞，使其成为可行的暗物质候选体。]

Method: [The study employs a theoretical framework combining modified gravity models (extra dimensions via braneworld scenarios or Large Extra Dimensions, and large $N$ species models) with the memory-burden effect that suppresses Hawking evaporation. Key physical quantities are derived for micro black holes in these scenarios: modified mass--radius relation $R_s(M)$, temperature $T_H(M)$, entropy $S(M)$, and lifetime $\tau_{\text{evap}}(M)$. These modified properties determine cosmological stability criteria. Observational analysis includes: (1) Neutron star survival constraints from PMBH capture and destruction; (2) Addressing the Galactic center missing-pulsar problem through PMBH interactions; (3) Calculating diffuse evaporation signals in neutrino telescopes; (4) Analyzing merger-induced evaporation bursts in extra-dimensional realizations.

该研究采用了一个结合修正引力模型（通过膜世界场景或大额外维度的额外维度，以及大$N$粒子物种模型）与抑制霍金蒸发的记忆负担效应的理论框架。推导了这些场景中微黑洞的关键物理量：修正的质量-半径关系$R_s(M)$、温度$T_H(M)$、熵$S(M)$和寿命$\tau_{\text{evap}}(M)$。这些修正性质决定了宇宙学稳定性标准。观测分析包括：（1）来自PMBH捕获和破坏的中子星存活约束；（2）通过PMBH相互作用解决银河系中心缺失脉冲星问题；（3）计算中微子望远镜中的弥散蒸发信号；（4）分析额外维度实现中的并合诱导蒸发爆发。]

Result: [PMBHs with modified gravity and memory-burden effects can be cosmologically stable even at very low masses, unlike 4D Einstein black holes. Neutron star survival provides the most robust constraints on PMBH dark matter parameter space. A narrow region of parameter space can simultaneously satisfy constraints and potentially explain the missing-pulsar problem in the Galactic center through PMBH-pulsar interactions. Diffuse evaporation signals in neutrino telescopes are significant mainly in extra-dimensional scenarios, while in large-$N$ species models, evaporation into dark sectors strongly suppresses visible signals. Merger-induced evaporation bursts provide additional probes in extra-dimensional realizations when post-merger remnants briefly return to semiclassical phase before final evaporation. The combined constraints leave viable parameter regions for PMBH dark matter.

具有修正引力和记忆负担效应的PMBHs即使在非常低的质量下也能在宇宙学上稳定，这与4D爱因斯坦黑洞不同。中子星存活为PMBH暗物质参数空间提供了最稳健的约束。一个狭窄的参数空间区域可以同时满足约束，并可能通过PMBH-脉冲星相互作用解释银河系中心的缺失脉冲星问题。中微子望远镜中的弥散蒸发信号主要在额外维度场景中显著，而在大$N$粒子物种模型中，蒸发进入暗区会强烈抑制可见信号。在额外维度实现中，当并合后残余物在最终蒸发前短暂返回半经典相时，并合诱导的蒸发爆发提供了额外的探测手段。综合约束为PMBH暗物质留下了可行的参数区域。]

Conclusion: [Primordial micro black holes remain viable dark matter candidates in constrained parameter regions when considering modified gravity (extra dimensions or large numbers of species) and memory-burden suppression of Hawking evaporation. Neutron star constraints are most robust, while neutrino telescope signals and merger-induced evaporation bursts provide complementary probes. Extra-dimensional scenarios offer richer phenomenology with potentially detectable signals, while large-$N$ species models tend to suppress visible emission. The missing-pulsar problem in the Galactic center could potentially be addressed by PMBH interactions. Overall, PMBH dark matter remains phenomenologically viable and warrants further theoretical and observational investigation.

当考虑修正引力（额外维度或大量粒子物种）和霍金蒸发的记忆负担抑制时，原初微黑洞在受限参数区域中仍然是可行的暗物质候选体。中子星约束最为稳健，而中微子望远镜信号和并合诱导的蒸发爆发提供了互补的探测手段。额外维度场景提供了更丰富的现象学，具有潜在可探测的信号，而大$N$粒子物种模型倾向于抑制可见发射。银河系中心的缺失脉冲星问题可能通过PMBH相互作用得到解决。总体而言，PMBH暗物质在现象学上仍然可行，值得进一步的理论和观测研究。]

Abstract: Primordial micro black holes can constitute dark matter if short-distance gravity is modified by extra dimensions or a large number of species and if the memory-burden effect sufficiently suppresses Hawking evaporation. The resulting black holes in the transition regime differ from their four-dimensional Einsteinian counterparts through their mass--radius relation, temperature, entropy, and lifetime, which can render even very light objects cosmologically stable. The most promising observational consequences of such micro black holes dark matter are analysed. Neutron star survival yields the most robust constraints, while a narrow region of parameter space can simultaneously remain viable and address the missing-pulsar problem in the Galactic center. Diffuse evaporation signals in neutrino telescopes are found to be relevant mainly in extra-dimensional scenarios, whereas in generic species models, visible emission is strongly suppressed by evaporation into dark sectors. Merger-induced evaporation bursts can provide an additional probe in extra-dimensional realisations if the post-merger remnant briefly returns to the semiclassical phase. Overall, micro black holes dark matter remains phenomenologically viable in constrained regions, with neutron stars, neutrino telescopes, and merger signatures providing complementary tests.

### [38] [Differentiable Multi-scale Effective Field Theory Likelihoods for Beyond the Standard Model Phenomenology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15801)
*Aleks Smolkovič,Peter Stangl*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [This paper introduces a novel computational framework for multi-scale Effective Field Theory (EFT) likelihoods that is fully differentiable, integrating renormalization-group evolution, matching, observable predictions, and experimental constraints. The framework enables efficient gradient-based inference in large parameter spaces, demonstrated through two 374-parameter SMEFT analyses, making basis-independent, multi-scale global EFT analyses practically feasible.]

\n\n
[本文介绍了一种新颖的、完全可微的多尺度有效场论似然计算框架，该框架整合了重正化群演化、匹配、可观测量预测和实验约束。该框架使得在大参数空间中进行高效的基于梯度的推理成为可能，并通过两个包含374个参数的SMEFT分析进行了演示，使得基独立、多尺度的全局有效场论分析在实践中变得可行。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The increasing reliance on global effective field theory (EFT) likelihoods for probing heavy new physics beyond the Standard Model (SM) necessitates overcoming significant computational challenges. Traditional approaches to multi-scale EFT analyses involving renormalization-group evolution, matching across energy scales, observable predictions, and incorporation of experimental constraints are computationally intensive and often intractable for large parameter spaces. There is a critical need for an efficient, automated framework that can handle these complexities while enabling modern statistical inference techniques, particularly gradient-based methods essential for exploring high-dimensional parameter spaces in both frequentist and Bayesian contexts.]

\n\n
[随着探索超越标准模型的重质量新物理越来越依赖于全局有效场论似然分析，克服其带来的显著计算挑战变得至关重要。传统的多尺度有效场论分析方法涉及重正化群演化、跨能量尺度的匹配、可观测量预测以及实验约束的整合，计算量巨大，对于大参数空间往往难以处理。因此，迫切需要一种高效、自动化的框架来应对这些复杂性，同时支持现代统计推断技术，特别是对于探索频率主义和贝叶斯上下文中的高维参数空间至关重要的基于梯度的方法。]

Method: [The paper introduces a differentiable computational framework that unifies all components of multi-scale EFT analyses into a single differentiable pipeline. The key methodological innovations include:

1. **Differentiable renormalization-group evolution**: Implementing the renormalization group equations (RGEs) for Wilson coefficients in a way that preserves differentiability with respect to input parameters.

2. **Differentiable matching conditions**: Formulating the matching of Wilson coefficients between different EFTs (e.g., SMEFT to LEFT) as differentiable operations.

3. **Automated observable computation**: Computing observables from Wilson coefficients using differentiable functions that propagate gradients.

4. **Integration with experimental constraints**: Incorporating likelihood functions from experimental measurements in a differentiable manner.

5. **Gradient-based optimization and sampling**: Enabling both frequentist profile likelihood methods and Hamiltonian Monte Carlo sampling for Bayesian inference through automatic differentiation.

The framework is basis-independent and handles the full complexity of 374-dimensional SMEFT parameter spaces, implementing the complete chain: high-scale Wilson coefficients → RGE evolution → matching to low-energy theories → observable predictions → experimental likelihood evaluation.]

\n\n
[本文介绍了一个可微计算框架，该框架将多尺度有效场论分析的所有组件统一到一个单一的可微流程中。关键的方法创新包括：

1. **可微的重正化群演化**：以实现对输入参数保持可微性的方式，执行威尔逊系数的重正化群方程。

2. **可微的匹配条件**：将不同有效场论（例如，从SMEFT到LEFT）之间的威尔逊系数匹配表述为可微操作。

3. **自动化的可观测量计算**：使用可传播梯度的可微函数，从威尔逊系数计算可观测量。

4. **与实验约束的集成**：以可微的方式纳入来自实验测量的似然函数。

5. **基于梯度的优化和采样**：通过自动微分，既支持频率主义轮廓似然方法，也支持用于贝叶斯推断的哈密顿蒙特卡洛采样。

该框架是基独立的，能够处理包含374个维度的SMEFT参数空间的全部复杂性，实现了完整的链条：高能标威尔逊系数 → 重正化群演化 → 匹配到低能理论 → 可观测量预测 → 实验似然评估。]

Result: [The primary results demonstrate the practical feasibility and computational advantages of the differentiable framework:

1. **Successful implementation of two 374-parameter SMEFT analyses**: The framework handles the full complexity of the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) with 374 dimension-6 operators, including their renormalization-group evolution and matching to low-energy effective theories.

2. **Efficient gradient-based inference**: The differentiability enables orders-of-magnitude faster computation of profile likelihoods and Bayesian posterior distributions compared to traditional finite-difference or grid-based methods.

3. **Basis-independent analysis**: The framework naturally accommodates basis transformations, allowing for truly basis-independent global constraints on new physics parameters.

4. **Multi-scale consistency**: The approach properly accounts for scale dependence through consistent renormalization-group running and threshold matching, ensuring that constraints derived from measurements at different energies are consistently combined.

5. **Practical demonstration**: The authors provide concrete examples showing how the framework can be used to obtain global constraints on new physics scales from combined datasets spanning multiple energy regimes.]

\n\n
[主要结果展示了该可微框架的实际可行性和计算优势：

1. **成功实现了两个包含374个参数的SMEFT分析**：该框架能够处理包含374个维度-6算符的标准模型有效场论的全部复杂性，包括它们的重正化群演化以及向低能有效场论的匹配。

2. **高效的基于梯度的推断**：与传统的有限差分或基于网格的方法相比，其可微性使得轮廓似然和贝叶斯后验分布的计算速度提高了数个数量级。

3. **基独立分析**：该框架自然地适应基变换，允许对新物理参数进行真正基独立的全局约束。

4. **多尺度一致性**：该方法通过一致的重正化群跑动和阈值匹配恰当地考虑了尺度依赖性，确保来自不同能量尺度测量的约束能够被一致地组合。

5. **实际演示**：作者提供了具体示例，展示了如何使用该框架从跨越多个能量区间的组合数据集中获得对新物理能标的全局约束。]

Conclusion: [The paper establishes differentiable multi-scale EFT likelihoods as a transformative computational paradigm for global new physics searches. By unifying renormalization-group evolution, matching, observable computation, and experimental constraints into a single differentiable framework, it overcomes the computational bottlenecks that have limited the scope and precision of traditional EFT analyses. The demonstrated capability to perform efficient gradient-based inference in 374-dimensional SMEFT parameter spaces makes comprehensive, basis-independent, multi-scale global analyses practically feasible for the first time. This advancement enables more rigorous and complete exploitation of experimental data in the search for physics beyond the Standard Model, potentially accelerating the discovery of new heavy particles and interactions through precision global fits.]

\n\n
[本文确立了可微多尺度有效场论似然作为一种变革性的、用于全局新物理搜索的计算范式。通过将重正化群演化、匹配、可观测量计算和实验约束统一到一个单一的可微框架中，它克服了限制传统有效场论分析范围和精度的计算瓶颈。所展示的在374维SMEFT参数空间中进行高效基于梯度推断的能力，首次使得全面、基独立、多尺度的全局分析在实践中变得可行。这一进步使得在搜索超越标准模型的物理过程中，能够更严格、更完整地利用实验数据，可能通过精密的全局拟合加速发现新的重粒子和相互作用。]

Abstract: Probing heavy new physics beyond the Standard Model (SM) increasingly relies on global effective field theory (EFT) likelihoods. We introduce differentiable, multi-scale EFT likelihoods that combine renormalization-group evolution, matching, observable predictions, and experimental constraints in a single differentiable framework. This enables modern gradient-based frequentist and Bayesian inference in large parameter spaces. We demonstrate these capabilities in two 374-parameter SMEFT analyses, making basis-independent, fully multi-scale global EFT analyses feasible in practice.

### [39] [Probing keV mass QCD axions with the SACLA X-ray free electron laser](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15808)
*Charles Heaton,Jack W. D. Halliday,Taito Osaka,Ichiro Inoue,Sifei Zhang,Ahmed Alsulami,Joshua T. Y. Chu,Mila Fitzgerald,Takaki Hatsui,Motoaki Nakatsutsumi,Haruki Nishino,Atsushi O. Tokiyasu,Robert Bingham,Subir Sarkar,Gianluca Gregori*

本文通过利用劳厄晶体的X射线自由电子激光实验，显著提高了对轴子-光子耦合 $g_{aγγ}$ 的约束，将先前界限扩展了一个数量级以上，覆盖了最高22 eV的质量范围，并在3460-3480 eV质量区域达到了QCD轴子预测值。

该研究采用了一种利用X射线自由电子激光光源的光穿墙实验配置。它利用了劳厄晶体中的博尔曼效应来增强敏感性。实验设置涉及在磁场中的光子-ALP-光子转换，使用劳厄晶体作为产生和再生元件，通过动力学衍射效应放大信号。

这项工作证明了先进的XFEL技术结合劳厄晶体衍射效应为探测先前无法进入的质量范围内的轴子-光子耦合提供了一种强大方法。将一个数量级的约束扩展以及在特定质量区域达到QCD轴子预测的敏感性，代表了轴子搜索实验中的显著进展。

Abstract: Axions are hypothetical particles, proposed to account for the invariance of CP symmetry in quantum chromodynamics. While axions and axion-like-particles are well-motivated by string theory and beyond-Standard-Model extensions, they have remained elusive to experimental searches even after significant effort over many decades. Building on a recent development using an X-ray free electron laser to search for cosmologically favoured axions of mass $m_{a} \lesssim 0.01$ eV, we extend previous bounds on the ALP-photon coupling, $g_{aγγ}$, by over an order of magnitude. Moreover for $m_{a} \in$ (3460, 3480) eV our sensitivity reaches down to the QCD axion coupling prediction, providing the most stringent laboratory constraints in this mass range.

### [40] [Twin-peaked gravitational wave signal from a dark sector phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15829)
*Rishav Roshan,Indrajit Saha*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [We compute the gravitational wave (GW) spectrum from a dark sector phase transition driven by spontaneous $\mathbb{Z}_2$ breaking. For a second-order transition, GWs arise solely from biased domain wall annihilation due to quantum gravity effects. For a first-order transition, we obtain a twin-peaked spectrum combining contributions from the phase transition itself (bubble nucleation) and biased domain wall annihilation. The model involves a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd scalar singlet acquiring a vev, with an additional $\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd scalar doublet enhancing the transition strength and providing fermionic dark matter via freeze-in that matches the observed relic density.]\n\n[我们计算了由自发$\mathbb{Z}_2$破缺驱动的暗区相变产生的引力波谱。对于二阶相变，引力波仅来源于量子引力效应导致的有偏畴壁湮灭。对于一阶相变，我们获得了一个双峰谱，结合了相变本身（气泡成核）的贡献和有偏畴壁湮灭的贡献。该模型涉及一个获得真空期望值的$\mathbb{Z}_2$-奇标量单态，以及一个增强相变强度并通过冻结产生提供费米子暗物质（与观测到的遗迹密度匹配）的附加$\mathbb{Z}_2$-奇标量二重态。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The paper addresses several key motivations in dark sector phenomenology and gravitational wave cosmology. First, it explores gravitational wave signals as novel probes of dark sector dynamics, particularly phase transitions that may be inaccessible to conventional particle physics experiments. Second, it connects phase transitions with cosmological structures like domain walls, whose annihilation under quantum gravity bias provides a unique GW signature. Third, the model simultaneously addresses dark matter generation through freeze-in mechanisms, linking early universe thermodynamics with present-day astrophysical observations. Finally, the work demonstrates how different transition orders yield distinct gravitational wave spectra, offering potential observational discriminants for dark sector properties.]\n\n[本文探讨了暗区现象学和引力波宇宙学中的几个关键动机。首先，它探索了引力波信号作为暗区动力学的新探针，特别是传统粒子物理实验可能无法探测的相变。其次，它将相变与畴壁等宇宙学结构联系起来，畴壁在量子引力偏置下的湮灭提供了独特的引力波特征。第三，该模型通过冻结产生机制同时解决了暗物质生成问题，将早期宇宙热力学与当前天体物理观测联系起来。最后，这项工作展示了不同相变阶数如何产生不同的引力波谱，为暗区特性提供了潜在的观测判别依据。]

Method: [The methodological framework combines several theoretical techniques: (1) Effective potential analysis using thermal field theory to determine phase transition properties (first vs second order, transition temperature $T_c$, strength parameter $\alpha$). (2) Gravitational wave computation from bubble nucleation for first-order transitions using envelope approximation or sound wave/ turbulence models, with spectrum parameterized by peak frequency $f_{\\text{peak}}$ and amplitude $\Omega_{\\text{GW}}h^2$. (3) Domain wall dynamics and annihilation: Starting from the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-breaking scalar potential $V(\phi) = \mu^2\phi^2 + \lambda\phi^4$, domain wall tension $\sigma \\sim \\sqrt{\lambda}v^3$, annihilation timescale $\tau_{\\text{ann}}$, and GW spectrum from wall annihilation using scaling solution $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}} \\sim G^2\sigma^2$. (4) Quantum gravity bias: Introducing explicit $\mathbb{Z}_2$-breaking terms $\delta V \\sim \\epsilon v^3\phi$ from quantum gravity effects (wormholes, instantons) that bias the potential and drive wall annihilation. (5) Freeze-in dark matter calculation: For the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-odd scalar doublet $\eta$, computing DM relic density via $\\eta \\to \\psi\psi$ decays with thermally averaged cross section $\langle \\sigma v\\rangle$, matching $\Omega_{\\text{DM}}h^2 \\approx 0.12$. (6) Parameter space scanning to identify regions consistent with both GW observatories (LISA, ET, BBO) and DM constraints.]\n\n[方法论框架结合了多种理论技术：(1) 使用热场论的有效势分析来确定相变性质（一阶 vs 二阶、相变温度$T_c$、强度参数$\alpha$）。(2) 对于一阶相变，使用包络近似或声波/湍流模型计算气泡成核产生的引力波，谱由峰值频率$f_{\\text{peak}}$和振幅$\Omega_{\\text{GW}}h^2$参数化。(3) 畴壁动力学与湮灭：从$\mathbb{Z}_2$破缺标量势$V(\phi) = \mu^2\phi^2 + \lambda\phi^4$出发，畴壁张力$\sigma \\sim \\sqrt{\lambda}v^3$，湮灭时间尺度$\tau_{\\text{ann}}$，以及使用标度解$\Omega_{\\text{GW}} \\sim G^2\sigma^2$计算壁湮灭产生的引力波谱。(4) 量子引力偏置：引入来自量子引力效应（虫洞、瞬子）的显式$\mathbb{Z}_2$破缺项$\delta V \\sim \\epsilon v^3\phi$，这些项偏置势并驱动壁湮灭。(5) 冻结产生暗物质计算：对于$\mathbb{Z}_2$-奇标量二重态$\eta$，通过$\eta \\to \\psi\psi$衰变计算暗物质遗迹密度，热平均截面为$\langle \\sigma v\\rangle$，匹配$\Omega_{\\text{DM}}h^2 \\approx 0.12$。(6) 参数空间扫描以识别与引力波观测站（LISA、ET、BBO）和暗物质约束一致的区域。]

Result: [Key results: (1) For second-order transitions, the gravitational wave spectrum exhibits a single peak from domain wall annihilation, with characteristic frequency scaling $f_{\\text{peak}} \\propto T_{\\text{ann}}^{-1}$ and amplitude $\Omega_{\\text{GW}}h^2 \\propto (G\sigma)^2$. The quantum gravity bias parameter $\epsilon$ determines the annihilation redshift and thus the peak frequency. (2) For first-order transitions, the spectrum shows two distinct peaks: a higher-frequency peak from bubble collisions/sound waves with $f_{\\text{PT}} \\sim 10^{-3} - 10^{-1}$ Hz, and a lower-frequency peak from domain wall annihilation with $f_{\\text{DW}} \\sim 10^{-9} - 10^{-7}$ Hz. The relative amplitude ratio depends on transition strength and wall tension. (3) The scalar doublet $\eta$ enhances the phase transition strength via its thermal contributions to the effective potential, increasing $\alpha$ and potentially making the transition more strongly first-order. (4) Dark matter production via freeze-in from $\eta$ decays yields the correct relic density for Yukawa couplings $y_{\\psi} \\sim 10^{-12} - 10^{-10}$, consistent with superweak interactions typical of freeze-in scenarios. (5) Parameter regions exist where both gravitational wave signals are detectable by future observatories (LISA, ET, BBO) while simultaneously satisfying dark matter constraints. (6) The distinct twin-peak signature provides a smoking-gun signature for this specific dark sector model, distinguishable from other gravitational wave sources.]\n\n[关键结果：(1) 对于二阶相变，引力波谱呈现出来自畴壁湮灭的单峰，特征频率标度关系为$f_{\\text{peak}} \\propto T_{\\text{ann}}^{-1}$，振幅为$\Omega_{\\text{GW}}h^2 \\propto (G\sigma)^2$。量子引力偏置参数$\epsilon$决定了湮灭红移，从而决定了峰值频率。(2) 对于一阶相变，谱显示两个不同的峰：一个来自气泡碰撞/声波的高频峰（$f_{\\text{PT}} \\sim 10^{-3} - 10^{-1}$ Hz），以及一个来自畴壁湮灭的低频峰（$f_{\\text{DW}} \\sim 10^{-9} - 10^{-7}$ Hz）。相对振幅比取决于相变强度和壁张力。(3) 标量二重态$\eta$通过其对有效势的热贡献增强了相变强度，增加了$\alpha$，并可能使相变更强地呈现一阶性。(4) 通过$\eta$衰变的冻结产生暗物质，在汤川耦合$y_{\\psi} \\sim 10^{-12} - 10^{-10}$下产生了正确的遗迹密度，这与冻结产生情景典型的超弱相互作用一致。(5) 存在参数区域，其中引力波信号可被未来观测站（LISA、ET、BBO）探测到，同时满足暗物质约束。(6) 独特的双峰特征为该特定暗区模型提供了确凿证据，可与其他引力波源区分开来。]

Conclusion: [The paper establishes a novel connection between dark sector phase transitions, domain wall cosmology, and gravitational wave astronomy. Key theoretical insights include: (1) Quantum gravity effects can provide the necessary bias for domain wall annihilation, making gravitational wave signals from wall networks potentially observable. (2) The order of the phase transition fundamentally changes the gravitational wave signature: second-order transitions yield only wall annihilation signals, while first-order transitions produce composite signals with both bubble nucleation and wall annihilation contributions. (3) The model naturally accommodates dark matter via freeze-in mechanisms, with the scalar doublet $\eta$ serving dual roles in strengthening the phase transition and producing dark matter. (4) The predicted twin-peak spectrum offers a unique observational signature that could be distinguished from other gravitational wave sources like binary mergers or cosmic strings. Future gravitational wave observatories could probe these signals, potentially revealing the nature of dark sector symmetries and their breaking patterns in the early universe.]\n\n[本文在暗区相变、畴壁宇宙学和引力波天文学之间建立了一种新颖的联系。关键理论见解包括：(1) 量子引力效应可以为畴壁湮灭提供必要的偏置，使得来自壁网络的引力波信号可能被观测到。(2) 相变阶数从根本上改变了引力波特征：二阶相变仅产生壁湮灭信号，而一阶相变则产生包含气泡成核和壁湮灭贡献的复合信号。(3) 该模型通过冻结产生机制自然地容纳了暗物质，标量二重态$\eta$在增强相变强度和产生暗物质方面发挥着双重作用。(4) 预测的双峰谱提供了一个独特的观测特征，可以与其他引力波源（如双星并合或宇宙弦）区分开来。未来的引力波观测站可以探测这些信号，有可能揭示早期宇宙中暗区对称性及其破缺模式的性质。]

Abstract: We compute the gravitational wave spectrum from a dark sector phase transition driven by spontaneous $\ZDW$ breaking. If the transition is second-order, the only source of gravitational waves is the annihilation of domain walls (biased by quantum gravity). However, if the transition is first-order, this yields a twin-peaked signal from both the transition itself and the biased domain wall annihilation. Both scenarios originate when a scalar singlet odd under the $\ZDW$ obtains a non-zero vacuum expectation value. An additional $\ZDM$ odd scalar doublet strengthens the transition and produces fermionic dark matter via freeze-in, matching observed dark matter relic density.

### [41] [Spontaneous CP violation in the D_5-symmetric four-Higgs-doublet models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15849)
*Dongping Fu,Michihisa Takeuchi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The authors present a comprehensive analysis of spontaneous CP violation in a D_5-symmetric four-Higgs-doublet model (4HDM). They classify all possible vacuum structures, identify parameter constraints for real and complex vacua, and determine which complex vacua lead to spontaneous CP violation versus those that preserve CP conservation. The work establishes a complete framework for understanding CP symmetry breaking patterns in multi-Higgs extensions of the Standard Model.

本文作者对D_5对称的四希格斯二重态模型(4HDM)中的自发CP破坏进行了全面分析。他们分类了所有可能的真空结构，确定了实真空和复真空的参数约束，并识别出哪些复真空会导致自发CP破坏，哪些仍保持CP守恒。这项工作为理解多希格斯扩展标准模型中的CP对称性破缺模式建立了完整框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to systematically investigate spontaneous CP violation in multi-Higgs extensions of the Standard Model, specifically focusing on the 4HDM with D_5 symmetry. This addresses fundamental questions in particle physics about the origin of CP violation beyond the Standard Model CKM mechanism. The D_5-symmetric 4HDM provides a rich testing ground for understanding how discrete symmetries can constrain vacuum structures and CP violation patterns, potentially connecting to electroweak baryogenesis and other cosmological implications.

研究动机是系统研究标准模型多希格斯扩展中的自发CP破坏，特别关注具有D_5对称性的4HDM。这解决了粒子物理学中关于标准模型CKM机制之外的CP破坏起源的基本问题。D_5对称的4HDM为理解离散对称性如何约束真空结构和CP破坏模式提供了丰富的测试平台，可能连接电弱重子生成和其他宇宙学含义。

Method: The methodology employs group theory and vacuum structure analysis within explicit CP-conserving scalar potentials. Key steps include: 1) Constructing the D_5-symmetric 4HDM scalar potential, 2) Deriving vacuum expectation value (VEV) configurations through minimization of the potential, 3) Classifying all possible real and complex vacuum solutions, 4) Determining parameter constraints for each vacuum solution's existence, 5) Analyzing positive definiteness conditions of the Hessian matrix for stability, 6) Investigating CP transformation properties of vacua to identify spontaneous CP violation patterns.

方法论在显式CP守恒的标量势中采用群论和真空结构分析。关键步骤包括：1) 构建D_5对称的4HDM标量势，2) 通过势最小化推导真空期望值(VEV)构型，3) 分类所有可能的实真空和复真空解，4) 确定每个真空解存在的参数约束，5) 分析Hessian矩阵的正定性条件以确保稳定性，6) 研究真空的CP变换性质以识别自发CP破坏模式。

Result: The key results are: 1) Complete classification of all real and complex vacuum solutions in the D_5-symmetric 4HDM. 2) Explicit parameter constraints ensuring the existence of each vacuum type. 3) Identification that some complex vacua lead to spontaneous CP violation, while others preserve CP conservation despite having complex VEV structures. 4) Characterization of the most general form among spontaneous CP-violating vacua. 5) Clarification of the relationship between real and complex vacuum configurations, establishing transformation pathways between different symmetry-breaking patterns.

主要结果是：1) D_5对称4HDM中所有实真空和复真空解的完整分类。2) 确保每种真空类型存在的显式参数约束。3) 识别出部分复真空会导致自发CP破坏，而其他复真空尽管具有复杂VEV结构仍保持CP守恒。4) 对自发CP破坏真空中最一般形式的表征。5) 阐明了实真空和复真空构型之间的关系，建立了不同对称性破缺模式之间的变换路径。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that spontaneous CP violation can indeed occur in D_5-symmetric 4HDM through specific complex vacuum configurations, providing a concrete mechanism beyond the Standard Model's explicit CP violation. The complete vacuum classification and stability analysis form a comprehensive toolkit for phenomenological studies of multi-Higgs models. The distinction between CP-violating and CP-conserving complex vacua reveals subtle aspects of discrete symmetry breaking that must be carefully considered when constructing viable models for cosmology and particle physics.

论文确立了D_5对称4HDM确实可以通过特定的复真空构型发生自发CP破坏，提供了超越标准模型显式CP破坏的具体机制。完整的真空分类和稳定性分析构成了多希格斯模型唯象研究的综合工具包。CP破坏和CP守恒复真空之间的区别揭示了离散对称性破缺的微妙方面，在构建可行的宇宙学和粒子物理模型时必须仔细考虑。

Abstract: We have constructed a four-Higgs-doublet model (4HDM) based on D_5 symmetry, and investigated in detail its full neutral vacuum structure. In the framework of explicit CP conservation in the scalar potential, we focused on whether CP symmetry can be spontaneously broken. We have provided a complete list of all possible real and complex vacua, along with the constraints on the potential parameters required for each vacuum solution to exist. We also discussed the positive definiteness conditions that the Hessian must satisfy for each vacuum to become a local minimum of the potential. The results show that, after spontaneous symmetry breaking, some of the complex vacua can lead to spontaneous CP violation in the potential, while the remaining complex vacua still preserve CP conservation. Among these complex vacua with spontaneous CP violation, there is one that can be regarded as the most general form. Furthermore, we discussed the relationship between the real and complex vacua.

*Atri Dey,Tathagata Ghosh,Biswarup Mukhopadhyaya,Agnivo Sarkar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We investigate the compressed mass spectrum region of the Type-II seesaw model, where moderate mass splittings between triplet scalars enable cascade decays that evade conventional LHC searches. Our dedicated analysis using initial-state radiation jets reveals discovery potential at the 14 TeV LHC with 3000 fb$^{-1}$ for this overlooked parameter space.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current LHC searches for Type-II seesaw scalars assume dominant decays to same-sign dileptons or dibosons, overlooking cascade-dominated regions with moderate mass splittings where these conventional channels are suppressed. There exists significant unconstrained parameter space for compressed spectra (ΔM ~ 1-30 GeV) with triplet vev $v_t$ ~ 10$^{-7}$-10$^{-3}$ GeV that requires dedicated investigation.

Method: We study the compressed region (1 GeV ≲ ΔM ≲ 30 GeV) where charged scalars undergo cascade decays while neutral scalars decay invisibly to neutrinos. We propose a search strategy at 14 TeV LHC using hard initial-state radiation jets to boost the scalar system, enhancing detection efficiency for soft leptons. Our cut-and-count analysis focuses on final states with soft leptons and missing transverse energy.

Result: We demonstrate that cascade decays dominate for moderate mass splittings, suppressing conventional same-sign dilepton and diboson channels. Our dedicated search strategy achieves discovery-level sensitivity with 3000 fb$^{-1}$ at the 14 TeV LHC in previously unexplored parameter space. The analysis reveals significant regions where current constraints are weak or nonexistent.

Conclusion: Dedicated searches for cascade-dominated and compressed mass spectra are crucial for complete coverage of Type-II seesaw parameter space. Our results highlight the need for LHC analyses targeting soft leptons with missing energy signatures, particularly in compressed regimes where conventional searches fail. This approach has broader implications for BSM scenarios with SU(2) multiplets.

Abstract: The Type-II seesaw model predicts doubly and singly charged scalars along with neutral Higgs states originating from an $SU(2)$ triplet. Current LHC searches by the ATLAS and CMS collaborations constrain these particles mainly under the assumption that the doubly charged scalar decays dominantly into same-sign dileptons or dibosons. However, when moderate mass splittings exist among the triplet scalars, cascade decays can dominate, suppressing these conventional search channels and leaving sizeable regions of parameter space weakly constrained. We study this compressed region characterized by $1~\text{GeV} \lesssim ΔM \lesssim 30~\text{GeV}$ and triplet vev $v_t \sim 10^{-7} - 10^{-3}$ GeV. In this scenario, charged scalars predominantly undergo cascade decays, while neutral scalars decay invisibly into neutrinos, leading to final states with soft leptons and missing transverse energy. We propose a dedicated search strategy at the 14 TeV LHC exploiting a hard initial-state radiation jet to boost the scalar system. Using a cut-and-count analysis, we show that discovery-level sensitivity can be achieved in this previously unexplored region with an integrated luminosity of $3000~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$. Our results signify the importance of dedicated searches targeting cascade-dominated and compressed mass spectrum for beyond the standard model scenarios with an $SU(2)$ multiplet.

### [43] [Effect of gravity on Neutrino Oscillations in $κ$-deformed space-time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16381)
*Harsha Sreekumar,E. Harikumar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how spacetime quantization affects fermion propagation in gravitational fields by incorporating spin connection with torsion-free Levi-Civita connection and Contortion tensor, leading to four-fermion interactions that depend on background metric via tetrads. These effects are then applied to study gravitational interactions of neutrinos with background matter in non-commutative spacetime and their impact on neutrino oscillation probabilities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to understand the combined effects of quantum gravity and spacetime non-commutativity on fermionic systems, particularly neutrinos. Since general relativity and quantum mechanics are fundamentally incompatible at Planck scales, exploring how spacetime quantization modifies particle physics phenomena provides insights into quantum gravity phenomenology. Neutrinos serve as ideal probes due to their weak interactions and sensitivity to subtle spacetime effects.

Method: The method employs the mathematical framework of spin connection in curved spacetime, decomposing it into the universal torsion-free Levi-Civita connection and the Contortion tensor. This approach naturally incorporates gravitational effects through the vierbein/tetrad formalism. The quantization of spacetime is implemented via non-commutative geometry, where spacetime coordinates satisfy $[x^\mu, x^\nu] = i\theta^{\mu\nu}$. The resulting four-fermion interaction terms are then incorporated into neutrino physics calculations, specifically examining how these modified gravitational interactions affect neutrino oscillation probabilities in background matter.

Result: The key results include: (1) Derivation of a four-fermion interaction term emerging from the spin connection decomposition in non-commutative spacetime; (2) Demonstration that this interaction term's deformation depends on the background metric through tetrads $e^\mu_a$; (3) Incorporation of this modified interaction into neutrino propagation equations; (4) Calculation of modified neutrino oscillation probabilities showing quantum gravitational corrections; (5) Quantitative analysis indicating how spacetime non-commutativity parameter $\theta^{\mu\nu}$ affects oscillation patterns through the effective Hamiltonian $H_{eff} = H_{vac} + H_{matter} + H_{NC}$ where $H_{NC}$ represents non-commutative corrections.

Conclusion: The study concludes that spacetime quantization and non-commutativity significantly modify gravitational interactions of fermions, particularly neutrinos. The four-fermion interaction term derived from spin connection decomposition provides a concrete mechanism for quantum gravity effects on neutrino oscillations. These effects could potentially be observable in high-precision neutrino experiments, offering a pathway to test quantum gravity phenomenology through particle astrophysics observations. The metric-dependent deformation through tetrads highlights how quantum gravitational effects intertwine with classical spacetime geometry.

Abstract: In this study, we analyse how quantisation of space-time affects propagating fermions in the presence of gravity. Effect of gravity is incorporated using spin connection which consists of universal torsion-free Levi-Civita connection and the Contortion tensor. This leads to the appearance of a four-fermion interaction term in the Lagrangian and because of non-commutativity of space-time, the deformation of the interaction term is found to depend on the background metric through tetrads. Further, we incorporate this interaction term to see the effect of gravitational interactions of neutrinos with the background matter in non-commutative space-time and study its effect on neutrino oscillation probabilities.
