### [44] [Polarization-dependent mass modifications of $φ$ meson with finite momentum in nuclear matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15971)
*Ahmad Jafar Arifi,Philipp Gubler,Kazuo Tsushima*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [The in-medium properties of $φ$ mesons with finite momentum reveal broken Lorentz symmetry in nuclear matter, resulting in distinct longitudinal and transverse polarization modes with different density and momentum dependencies. The longitudinal mode shows momentum-dependent mass shifts through kaon-loop couplings to vector mean fields.]

[通过研究有限动量下的$φ$介子在核介质中的性质，揭示了核物质中破缺的洛伦兹对称性，导致纵向和横向极化模式具有不同的密度和动量依赖性。纵向模式通过与矢量平均场的kaon-loop耦合表现出动量相关的质量偏移。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Most studies of vector mesons in nuclear matter focus on particles at rest, overlooking momentum-dependent effects that become important for experimental measurements of high-momentum hadrons. The breakdown of Lorentz invariance in medium leads to momentum-dependent spectral functions that differ significantly between longitudinal and transverse polarizations, affecting observable signatures in heavy-ion collisions and nuclear reactions.]

[以往对核物质中矢量介子的研究主要集中于静止粒子，忽略了动量依赖性效应——这对高动量强子的实验测量至关重要。介质中洛伦兹不变性的破缺导致动量依赖的光谱函数，其纵向和横向极化模式表现出显著差异，影响重离子碰撞和核反应中的观测信号。]

Method: [Using an effective Lagrangian approach incorporating $φKK$ couplings and mean-field interactions, we compute the self-energy for both longitudinal ($L$) and transverse ($T$) polarizations with finite momentum $k$. Loop integrals involving kaon propagators are regulated via two schemes: (1) covariant form factors $F(q) = \\frac{\\Lambda^2}{\\Lambda^2 - q^2}$ and (2) dimensional regularization with subtractions at the vacuum mass. The coupling of the longitudinal mode to the vector mean field $V_μ$ through derivative interactions $∂_μφ^ν$ yields momentum dependence absent in transverse modes.]

[采用包含$φKK$耦合和平均场相互作用的有效拉格朗日方法，我们计算了有限动量$k$下纵向($L$)和横向($T$)极化模式的自身能量。涉及kaon传播子的圈积分通过两种方案正规化：(1) 协变形状因子$F(q) = \\frac{\\Lambda^2}{\\Lambda^2 - q^2}$；(2) 在真空质量处进行减除的维数正规化。纵向模式通过导数相互作用$∂_μφ^ν$与矢量平均场$V_μ$的耦合产生了横向模式中不存在的动量依赖性。]

Result: [For transverse polarizations, the in-medium mass shift $Δm_T = m_T^* - m_φ$ is independent of the $φ$-meson momentum $k$, depending only on nuclear density. For longitudinal polarizations, the mass shift decreases quadratically with momentum: $Δm_L(k) = Δm_L(0) + αk^2/m_φ^2$, where $α$ is negative and determined by coupling to the vector mean field. The width modifications also show polarization-dependent behavior, with the longitudinal width becoming more suppressed at higher momenta due to reduced phase space for kaon decay channels.]

[对于横向极化，介质中的质量偏移$Δm_T = m_T^* - m_φ$与$φ$介子动量$k$无关，仅取决于核密度。对于纵向极化，质量偏移随动量二次方减小：$Δm_L(k) = Δm_L(0) + αk^2/m_φ^2$，其中$α$为负值，由与矢量平均场的耦合决定。宽度修正也显示出极化依赖行为，由于kaon衰变通道的相空间减小，纵向宽度在更高动量下受到更强抑制。]

Conclusion: [The momentum dependence of $φ$-meson spectral functions in nuclear matter reveals fundamental broken Lorentz symmetry with observable consequences: transverse modes are density-sensitive but momentum-independent, while longitudinal modes carry both density and momentum information through coupling to vector mean fields. This provides new experimental signatures for upcoming measurements at J-PARC and future facilities, offering a precision test of chiral dynamics and in-medium QCD properties beyond the static limit.]

[核物质中$φ$介子光谱函数的动量依赖性揭示了基本的破缺洛伦兹对称性及其可观测后果：横向模式对密度敏感但与动量无关，而纵向模式通过矢量平均场的耦合携带密度和动量双重信息。这为J-PARC及未来设施的测量提供了新的实验特征信号，为超越静态极限的手征动力学和介质内QCD性质提供了精确检验。]

Abstract: We investigate the in-medium properties of the $φ$ meson with finite momentum, going beyond the commonly studied case at rest. In a nuclear medium, Lorentz invariance is broken, leading to distinct longitudinal and transverse polarization modes that evolve differently with density and momentum. Within an effective Lagrangian approach, we calculate the polarization-dependent mass shifts and width modifications of the $φ$ meson arising from kaon loops and mean-field interactions. The divergent loop integrals are regulated using two different schemes: a covariant form factor and dimensional regularization. Our results show that the mass shift of the transverse polarization is independent of the $φ$-meson momentum, whereas that of the longitudinal polarization decreases quadratically with momentum. This difference originates from the coupling of the longitudinal mode to the vector mean field and derivative-type interactions in the self-energy. These effects have direct implications for experimental observables, especially for upcoming measurements at J-PARC, and provide a new prediction for experiments studying hadron dynamics in dense matter.

</details>


### [45] [Light baryon static properties in dispersive approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15989)
*Shuge Zeng,Hsiang-nan Li,Fanrong Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [This paper extends dispersive analysis from mesons to light baryons, using dispersion relations as inverse problems to extract baryon static properties directly from spectral densities. The method simultaneously implements chiral-even and chiral-odd constraints to uniquely determine baryon masses and pole residues, finding a universal set of quark and gluon condensates that consistently describe ρ meson, proton, and Δ(1232) baryon masses.]

\n\n
[这篇论文将色散分析从介子扩展到轻子重子，使用色散关系作为逆问题直接从谱密度中提取重子静态性质。该方法同时实施手征偶和手征奇约束，唯一确定重子质量和极点残差，发现一组通用的夸克和胶子凝聚能够一致地描述ρ介子、质子和Δ(1232)重子的质量。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation stems from extending a previously developed dispersive formalism for mesons to baryonic systems, addressing limitations in conventional QCD sum rule approaches. Current methods often involve phenomenological parametrizations and approximations that may obscure direct connections between OPE inputs and physical observables. The authors seek to establish a more rigorous, analytically consistent framework that treats dispersion relations as inverse problems to extract baryon properties directly from spectral densities without intermediate modeling assumptions.]

\n\n
[动机源自将先前为介子开发的色散形式体系扩展到重子系统，解决传统QCD求和规则方法的局限性。当前方法通常涉及唯象参数化和近似，可能模糊OPE输入与物理可观测量之间的直接联系。作者旨在建立一个更严格、解析一致的理论框架，将色散关系视为逆问题，直接从谱密度中提取重子性质，而无需中间建模假设。]

Method: [The methodology involves treating dispersion relations for baryonic correlation functions as inverse problems. The formalism solves for the spectral density using available operator-product-expansion (OPE) inputs directly, rather than parametrizing the spectral function phenomenologically. Key innovations include: (1) simultaneous implementation of both chiral-even and chiral-odd dispersive constraints, (2) direct extraction of baryon static properties from the spectral density solution, and (3) using the OPE factorization with universal quark and gluon condensates. The approach bypasses conventional spectral function modeling and directly connects QCD condensates to baryon observables through analytic continuation.]

\n\n
[方法学涉及将重子关联函数的色散关系处理为逆问题。该形式体系直接使用可用的算符乘积展开输入来求解谱密度，而不是唯象地参数化谱函数。关键创新包括：(1) 同时实施手征偶和手征奇色散约束，(2) 直接从谱密度解中提取重子静态性质，(3) 使用具有通用夸克和胶子凝聚的OPE因子化。该方法绕过了传统的谱函数建模，通过解析延拓直接将QCD凝聚与重子可观测量联系起来。]

Result: [The key results demonstrate: (1) The simultaneous chiral-even and chiral-odd constraints uniquely determine baryon masses and pole residues without ambiguities typically encountered in conventional sum rules. (2) A common universal set of quark and gluon condensates appearing in OPE factorization successfully accommodates the masses of a ρ meson, proton, and Δ(1232) baryon, showing consistency across different hadronic systems. (3) The approach exhibits advantages over conventional QCD sum rule treatments by eliminating model-dependent spectral function parametrizations and providing a more direct connection between QCD vacuum structure and baryon properties.]

\n\n
[关键结果表明：(1) 同时的手征偶和手征奇约束唯一地确定了重子质量和极点残差，避免了传统求和规则中常见的模糊性。(2) OPE因子化中出现的一组通用的夸克和胶子凝聚成功地容纳了ρ介子、质子和Δ(1232)重子的质量，显示了不同强子系统之间的一致性。(3) 与传统QCD求和规则处理相比，该方法消除了依赖于模型的谱函数参数化，提供了QCD真空结构与重子性质之间更直接的连接，显示出优势。]

Conclusion: [The work establishes that dispersive analyses can be successfully extended from mesons to baryons, providing a novel nonperturbative analytical method for studying baryon systems. The formalism's ability to simultaneously incorporate chiral-even and chiral-odd constraints with universal condensates demonstrates a more fundamental connection between QCD vacuum structure and hadron properties. The approach offers advantages over conventional sum rule techniques by treating dispersion relations as inverse problems, encouraging broader applications to various baryonic systems and potentially enabling more precise determinations of hadronic parameters from first principles QCD.]

\n\n
[这项工作确立了色散分析可以从介子成功扩展到重子，为研究重子系统提供了一种新颖的非微扰解析方法。该形式体系同时结合手征偶和手征奇约束与通用凝聚的能力，展示了QCD真空结构与强子性质之间更基本的联系。通过将色散关系处理为逆问题，该方法相对于传统求和规则技术具有优势，鼓励在各种重子系统中的广泛应用，并可能实现从第一性原理QCD更精确地确定强子参数。]

Abstract: We extend our dispersive analyses on meson static properties to those of light baryons. The formalism treats the dispersion relation, which a baryonic correlation function obeys, as an inverse problem, solve for the involved spectral density with available operator-product-expansion (OPE) inputs directly, and extract baryon static properties from the spectral density. We observe that the simultaneous implementation of the chiral-even and chiral-odd dispersive constraints unambiguously determines baryon masses and pole residues. A common set of quark and gluon condensates, which appear in OPE factorization and are universal, is found to accommodate the masses of a $ρ$ meson, a proton and a $Δ(1232)$ baryon. The advantage of our approach over the conventional handling of QCD sum rules is advocated. This work encourages broad applications of our nonperturbative analytical method to baryon systems.

</details>


### [46] [Probing the equivalence of chiral LCSRs in $D \to πe ν_e$ decays and extraction of $|V_{cd}|$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16038)
*Xiu-Fen Wang,Hai-Jiang Tian,Yin-Long Yang,Long Zeng,Hai-Bing Fu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [The paper calculates $D\toπ$ transition form factors using light-cone sum rules with chiral currents and LCHO model for twist-2,3 LCDAs. Results include branching fractions and $|V_{cd}|$ extraction with good agreement to existing literature.]

\n\n
[该论文使用手征流下的光锥求和规则以及LCHO模型对twist-2,3光锥分布振幅，计算了$D\toπ$跃迁形状因子。结果给出了分支比和$|V_{cd}|$的提取值，与现有文献结果吻合良好。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Accurate determination of $D\toπ$ semileptonic decay form factors is crucial for extracting the CKM matrix element $|V_{cd}|$ and testing Standard Model predictions. However, theoretical calculations face challenges from non-perturbative QCD effects, requiring reliable methods like light-cone sum rules with proper treatment of hadronic distribution amplitudes.]

\n\n
[精确确定$D\toπ$半轻衰变的形状因子对于提取CKM矩阵元$|V_{cd}|$和检验标准模型预言至关重要。然而，理论计算面临非微扰QCD效应的挑战，需要可靠的方法如光锥求和规则并结合恰当的强子分布振幅处理。]

Method: [Employed light-cone sum rule (LCSR) within chiral current approach. Used two different correlator currents: (1) right-handed current for vector form factor calculation up to next-to-leading-order accuracy, (2) left-handed current for leading-order accuracy. Constructed twist-2 and twist-3 light-cone distribution amplitudes (LCDAs) using light-cone harmonic oscillator (LCHO) model. Extended TFFs to whole physical $q^2$-region using simplified $z$-series expansion. Theoretical framework incorporates perturbative QCD calculations with hadronic parametrization.]

\n\n
[采用了手征流下的光锥求和规则方法。使用两种不同的关联子流：(1)右手流用于计算矢量形状因子，达到次领头阶精度；(2)左手流用于领头阶精度。使用光锥谐振子模型构建了twist-2和twist-3的光锥分布振幅。通过简化的$z$-级数展开将形状因子扩展到整个物理$q^2$区域。理论框架结合了微扰QCD计算和强子参数化。]

Result: [Calculated branching fractions: $\mathcal{B}(D^0\to π^-e^+ν_e)_{\text{I}} = 0.31_{-0.05}^{+0.05}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^+\to π^0e^+ν_e)_{\text{I}} = 0.39_{-0.06}^{+0.06}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^0\to π^-e^+ν_e)_{\text{II}} = 0.27_{-0.03}^{+0.05}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^+\to π^0e^+ν_e)_{\text{II}} = 0.34_{-0.04}^{+0.06}$ (in units of $10^{-2}$). Extracted CKM matrix elements: $|V_{cd}|_{\text{I}} = (0.21^{+0.02}_{-0.02}) \times 10^{-2}$, $|V_{cd}|_{\text{II}} = (0.23^{+0.02}_{-0.02}) \times 10^{-2}$. Results show good agreement with existing literature within uncertainties, validating the LCHO model for twist-2,3 LCDAs and the chiral current LCSR approach.]

\n\n
[计算了分支比：$\mathcal{B}(D^0\to π^-e^+ν_e)_{\text{I}} = 0.31_{-0.05}^{+0.05}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^+\to π^0e^+ν_e)_{\text{I}} = 0.39_{-0.06}^{+0.06}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^0\to π^-e^+ν_e)_{\text{II}} = 0.27_{-0.03}^{+0.05}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^+\to π^0e^+ν_e)_{\text{II}} = 0.34_{-0.04}^{+0.06}$（单位为$10^{-2}$）。提取的CKM矩阵元：$|V_{cd}|_{\text{I}} = (0.21^{+0.02}_{-0.02}) \times 10^{-2}$, $|V_{cd}|_{\text{II}} = (0.23^{+0.02}_{-0.02}) \times 10^{-2}$。结果在误差范围内与现有文献吻合良好，验证了LCHO模型对twist-2,3 LCDAs以及手征流光锥求和规则方法的有效性。]

Conclusion: [The study demonstrates that light-cone sum rules with chiral currents combined with LCHO-model constructed twist-2,3 LCDAs provide a reliable framework for calculating $D\toπ$ transition form factors. The extracted $|V_{cd}|$ values are consistent with other determinations, supporting the Standard Model CKM matrix structure. The method offers improved theoretical control over non-perturbative QCD effects in heavy-light transitions.]

\n\n
[研究表明，结合手征流的光锥求和规则与LCHO模型构建的twist-2,3 LCDAs为计算$D\toπ$跃迁形状因子提供了可靠框架。提取的$|V_{cd}|$值与其他测定结果一致，支持了标准模型的CKM矩阵结构。该方法为重-轻夸克跃迁中的非微扰QCD效应提供了改进的理论控制。]

Abstract: In the paper, we have carried out research on the $D\toπ$ decay process. We employ two different currents to study the $D\toπ$ transition form factors (TFFs) by using the light-cone sum rule within the framework of chiral current approach. Firstly, we follow the right-handed and left-handed currents for the correlators to present the expression of the vector form factors upto next-leading-order and leading-order accuracy, respectively. Here the twist-2 and twist-3 light-cone distribution amplitudes are constructed by the light-cone harmonic oscillator model. After exploring the TFFs into the whole physical $q^2$-region with the simplified $z$-series expansion, we obtain the branching fractions $\mathcal{B}(D^0\to π^-e^+ν_e)_{\text{I}} = 0.31_{-0.05}^{+0.05}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^+\to π^0e^+ν_e)_{\text{I}} = 0.39_{-0.06}^{+0.06}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^0\to π^-e^+ν_e)_{\text{II}} = 0.27_{-0.03}^{+0.05}$, $\mathcal{B}(D^+\to π^0e^+ν_e)_{\text{II}} = 0.34_{-0.04}^{+0.06}$, and extract the CKM matrix element $|V_{cd}|_{\text{I}} = ( 0.21^{+0.02}_{-0.02} )\times 10^{-2}$ as well as $|V_{cd}|_{\text{II}} = ( 0.23^{+0.02}_{-0.02}) \times 10^{-2}$. To verify the credibility of our calculations, these results are further compared with existing findings in the literature, showing good agreement within uncertainties.

</details>


### [47] [Light baryon spectra and Regge trajectories from anomalous holographic hard wall models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16727)
*Rafael A. Costa-Silva,Henrique Boschi-Filho*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [This work introduces anomalous modifications to the holographic hard wall model to describe light baryon spectra, incorporating logarithmic anomalous dimensions from semiclassical AdS/CFT analysis to improve Regge trajectory predictions for spin-1/2 and 3/2 baryons.]

\n\n
[本研究引入对全息硬壁模型的异常修正来描述轻重子谱系，结合了来自半经典AdS/CFT分析的对数反常维度，以改进自旋-1/2和3/2重子的Regge轨迹预测。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The holographic hard wall (HW) model, while successful for mesons, requires refinement for baryon spectra. The original HW model's predictions for baryonic Regge trajectories deviate from experimental data. Recent applications of anomalous dimensions from semiclassical AdS/CFT analysis to glueballs and unflavored mesons showed improved mass spectra. This motivates exploring similar anomalous modifications to the HW model for light baryons (spin 1/2 and 3/2) to better match PDG data and achieve more linear Regge trajectories.]

\n\n
[全息硬壁模型在介子方面虽然成功，但对重子谱系需要进一步改进。原始HW模型对重子Regge轨迹的预测与实验数据存在偏差。最近将半经典AdS/CFT分析中的反常维度应用于胶球和无味介子显示出改进的质量谱。这启发了探索对HW模型的类似异常修正，用于轻重子（自旋1/2和3/2），以更好地匹配PDG数据并获得更线性的Regge轨迹。]

Method: [Three anomalous versions of the holographic hard wall model are proposed: 

1. AHW$_1$: Incorporates anomalous dimension $\\Delta_{\\rm anom.}=a\\ln L +b$, where $a$ and $b$ are phenomenological constants fitted to PDG data, and $L$ is angular momentum.

2. AHW$_2$: Extends the anomalous dimension to include spin dependence: $\\Delta_{\\rm anom.}=a\\ln (L+S+1/2) +b$, where $S$ is spin.

3. Linear anomalous model: Uses $\\Delta_{\\rm Lin.}=a L^c +b$ with constants $a$, $b$, and $c$ fitted to light baryon masses.

The anomalous contributions originate from semiclassical analysis of AdS/CFT correspondence. The parameters are adjusted numerically to optimize agreement with experimental baryon masses from PDG.]

\n\n
[提出了三种异常版本的全息硬壁模型：

1. AHW$_1$：包含反常维度$\\Delta_{\\rm anom.}=a\\ln L +b$，其中$a$和$b$是根据PDG数据拟合的现象学常数，$L$是角动量。

2. AHW$_2$：将反常维度扩展到包含自旋依赖性：$\\Delta_{\\rm anom.}=a\\ln (L+S+1/2) +b$，其中$S$是自旋。

3. 线性异常模型：使用$\\Delta_{\\rm Lin.}=a L^c +b$，常数$a$、$b$和$c$根据轻重子质量拟合。

反常贡献源于AdS/CFT对应的半经典分析。参数通过数值调整以优化与PDG实验重子质量的一致性。]

Result: [All three anomalous HW models produce improved predictions compared to the original HW model:

1. AHW$_1$ and AHW$_2$ yield better fits to light baryon masses from PDG, showing approximately linear Regge trajectories $(M^2\\times L)$.

2. The linear anomalous model (AHW$_3$) generates Regge trajectories that are asymptotically linear, in addition to providing masses compatible with PDG data.

3. The logarithmic anomalous dimensions from semiclassical AdS/CFT analysis successfully extend to baryonic systems, demonstrating the universality of this approach across different hadronic sectors.]

\n\n
[所有三种异常HW模型相比原始HW模型都产生了改进的预测：

1. AHW$_1$和AHW$_2$对PDG的轻重子质量产生了更好的拟合，显示出近似线性的Regge轨迹$(M^2\\times L)$。

2. 线性异常模型（AHW$_3$）除了提供与PDG数据兼容的质量外，还生成了渐近线性的Regge轨迹。

3. 来自半经典AdS/CFT分析的对数反常维度成功扩展到重子系统，证明了这种方法在不同强子扇区中的普适性。]

Conclusion: [Anomalous modifications to the holographic hard wall model significantly improve its predictive power for light baryon spectra. The logarithmic anomalous dimensions derived from semiclassical AdS/CFT analysis provide a robust framework for describing both mesonic and baryonic hadrons. The three proposed models (AHW$_1$, AHW$_2$, and the linear variant) offer different levels of phenomenological refinement, with the logarithmic forms showing particular promise for generating linear Regge trajectories. This work establishes the efficacy of incorporating anomalous dimensions into holographic QCD models for baryonic systems.]

\n\n
[对全息硬壁模型的异常修正显著提高了其对轻重子谱系的预测能力。从半经典AdS/CFT分析推导的对数反常维度为描述介子和重子强子提供了一个稳健的框架。提出的三种模型（AHW$_1$、AHW$_2$和线性变体）提供了不同层次的现象学改进，其中对数形式在生成线性Regge轨迹方面显示出特别的潜力。这项工作确立了将反常维度纳入全息QCD模型以处理重子系统的有效性。]

Abstract: In this work we propose anomalous versions of the holographic hard wall (HW) model to describe the spectra of light baryons of spin 1/2 and 3/2, and obtain their Regge trajectories. The anomalous contributions to the dimensions of the baryonic operators of logarithm form come from a semiclassical analysis of the AdS/CFT correspondence and were used recently for glueballs and light unflavoured mesons. Inspired by these results, we first propose an anomalous dimension of the form $Δ_{\rm anom.}=a\ln L +b$, where $a$ and $b$ are phenomenological constants to be adjusted numerically to better fit the experimental data of the PDG, and $L$ is the angular momentum of each baryonic state. Second, we discuss the case where the anomalous dimension also depends on the spin $S$ as $Δ_{\rm anom.}=a\ln (L+S+1/2) +b$, and fix the parameters $a$ and $b$ targeting PDG data. These two models, called AHW$_1$ and AHW$_2$, give better results for light baryon masses $(M)$ in comparison with the original HW model and show approximately linear Regge trajectories $(M^2\times L)$. We also consider a third anomalous HW model in which the dimension of the baryonic operator increases as $Δ_{\rm Lin.}=a L^c +b$, where $a$, $b$, and $c$ are constants adjusted to fit the light baryonic masses of PDG. Apart from compatible masses with PDG data, this case produces Regge trajectories that are asymptotically linear.

</details>


### [48] [Investigation of the $D^{0} \rightarrow K_S^{0} π^{0} η,\ K_S^{0} π^{0} π^0$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16082)
*Wei Liang,Chu-Wen Xiao,Guo-Mei Gan,Shi-Qi Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a theoretical analysis of $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$ and $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$ decays using a unified final state interaction formalism that incorporates S-wave meson-meson interactions from chiral unitary approach and P-wave contributions from $\bar{K}^*(892)$ resonance. The combined fit to BESIII data reveals the dynamical origin of observed structures: $a_0(980)$ in $π^0η$ distribution, and $f_0(500)/\bar{K}^*(892)$ combination plus $f_0(980)$ in $π^0π^0$ distribution.

本文使用统一的末态相互作用形式对 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$ 和 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$ 衰变进行理论分析，该方法结合了手征幺正方法中的S波介子-介子相互作用以及 $\bar{K}^*(892)$ 共振的P波贡献。与BESIII数据的联合拟合揭示了观测结构的动力学起源：$π^0η$ 分布中的 $a_0(980)$，以及 $π^0π^0$ 分布中的 $f_0(500)/\bar{K}^*(892)$ 组合加上 $f_0(980)$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to provide a theoretical understanding of the recently reported BESIII data on $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$ and $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$ decays. Specifically, the experimental data shows intriguing structures in the invariant mass distributions: a peak near 1.0 GeV in $π^0η$ distribution and a near-threshold enhancement plus cusp-like structure around 1 GeV$^2$ in $π^0π^0$ distribution. The authors aim to interpret these features within a unified theoretical framework that properly accounts for final state interactions, particularly the interplay between S-wave meson-meson scattering amplitudes from chiral unitary approach and P-wave resonance contributions.

主要动机是为最近BESIII报告的 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$ 和 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$ 衰变数据提供理论理解。具体来说，实验数据显示不变质量分布中存在有趣的结构：$π^0η$ 分布中1.0 GeV附近的峰，以及 $π^0π^0$ 分布中的近阈值增强和1 GeV$^2$附近的尖端结构。作者旨在统一理论框架内解释这些特征，该框架适当考虑了末态相互作用，特别是手征幺正方法中的S波介子-介子散射振幅与P波共振贡献之间的相互作用。

Method: The methodology employs a unified final state interaction (FSI) formalism combining two distinct components: (1) S-wave pseudoscalar meson-pseudoscalar meson interactions described within a chiral unitary approach, which dynamically generates resonances like $a_0(980)$ and $f_0(500)/f_0(980)$; (2) P-wave contributions from the intermediate vector resonance $\bar{K}^*(892)$. The theoretical framework incorporates coherence (interference) between S- and P-wave amplitudes. The approach utilizes unitarized chiral perturbation theory amplitudes for meson-meson scattering in coupled channels. For $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$, the formalism includes $πη \to πη$ and $K\bar{K} \to πη$ transitions. For $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$, it involves $ππ \to ππ$ and $K\bar{K} \to ππ$ transitions. The free parameters (coupling constants, production strengths) are determined through a combined fit to the experimental invariant mass spectra from BESIII.

该方法采用统一的末态相互作用(FSI)形式，结合两个不同组成部分：(1) 在手征幺正方法中描述的S波赝标介子-赝标介子相互作用，该方法动态生成 $a_0(980)$ 和 $f_0(500)/f_0(980)$ 等共振；(2) 来自中间矢量共振 $\bar{K}^*(892)$ 的P波贡献。理论框架包含了S波和P波振幅之间的相干性(干涉)。该方法利用耦合道中介子-介子散射的幺正化手征微扰理论振幅。对于 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$，形式包括了 $πη \to πη$ 和 $K\bar{K} \to πη$ 跃迁。对于 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$，涉及 $ππ \to ππ$ 和 $K\bar{K} \to ππ$ 跃迁。自由参数(耦合常数、产生强度)通过对BESIII实验不变质量谱的联合拟合确定。

Result: The theoretical analysis yields excellent agreement with BESIII experimental data for both decays. For $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$, the structure near 1.0 GeV in $π^0η$ invariant mass distribution is identified as the $a_0(980)$ resonance, dynamically generated from S-wave $πη/K\bar{K}$ interactions within the chiral unitary approach. For $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$, the near-threshold enhancement in $π^0π^0$ mass distribution arises from combined contributions of the $f_0(500)$ (generated from S-wave $ππ/K\bar{K}$ interactions) and the intermediate $\bar{K}^*(892)$ resonance. The cusp-like structure around 1 GeV$^2$ is associated with the $f_0(980)$ resonance, also dynamically generated from coupled-channel interactions. The successful description confirms that these scalar resonances ($a_0(980)$, $f_0(500)$, $f_0(980)$) emerge as dynamically generated states rather than elementary particles in the quark model. The interference between S-wave (from chiral unitary approach) and P-wave (from $\bar{K}^*(892)$) amplitudes is crucial for reproducing the observed spectral shapes.

理论分析显示与BESIII两个衰变的实验数据高度一致。对于 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$，$π^0η$ 不变质量分布中1.0 GeV附近的结构被确认为 $a_0(980)$ 共振，在手征幺正方法中从S波 $πη/K\bar{K}$ 相互作用动态生成。对于 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$，$π^0π^0$ 质量分布中的近阈值增强来自 $f_0(500)$(从S波 $ππ/K\bar{K}$ 相互作用生成)和中间 $\bar{K}^*(892)$ 共振的组合贡献。1 GeV$^2$附近的尖端结构与 $f_0(980)$ 共振相关，也从耦合道相互作用动态生成。成功的描述证实了这些标量共振($a_0(980)$、$f_0(500)$、$f_0(980)$)是作为动态生成态出现，而非夸克模型中的基本粒子。S波(来自手征幺正方法)和P波(来自 $\bar{K}^*(892)$)振幅之间的干涉对于重现观测到的谱形至关重要。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that a unified final state interaction formalism incorporating both S-wave meson-meson scattering from chiral unitary approach and P-wave $\bar{K}^*(892)$ resonance contributions successfully explains the BESIII data on $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$ and $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$ decays. The observed structures ($a_0(980)$ signal in $π^0η$, near-threshold enhancement and cusp in $π^0π^0$) find natural interpretation as dynamically generated scalar resonances from coupled-channel meson-meson interactions. This work provides strong evidence for the molecular nature of light scalar mesons ($a_0(980)$, $f_0(500)$, $f_0(980)$) and highlights the importance of coherent interference between different partial wave contributions in understanding hadronic decays of heavy mesons. The methodology establishes a framework for analyzing similar multi-body decays where both scalar resonances (dynamically generated) and conventional $q\bar{q}$ resonances coexist and interfere.

本文证明，结合手征幺正方法的S波介子-介子散射和P波 $\bar{K}^*(892)$ 共振贡献的统一末态相互作用形式，成功解释了BESIII关于 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 η$ 和 $D^0 \to K_S^0 π^0 π^0$ 衰变的数据。观测到的结构($π^0η$ 中的 $a_0(980)$ 信号，$π^0π^0$ 中的近阈值增强和尖端)被自然地解释为来自耦合道介子-介子相互作用的动态生成标量共振。这项工作为轻标量介子($a_0(980)$、$f_0(500)$、$f_0(980)$)的分子性质提供了有力证据，并强调了不同分波贡献之间相干干涉在理解重介子强子衰变中的重要性。该方法建立了一个分析类似多体衰变的框架，其中标量共振(动态生成)和传统 $q\bar{q}$ 共振共存并发生干涉。

Abstract: Inspired by the invariant mass distributions for the decays $D^{0} \rightarrow K_S^{0} π^{0} η$ and $D^{0} \rightarrow K_S^{0} π^{0} π^{0}$ reported by the BESIII Collaboration, we investigate these processes with an unified final state interaction formalism by incorporating both the $S$-wave pseudoscalar meson-pseudoscalar meson interactions within a chiral unitary approach and the $P$-wave contribution from the intermediate resonance $\bar{K}^*(892)$. By performing a combined fit to the invariant mass spectra and taking into account the coherence between the $S$- and $P$-waves, our results are in agreement with the experimental data. For the decay $D^{0} \rightarrow K_S^{0} π^{0} η$, the structure near 1.0 GeV in the $π^0 η$ invariant mass distribution corresponds to the signal of the $a_{0}(980)$, which is dynamically generated from the $S$-wave interactions. In the case of $D^{0} \rightarrow K_S^{0} π^{0} π^{0}$, the near-threshold enhancement in the $π^0π^0$ mass distribution arises from the combined contributions of the $f_0(500)$ and the intermediate $\bar{K}^*(892)$, while the cusp-like structure around 1 GeV$^2$ is associated with the $f_0(980)$.

### [49] [Two-loop Six-point Planar Massless Feynman Integrals to Higher $ε$ Orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16831)
*Yuanche Liu,Antonela Matijašić,Tiziano Peraro,Yingxuan Xu,Zihua Yang,Yang Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper computes two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integrals to higher orders in dimensional regularization (ε-expansion) up to weight six, identifying the complete alphabet of 269 letters, deriving analytic canonical differential equations, and efficiently evaluating the pure basis in physical scattering regions using Chebyshev pseudospectral transport.

本文计算了两圈六点平面无质量费曼积分在维度正则化参数ε的高阶展开（达到权重六），识别了包含269个字母的完整字母表，导出了解析正则微分方程，并使用切比雪夫伪谱输运方法在物理散射区域高效评估了纯基函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Two-loop multi-leg scattering amplitudes in gauge theories require higher-order ε-expansions of Feynman integrals beyond weight four. Current calculations for two-loop gauge theory amplitudes only reach weight four in ε-expansion, limiting applications to three-loop computations and formal studies of symbol structures and cluster algebras. There is a need to extend these calculations to higher transcendental weights (weight six) to enable future three-loop amplitude calculations and deepen theoretical understanding of mathematical structures.

规范理论中两圈多腿散射振幅需要费曼积分在维度正则化参数ε的高阶展开，超越权重四。当前两圈规范理论振幅计算仅达到ε展开的权重四，限制了其在三圈计算以及符号结构和丛代数形式研究中的应用。需要将这些计算扩展到更高超越权重（权重六），以支持未来的三圈振幅计算并深化对数学结构的理论理解。

Method: The authors employ modern rational reconstruction methods to identify the complete alphabet of 269 letters relevant for all-weight orders. They derive analytic canonical differential equations for the Feynman integrals. A novel computational technique is introduced: Chebyshev pseudospectral transport method for efficient evaluation of the pure basis up to weight six (to $\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$) in physical scattering regions. This involves representing the differential equations in terms of Chebyshev polynomials for numerical integration.

作者采用现代有理重构方法来识别与所有权重阶相关的完整269个字母的字母表。他们导出了费曼积分的解析正则微分方程。引入了一种新颖的计算技术：切比雪夫伪谱输运方法，用于在物理散射区域高效评估直至权重六（达到$\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$）的纯基函数。这涉及用切比雪夫多项式表示微分方程进行数值积分。

Result: Complete alphabet identification with 269 letters for two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integrals. Derivation of analytic canonical differential equations. Symbols computed up to weight six. Efficient evaluation of pure basis up to weight six ($\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$) in physical scattering regions using Chebyshev pseudospectral transport. Demonstration that the method provides high-precision numerical results suitable for amplitude computations.

识别了两圈六点平面无质量费曼积分的完整269个字母字母表。导出了解析正则微分方程。计算了直至权重六的符号。使用切比雪夫伪谱输运方法在物理散射区域高效评估了直至权重六（$\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$）的纯基函数。证明了该方法能够提供适用于振幅计算的高精度数值结果。

Conclusion: The work extends two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integral calculations from weight four to weight six in ε-expansion, providing essential building blocks for future three-loop amplitude computations. The identification of the complete 269-letter alphabet and derivation of canonical differential equations represent significant advances in understanding the mathematical structure of multi-loop integrals. The Chebyshev pseudospectral transport method offers an efficient computational approach for evaluating high-weight transcendental functions in physical regions, with applications extending to formal studies of symbols and cluster algebras.

该工作将两圈六点平面无质量费曼积分的计算从ε展开的权重四扩展到权重六，为未来的三圈振幅计算提供了基本构建模块。完整269个字母字母表的识别和正则微分方程的推导代表了对多圈积分数学结构理解的重大进展。切比雪夫伪谱输运方法为在物理区域评估高权重超越函数提供了一种高效的计算方法，其应用范围扩展到符号和丛代数的形式研究。

Abstract: In this work, we calculate two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integrals at higher orders in the dimensional regulator $ε$, corresponding to higher transcendental weights. In previous works, these integrals were calculated up to weight four for the purpose of two-loop gauge theory amplitudes. Using modern rational reconstruction methods, we identify the complete alphabet with $269$ letters relevant for the all-weight orders, derive the analytic canonical differential equation and obtain the symbols up to weight six. As a proof of concept, using a new method with Chebyshev pseudospectral transport, we show that the corresponding pure basis can be efficiently evaluated up to weight six, i.e., to $ \mathcal{O}(ε^2)$ in a physical scattering region. The results of this work can be applied to future three-loop amplitudes and provide new data for the formal study of symbols and cluster algebra.

### [50] [Puzzles in charmed baryon semileptonic decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16323)
*Chao-Qiang Geng,Chia-Wei Liu,Sheng-Lin Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper addresses large apparent $SU(3)_F$ flavor symmetry breaking in semileptonic decays of singly charmed baryons, where tensions with lattice QCD suggest either unknown hadronic mechanisms or new physics. The authors develop a systematic framework that matches lattice-QCD inputs onto an $SU(3)_F$ analysis including first-order symmetry breaking, making precise predictions for ratios of branching fractions: ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΣ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(2.6\pm0.3)\%$ and ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΛ^0\ell^+ ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(1.1\pm0.1)\%.$ These predictions provide clean experimental tests to determine whether the observed large $SU(3)_F$ breaking arises from standard hadronic effects or signals new physics.

本文针对单粲重子的半轻衰变中表现出的巨大$SU(3)_F$味对称性破缺问题展开研究，其中与格点QCD的紧张关系暗示了未知的强子机制或新物理的存在。作者开发了一个系统性的框架，将格点QCD输入匹配到包含一阶对称性破缺的$SU(3)_F$分析中，并精确预测了分支比比值：${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΣ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(2.6\pm0.3)\%$ 和 ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΛ^0\ell^+ ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(1.1\pm0.1)\%.$ 这些预测提供了清晰的实验检验方法，以确定观测到的大$SU(3)_F$破缺是源于标准强子效应，还是新物理的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent observations in semileptonic decays of singly charmed baryons reveal unexpectedly large apparent $SU(3)_F$ flavor symmetry breaking that creates tension with lattice QCD predictions. This discrepancy suggests two possibilities: either there is an unanticipated hadronic mechanism within the Standard Model that generates such large symmetry breaking, or it could signal new physics beyond the Standard Model. Resolving this puzzle is crucial for understanding heavy quark physics, flavor symmetry breaking patterns, and potentially discovering physics beyond the Standard Model. The authors aim to develop a systematic approach to clarify the origin of this anomalous breaking.

最近在单粲重子的半轻衰变观测中揭示了意外巨大表观$SU(3)_F$味对称性破缺，这与格点QCD预测产生紧张关系。这种差异暗示两种可能性：要么是标准模型内存在未预料的强子机制产生如此大的对称性破缺，要么可能是超出标准模型的新物理信号。解决这个谜题对于理解重夸克物理、味对称性破缺模式以及潜在发现超出标准模型的物理至关重要。作者旨在开发一种系统方法来澄清这种反常破缺的来源。

Method: The authors formulate a systematic theoretical framework that bridges lattice QCD calculations and $SU(3)_F$ flavor symmetry analyses. The method involves: (1) Performing a rigorous matching of lattice-QCD inputs onto an $SU(3)_F$ expansion, (2) Incorporating first-order symmetry breaking corrections within the $SU(3)_F$ formalism, (3) Deriving constraints from the symmetry structure of the weak Hamiltonian and baryon wavefunctions, (4) Using the measured branching fractions of reference channels to normalize predictions, and (5) Calculating specific ratios of branching fractions that are particularly sensitive to the origin of the $SU(3)_F$ breaking. The framework systematically accounts for both symmetry-conserving and symmetry-breaking contributions.

作者建立了一个连接格点QCD计算和$SU(3)_F$味对称性分析的系统性理论框架。方法包括：(1) 将格点QCD输入严格匹配到$SU(3)_F$展开，(2) 在$SU(3)_F$形式中纳入一阶对称性破缺修正，(3) 从弱哈密顿量和重子波函数的对称结构中推导约束条件，(4) 使用参考道测量的分支比对预测进行归一化，(5) 计算对$SU(3)_F$破缺来源特别敏感的分支比比值。该框架系统地考虑了对称性守恒和对称性破缺的贡献。

Result: The framework yields precise predictions for two key branching fraction ratios that serve as clean experimental probes: ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΣ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(2.6\pm0.3)\%$ and ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΛ^0\ell^+ ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(1.1\pm0.1)\%.$ These predictions are significantly different from what would be expected if the large apparent $SU(3)_F$ breaking were due to new physics rather than hadronic mechanisms. The small uncertainties reflect the constrained nature of the systematic framework. The results provide specific targets for experimental measurements at facilities like LHCb, Belle II, and BESIII.

该框架为两个关键分支比比值提供了精确预测，作为清晰的实验探针：${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΣ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(2.6\pm0.3)\%$ 和 ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΛ^0\ell^+ ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(1.1\pm0.1)\%.$ 这些预测与如果大表观$SU(3)_F$破缺源于新物理而非强子机制的情况有显著差异。小不确定性反映了系统框架的约束性质。结果为LHCb、Belle II和BESIII等设施的实验测量提供了具体目标。

Conclusion: The systematic framework connecting lattice QCD to $SU(3)_F$ symmetry analysis with first-order breaking corrections provides a powerful tool to resolve the puzzle of large apparent $SU(3)_F$ breaking in singly charmed baryon decays. The precise predictions for specific branching fraction ratios offer clear experimental tests that can distinguish between two competing explanations: unexpected hadronic mechanisms within the Standard Model versus new physics. Future measurements of these ratios at particle physics experiments will provide decisive evidence about the origin of the anomalous symmetry breaking. This approach demonstrates how combining precise lattice QCD calculations with systematic symmetry analyses can resolve tensions in flavor physics.

连接格点QCD与包含一阶破缺修正的$SU(3)_F$对称性分析的系统框架为解决单粲重子衰变中大表观$SU(3)_F$破缺的谜题提供了有力工具。对特定分支比比值的精确预测提供了清晰的实验检验方法，能够区分两种竞争解释：标准模型内未预料的强子机制与新物理。未来在粒子物理实验中对这些比值的测量将为反常对称性破缺的来源提供决定性证据。这种方法展示了如何将精确的格点QCD计算与系统性的对称性分析相结合，以解决味物理中的紧张关系。

Abstract: Large apparent $SU(3)_F$ breaking and a tension with lattice QCD have recently emerged in semileptonic decays of singly charmed baryons, hinting at either an unexpected hadronic mechanism or new physics. We formulate a framework that systematically matches lattice-QCD inputs onto an $SU(3)_F$ analysis including first-order symmetry breaking. We predict ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΣ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(2.6\pm0.3)\%,$ and ${\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΛ^0\ell^+ ν_\ell)/{\mathcal{B}}(Ξ_c^+\toΞ^0\ell^+ν_\ell)=(1.1\pm0.1)\%$, whose precise measurements would cleanly determine the origin of the anomalously large $SU(3)_F$ breaking.

### [51] [A Common Origin for Diverse Neutrino Mass Matrix Textures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16561)
*Manash Dey,Pralay Chakraborty,Dipshikha Das,Subhankar Roy*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We demonstrate that a $Δ(27)$ flavor symmetry framework, combined with Type-I+II seesaw mechanisms, can unify multiple neutrino mass textures from the literature without additional assumptions, showing their common theoretical origin through specific vacuum alignments and Yukawa structures.

我们证明，结合 Type-I+II seesaw 机制的 $Δ(27)$ 味对称框架可以统一文献中的多种中微子质量结构，无需额外假设，通过特定的真空对齐和 Yukawa 结构展示它们的共同理论起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The phenomenological literature contains diverse neutrino mass textures used to explain neutrino oscillation data, but their theoretical origins often appear disconnected. This work aims to unify these viable textures within a single minimal $Δ(27)$ flavor symmetry framework using Type-I+II seesaw mechanisms, demonstrating their common origin rather than treating them as independent phenomenological constructions.

现象学文献包含多种用于解释中微子振荡数据的中微子质量结构，但它们的理论起源通常看似不相关。这项工作旨在通过 $Δ(27)$ 味对称框架和 Type-I+II seesaw 机制，将这些可行结构统一在一个单一的最小框架内，展示它们的共同起源，而非将它们视为独立的现象学构造。

Method: The analysis employs a $Δ(27)$ discrete flavor symmetry framework combined with Type-I+II seesaw mechanisms. The method involves:
1. Constructing the minimal $Δ(27)$ particle content and symmetry assignments for leptons and scalars
2. Implementing both Type-I (right-handed neutrino) and Type-II (scalar triplet) seesaw mechanisms within this framework
3. Analyzing different vacuum alignment patterns for scalar fields that break $Δ(27)$ symmetry
4. Deriving neutrino mass matrices from the interplay between Yukawa couplings, vacuum alignments, and seesaw contributions
5. Mapping specific combinations of parameters to known neutrino mass textures from the literature

分析采用 $Δ(27)$ 离散味对称框架结合 Type-I+II seesaw 机制。方法包括：
1. 构建轻子和标量场的最小 $Δ(27)$ 粒子内容和对称性分配
2. 在该框架内同时实现 Type-I（右手中微子）和 Type-II（标量三重态）seesaw 机制
3. 分析破坏 $Δ(27)$ 对称性的标量场的不同真空对齐模式
4. 从 Yukawa 耦合、真空对齐和 seesaw 贡献之间的相互作用推导中微子质量矩阵
5. 将特定参数组合映射到文献中已知的中微子质量结构

Result: The analysis shows that:
1. The $Δ(27)$ framework naturally generates several established neutrino mass textures through specific vacuum alignment choices without additional model assumptions
2. Different vacuum alignments of $Δ(27)$ scalar fields lead to distinct neutrino mass matrix structures
3. The combination of Type-I and Type-II seesaw mechanisms within this framework provides sufficient freedom to reproduce viable textures while maintaining predictive power
4. Textures such as the two-zero texture patterns, democratic textures, and specific mixing patterns emerge naturally from different symmetry breaking patterns
5. The minimal model demonstrates how apparently disconnected phenomenological textures share a common origin in $Δ(27)$ flavor symmetry breaking

分析表明：
1. $Δ(27)$ 框架通过特定的真空对齐选择自然生成多种已建立的中微子质量结构，无需额外模型假设
2. $Δ(27)$ 标量场的不同真空对齐导致不同的中微子质量矩阵结构
3. 该框架内 Type-I 和 Type-II seesaw 机制的结合提供了足够的自由度来重现可行结构，同时保持预测能力
4. 诸如双零结构、民主结构以及特定混合模式等结构自然地从不同的对称性破缺模式中出现
5. 最小模型展示了看似不相关的现象学结构如何在 $Δ(27)$ 味对称破缺中共享共同起源

Conclusion: The $Δ(27)$ flavor symmetry framework provides a unifying theoretical origin for diverse neutrino mass textures found in phenomenological analyses. Through specific vacuum alignments and the interplay of Type-I+II seesaw mechanisms, the minimal setup naturally reproduces multiple viable textures without ad hoc assumptions, demonstrating their common foundation in discrete flavor symmetry breaking patterns. This approach offers a systematic way to classify neutrino mass textures based on their underlying symmetry structures.

$Δ(27)$ 味对称框架为现象学分析中发现的多种中微子质量结构提供了统一的理谕起源。通过特定的真空对齐以及 Type-I+II seesaw 机制的相互作用，最小设置自然重现了多个可行结构，无需特设假设，展示了它们在离散味对称破缺模式中的共同基础。这种方法提供了一种基于底层对称结构的系统方法来分类中微子质量结构。

Abstract: We plan to decipher the common origin of neutrino mass textures within a $Δ(27)$ based framework, in association with Type-I+II seesaw mechanism. Motivated by the diversity of texture structures used in phenomenological analyses, we examine how a single framework can reproduce them without additional assumptions. We show that the interplay between vacuum alignments, model parameters, and specific Yukawa choices naturally yields several well established neutrino mass textures in the literature. Our goal is to demonstrate that a minimal $Δ(27)$ framework can unify these viable textures within a common theoretical origin.

### [52] [Finite size effects on critical correlations in momentum space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16594)
*Athanasios Brofas,Fotios K. Diakonos*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Theoretical analysis of momentum-space baryon density correlations near the QCD critical end point, demonstrating how finite-size effects modify scaling behavior and establishing conditions for recovering infinite-volume scaling within experimental momentum ranges.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QCD critical end point (CEP) search is central to heavy-ion physics, with baryon-number fluctuations serving as key probe due to net-baryon density acting as effective order parameter near CEP. Critical dynamics exhibit long-range correlations and power-law scaling in real-space two-point function, but finite fireball size and lifetime impose cutoffs that regulate correlation length growth. These finite-size constraints substantially modify fluctuation structure in momentum space where measurements occur, necessitating theoretical analysis of momentum-space two-point correlation function for systems of finite spatial extent.

Method: Develop theoretical framework for momentum-space two-point correlation function $G(q)$ in finite-size systems near critical point. Employ field-theoretic approach with effective order parameter field $\phi(\mathbf{x}) \sim \delta n_B(\mathbf{x})$ representing baryon density fluctuations. Incorporate finite-size effects through boundary conditions or finite-volume integration. Derive scaling form $G(q) \sim q^{-2+\eta} F(q\xi, qL)$ where $\xi$ is correlation length, $L$ is system size, and $\eta$ is anomalous dimension. Analyze crossover between finite-size dominated regime ($qL \ll 1$) and infinite-volume scaling regime ($qL \gg 1$). Establish condition for recovering infinite-volume scaling exponent within experimentally accessible momentum range: must satisfy $1/\xi \ll q \ll 1/L$ simultaneously.

Result: Finite-size effects produce momentum-dependent effective scaling exponent $\eta_{\text{eff}}(qL)$ that interpolates between $\eta_{\text{eff}} \to \eta$ for $qL \gg 1$ (infinite-volume limit) and modified behavior for $qL \ll 1$. Scaling function $F(q\xi, qL)$ exhibits distinct regimes: (1) Critical regime: $G(q) \sim q^{-2+\eta}$ when $q\xi \gg 1$ and $qL \gg 1$; (2) Finite-size dominated regime: $G(q) \sim L^{2-\eta} g(qL)$ when $qL \ll 1$, where $g$ is universal scaling function; (3) Crossover region: complicated interpolation between limits. Experimental measurement of true critical exponent $\eta$ requires accessing momentum range satisfying $q_{\text{min}} > 1/L$ and $q_{\text{max}} < 1/\xi$ simultaneously, which imposes stringent constraints on fireball size $L$ and correlation length $\xi$ achievable in heavy-ion collisions.

Conclusion: Finite-size effects in heavy-ion collisions fundamentally alter momentum-space correlation structure near QCD critical point. Recovering infinite-volume critical scaling requires accessing intermediate momentum regime $1/L \ll q \ll 1/\xi$, presenting experimental challenge due to competing constraints on $L$ and $\xi$. This analysis provides quantitative framework for interpreting fluctuation measurements in finite systems and establishes necessary conditions for extracting true critical exponents from heavy-ion collision data. Results highlight importance of systematic finite-size scaling analysis in search for QCD critical end point.

Abstract: The search for the QCD critical end point (CEP) is a major objective of contemporary heavy-ion physics, motivating the study of fluctuation observables that are sensitive to critical dynamics. In particular, baryon-number fluctuations provide a natural probe because the net-baryon density can serve as an effective order parameter in the vicinity of the CEP. Near criticality, long-range correlations and power-law scaling are expected to emerge in the real-space two-point function of the baryon density, yet the finite size and finite lifetime of the fireball created in heavy-ion collisions impose intrinsic cutoffs that regulate the growth of the correlation length. These finite-size constraints significantly modify the observable structure of fluctuations, especially in momentum space, where experiments perform measurements. In this work we present a theoretical analysis of the momentum-space two-point correlation function for a system of finite spatial extent. We show that finite size effects lead to an effective scaling exponent which coincides with that of the infinitely extended system only in a prescribed scaling region within the experimentally accessible momentum range.

</details>


### [53] [Role of $Ξ(1690)$ in the $J/ψ\toΞ^0\barΛK^0$ reaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16640)
*Wen-Tao Lyu,Lian-Rong Dai,Eulogio Oset*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Analysis of $J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$ decay reveals crucial role of dynamically generated $Ξ(1690)$ resonance within chiral unitary approach, providing good description of invariant mass distributions and highlighting limitations of BESIII analysis.

对$J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$衰变的分析揭示了在幺正手征方法中动态生成的$Ξ(1690)$共振态的关键作用，为不变质量分布提供了良好描述，并突显了BESIII分析的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The BESIII collaboration recently measured the $J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$ decay process, but their analysis neglected the potential contributions from the $Ξ(1690)$ resonance. This work aims to investigate this decay by properly including both $Ξ(1690)$ and $Λ(1890)$ resonances, particularly focusing on the dynamically generated nature of $Ξ(1690)$ within the chiral unitary approach framework.

BESIII合作组最近测量了$J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$衰变过程，但他们的分析忽略了$Ξ(1690)$共振态的潜在贡献。本文旨在通过适当包含$Ξ(1690)$和$Λ(1890)$共振态来研究该衰变，特别关注幺正手征方法框架内$Ξ(1690)$的动态生成性质。

Method: The analysis employs the chiral unitary approach, where $Ξ(1690)$ is dynamically generated from $S$-wave pseudoscalar meson-octet baryon interactions. The theoretical framework incorporates contributions from both $Ξ(1690)$ and $Λ(1890)$ resonances to model the $J/ψ$ decay amplitude. Theoretical uncertainties are systematically evaluated using the parametric bootstrap method, which provides statistical confidence intervals for model predictions by resampling parameter distributions.

分析采用幺正手征方法，其中$Ξ(1690)$由$S$波赝标介子-八重态重子相互作用动态生成。理论框架包含$Ξ(1690)$和$Λ(1890)$共振态的贡献以模拟$J/ψ$衰变振幅。使用参数自助法系统评估理论不确定性，该方法通过对参数分布重新采样为模型预测提供统计置信区间。

Result: The theoretical model successfully describes three key invariant mass distributions: $\barΛK^0$, $Ξ^0 K^0$, and $\barΛΞ^0$. The results demonstrate that $Ξ(1690)$ plays a crucial role in the decay process, contrary to its omission in the BESIII experimental analysis. The parametric bootstrap method provides quantitative uncertainty estimates, reinforcing the robustness of the theoretical predictions. The analysis reveals that the $Ξ(1690)$ contribution is essential for understanding the observed distributions.

理论模型成功描述了三个关键的不变质量分布：$\barΛK^0$, $Ξ^0 K^0$, 和$\barΛΞ^0$。结果表明，与BESIII实验分析中的忽略相反，$Ξ(1690)$在衰变过程中起着关键作用。参数自助法提供了定量不确定性估计，增强了理论预测的稳健性。分析表明，$Ξ(1690)$的贡献对于理解观察到的分布至关重要。

Conclusion: This work establishes that $Ξ(1690)$, dynamically generated within the chiral unitary approach, is essential for explaining the $J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$ decay distributions. The theoretical framework successfully reproduces experimental data while highlighting limitations in the original BESIII analysis. Future high-precision measurements will further constrain the properties of both $Ξ(1690)$ and $Λ(1890)$ resonances, providing deeper insights into their nature and generation mechanisms.

这项工作确定，在幺正手征方法中动态生成的$Ξ(1690)$对于解释$J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$衰变分布至关重要。理论框架成功复现了实验数据，同时突显了原始BESIII分析的局限性。未来的高精度测量将进一步约束$Ξ(1690)$和$Λ(1890)$共振态的性质，为其本质和生成机制提供更深入的见解。

Abstract: Motivated by the recent BESIII measurements of the $J/ψ\to Ξ^0 \barΛK_S^0 + c.c.$ process, we investigate this reaction by considering the contributions from the $Ξ(1690)$ and $Λ(1890)$ resonances. The $Ξ(1690)$ state is dynamically generated from the $S$-wave pseudoscalar meson-octet baryon interactions within the chiral unitary approach. Our theoretical model provides a good description of the $\barΛK^0$, $Ξ^0 K^0$, and $\barΛΞ^0$ invariant mass distributions. The results indicate that the $Ξ(1690)$ resonance, which was neglected in the experimental analysis by BESIII, plays a crucial role in this process. Furthermore, we evaluate the theoretical uncertainties of our model using the parametric bootstrap method. Future high-precision measurements of this process will further help to elucidate the properties of the $Ξ(1690)$ and $Λ(1890)$ states.

### [54] [Spin entanglement signatures of proton from a light-front Hamiltonian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16681)
*Chen Qian,Siqi Xu,Yang-Guang Yang,Xingbo Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [Analysis compares quantum entanglement in proton spin structure between BLFQ (Basis Light-Front Quantization) approach and quark-diquark model, revealing quark-diquark yields substantially more entangled spin states due to larger W-type and Bell-type entanglement. BLFQ shows evolution toward effective quark-diquark configuration with stronger coupling.]

\n\n
[分析比较了BLFQ（基矢光前量子化）方法和夸克-双夸克模型中质子自旋结构的量子纠缠，揭示夸克-双夸克模型产生显著更纠缠的自旋态，这主要源于更大的W型和贝尔型纠缠。BLFQ显示在更强耦合下向有效夸克-双夸克构型演化。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Quantum entanglement provides a quantitative probe of internal hadron structure and quantum correlations in hadron wave functions. For baryons, the spin state of three valence quarks forms a tripartite qubit system whose entanglement structure can be characterized by four classes of three-qubit states. The paper aims to compare proton spin entanglement from Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) with that from a quark-diquark model to understand fundamental differences in entanglement structure and correlation patterns.]

\n\n
[量子纠缠为强子内部结构和强子波函数中的量子关联提供了定量探针。对于重子，三个价夸克的自旋态构成一个三方量子比特系统，其纠缠结构可用四类三量子比特态来表征。本文旨在比较基矢光前量子化（BLFQ）方法与夸克-双夸克模型中质子自旋纠缠，以理解纠缠结构和关联模式的基本差异。]

Method: [The study analyzes both bipartite and tripartite entanglement measures for the proton spin state. For the quark-diquark model, it treats the proton as a composite of a quark and diquark with prescribed wave functions. For BLFQ, it uses light-front quantum field theory framework with Hamiltonian diagonalization in a truncated Fock space basis. The entanglement is quantified using appropriate quantum information measures for three-qubit systems (e.g., concurrence, tangle, negativity). The analysis focuses on the valence Fock sector and investigates how entanglement evolves with coupling strength and quark mass parameters within BLFQ.]

\n\n
[该研究分析了质子自旋态的双部纠缠和三相纠缠度量。对于夸克-双夸克模型，将质子处理为具有特定波函数的夸克和双夸克复合体。对于BLFQ，采用光前量子场论框架，在截断的福克空间基矢中对角化哈密顿量。纠缠使用适当的三量子比特系统量子信息度量（如并发度、纠缠度、负性度）进行量化。分析聚焦于价福克扇区，并研究BLFQ中纠缠如何随耦合强度和夸克质量参数演化。]

Result: [1. The quark-diquark model yields substantially more entangled spin states than BLFQ wave functions in the valence Fock sector. 2. The difference mainly originates from larger W-type and Bell-type entanglement in the quark-diquark model. 3. Within BLFQ, larger coupling constant and smaller quark mass drive the spin correlation among valence quarks toward an effective quark-diquark configuration with an active $d$ quark and a correlated $uu$ pair. 4. The entanglement structure in BLFQ shows parametric evolution that can be tuned toward quark-diquark-like patterns with appropriate parameters.]

\n\n
[1. 夸克-双夸克模型在价福克扇区中产生比BLFQ波函数显著更纠缠的自旋态。2. 这种差异主要源于夸克-双夸克模型中更大的W型和贝尔型纠缠。3. 在BLFQ内，更大的耦合常数和更小的夸克质量将价夸克间的自旋关联驱动向具有活跃$d$夸克和相关$uu$对的有效夸克-双夸克构型。4. BLFQ中的纠缠结构显示参数演化，可通过适当参数调整向类夸克-双夸克模式转变。]

Conclusion: [The analysis reveals fundamental differences in entanglement structure between the quark-diquark model and BLFQ approach to proton structure. The quark-diquark model's more entangled spin states suggest stronger quantum correlations among valence quarks in that phenomenological picture. Within the BLFQ framework, the evolution toward quark-diquark-like configurations with increasing coupling and decreasing quark mass indicates that entanglement measures can serve as sensitive probes of the underlying dynamics and confinement mechanisms in QCD. The study demonstrates how quantum information concepts provide new quantitative tools for distinguishing between different theoretical approaches to hadron structure.]

\n\n
[分析揭示了夸克-双夸克模型与BLFQ方法在质子结构上纠缠结构的基本差异。夸克-双夸克模型中更纠缠的自旋态表明该唯象图景中价夸克间更强的量子关联。在BLFQ框架内，随着耦合增加和夸克质量减小而向类夸克-双夸克构型的演化表明，纠缠度量可作为QCD中基础动力学和禁闭机制的敏感探针。该研究展示了量子信息概念如何为区分不同强子结构理论方法提供新的定量工具。]

Abstract: Quantum entanglement provides a quantitative probe of the internal structure of hadrons and offers a sensitive means to study the quantum correlation in the hadron wave functions. For baryons, the spin state of the three valence quarks forms a tripartite qubit system, whose entanglement structure can be characterized by the four classes of three-qubit states. In this work, we compare the proton spin entanglement obtained from Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) with that from a quark-diquark model. By analyzing both bipartite and tripartite entanglement, we find that the quark-diquark model yields a substantially more entangled spin state than the BLFQ wave function in the valence Fock sector. This difference mainly originates from the larger W-type and Bell-type entanglement in the quark-diquark model. Within BLFQ, larger stronger coupling constant and smaller quark mass drive the spin correlation among the valence quarks towards an effective quark-diquark configuration with an active $d$ quark and a correlated $uu$ pair.

### [55] [On the survival of strong nuggets in the early Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16686)
*Haoyang Qi,Wen-Li Yuan,Yudong Luo,Chao Chen,Shi Pi,Renxin Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Survival of primordial strange quark nuggets (A∼10^{10-30}) as dark matter through strangeon matter phase transition, evading early Universe evaporation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The paper addresses the cosmological survival problem of primordial quark nuggets as dark matter candidates. In standard scenarios, quark nuggets formed during the QCD phase transition would evaporate due to weak interactions in the early Universe. The authors propose that a subsequent phase transition to strangeon matter (a more stable configuration of strange quark matter) could allow nuggets with baryon number A∼10^{10-30} to survive, making them viable dark matter candidates within the Standard Model framework without requiring new particles.]

本文探讨了原始夸克块作为暗物质候选者的宇宙学存活问题。在标准情景中，量子色动力学相变期间形成的夸克块会在早期宇宙中由于弱相互作用而蒸发。作者提出，随后向奇异子物质（一种更稳定的奇异夸克物质构型）的相变可以使重子数 A∼10^{10-30} 的块得以存活，使它们成为标准模型框架内可行的暗物质候选者，而无需引入新粒子。

Method: [The authors formulate the cosmic phase transition sequence: first-order QCD phase transition producing strange quark nuggets, followed by a transition to strangeon matter. They construct the equation of state for both phases and compute the stability criteria. The analysis incorporates cosmological constraints including the dark-to-luminous matter ratio Ω_D/Ω_B, mass-radius relations from compact object observations, and tidal deformability measurements from gravitational wave events. They establish a parameter space where strangeon nuggets survive evaporation and satisfy all observational constraints.]

作者构建了宇宙相变序列：产生奇异夸克块的一阶量子色动力学相变，随后向奇异子物质的转变。他们构建了两种物态的物态方程并计算了稳定性判据。该分析包含了宇宙学约束，包括暗物质-可见物质比例 Ω_D/Ω_B、来自致密天体观测的质量-半径关系以及来自引力波事件的潮汐形变测量。他们建立了一个参数空间，其中奇异子块能够存活并满足所有观测约束。

Result: [The analysis identifies a viable parameter space where strangeon nuggets with baryon number A∼10^{10-30} can survive cosmic evolution. The strangeon phase transition provides sufficient stabilization against weak decay, allowing nuggets to evade evaporation in the early Universe. The model accommodates the observed dark matter abundance with Ω_D/Ω_B∼5 and satisfies constraints from compact object mass-radius relations and tidal deformability measurements from binary neutron star mergers (GW170817).]

分析确定了一个可行的参数空间，其中重子数 A∼10^{10-30} 的奇异子块能够在宇宙演化中存活。奇异子相变提供了足够的稳定性以抵抗弱衰变，使块能够避免在早期宇宙中蒸发。该模型与观测到的暗物质丰度 Ω_D/Ω_B∼5 相符，并满足来自致密天体质量-半径关系和双中子星合并（GW170817）潮汐形变测量的约束。

Conclusion: [Strangeon nuggets represent a viable dark matter candidate within the Standard Model that survives cosmic evolution through a stabilizing phase transition. The model naturally explains the observed dark-to-luminous matter ratio and satisfies astrophysical constraints from compact object observations. This provides a novel mechanism for dark matter formation without requiring new fundamental particles or extensions to the Standard Model.]

奇异子块代表了一种在标准模型内可行的暗物质候选者，通过稳定化相变在宇宙演化中存活下来。该模型自然地解释了观测到的暗物质-可见物质比例，并满足来自致密天体观测的天体物理约束。这为暗物质形成提供了一种新颖的机制，无需引入新的基本粒子或对标准模型进行扩展。

Abstract: Strong nuggets with a baryon number of $A\sim 10^{10-30}$ could be able to survive from the cosmic separation of the QCD phases, provided the transition from strange quark matter to strangeon matter is accounted for, thereby evading evaporation in the early Universe. Such strangeon nuggets may serve as a dark matter candidate within particle standard model. We formulate the corresponding phase transition of cosmic strange matter, establishing a parameter space which reasonably accommodates observational constraints on the dark-to-luminous matter ratio and the mass-radius relation, as well as tidal deformability of compact objects.

### [56] [New benchmarks for direct detection of freeze-in dark matter in vector portal models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16863)
*David Cerdeño,Patrick Foldenauer,Rafael López Noé,Óscar Zapata*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [The paper investigates MeV-scale fermionic dark matter freeze-in production via vector mediators in scenarios with low reheating temperatures, analyzing detectability through electron and nuclear recoils in direct detection experiments and solar neutrino coherent scattering signals for various anomaly-free gauge extensions ($U(1)_D$, $U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$, $U(1)_{B-L}$).]

[本文研究通过矢量介质在低再加热温度情景下产生MeV尺度费米子暗物质的冻结机制，分析各种异常规范扩展（$U(1)_D$、$U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$、$U(1)_{B-L}$）下，通过直接探测实验中的电子反冲和核反冲以及太阳中微子相干散射信号的可探测性。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation is to explore the discovery potential of future direct detection experiments for MeV-scale fermionic dark matter produced via freeze-in with low reheating temperatures, where traditional WIMP searches are less sensitive. The study addresses the interplay between dark matter and neutrino sectors in anomaly-free gauge extensions, examining how experimental constraints from electron recoil data can be circumvented and identifying regions of parameter space accessible to next-generation detectors through both dark matter and neutrino scattering signals.]

[研究动机是探索未来直接探测实验对通过低再加热温度下冻结机制产生的MeV尺度费米子暗物质的发现潜力，传统WIMP搜索对此类质量区间的灵敏度较低。本研究处理异常规范扩展中暗物质与中微子部门的相互作用，研究如何规避电子反冲数据的实验限制，并通过暗物质和中微子散射信号识别下一代探测器可访问的参数空间区域。]

Method: [The method employs analytical calculations of freeze-in dark matter production rates in the low-reheating-temperature regime, considering various gauge structures: (1) minimal kinetic mixing dark photon of secluded $U(1)_D$, (2) gauge bosons of anomaly-free $U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$ (with $i,j=e,μ,τ$), and (3) $U(1)_{B-L}$ gauge extensions. The analysis computes DM relic abundance constraints, applies current experimental bounds from DAMIC-M and PandaX-4T electron recoil data, and projects sensitivity of future detectors. For nuclear recoil signatures, the study calculates scattering cross sections for massive dark photon scenarios. For neutrino sector signatures, it analyzes enhanced coherent scattering of solar neutrinos mediated by the new gauge bosons.]

[该方法采用低再加热温度区域下冻结暗物质产生率的解析计算，考虑各种规范结构：(1) 隔离$U(1)_D$的最小动能混合暗光子，(2) 异常自由$U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$的规范玻色子（$i,j=e,μ,τ$），(3) $U(1)_{B-L}$规范扩展。分析计算了暗物质遗迹丰度约束，应用了DAMIC-M和PandaX-4T电子反冲数据的当前实验界限，并预测了未来探测器的灵敏度。对于核反冲信号，研究计算了大质量暗光子情景的散射截面。对于中微子部门信号，分析了新规范玻色子介导的太阳中微子相干散射增强。]

Result: [Key results include: (1) For ultralight dark photons, current electron recoil constraints from DAMIC-M and PandaX-4T can be avoided if DM constitutes less than 40% of total cold DM, with future detectors potentially sensitive to sub-1% fractions for masses >1 MeV. (2) For massive dark photons, allowed parameter space exists for 50 MeV $\lesssim m_{\rm DM}\lesssim$ 500 MeV that could be detectable via nuclear recoils in direct detection experiments, particularly with low reheating temperatures. (3) For $U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$ and $U(1)_{B-L}$ extensions, freeze-in at low reheating temperatures can reproduce observed DM abundance with gauge couplings up to $g_X\sim10^{-2}$ for MeV-scale DM. Direct detection experiments can probe significant portions of this parameter space through nuclear recoils in the 50-500 MeV mass range. Additionally, enhanced solar neutrino coherent scattering signals provide complementary discovery channels and model discrimination capability.]

[关键结果包括：(1) 对于超轻暗光子，如果暗物质占总冷暗物质的比例小于40%，可以规避DAMIC-M和PandaX-4T的当前电子反冲限制，未来探测器可能对质量>1 MeV的亚1%比例敏感。(2) 对于大质量暗光子，存在50 MeV $\lesssim m_{\rm DM}\lesssim$ 500 MeV范围内的允许参数空间，可通过直接探测实验中的核反冲探测，特别是在低再加热温度下。(3) 对于$U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$和$U(1)_{B-L}$扩展，低再加热温度下的冻结机制可以重现观测到的暗物质丰度，对于MeV尺度暗物质，规范耦合可达$g_X\sim10^{-2}$。直接探测实验可以通过50-500 MeV质量范围内的核反冲探测该参数空间的显著部分。此外，增强的太阳中微子相干散射信号提供了互补的发现通道和模型区分能力。]

Conclusion: [The study demonstrates that MeV-scale fermionic dark matter from freeze-in production with low reheating temperatures offers promising discovery prospects for future direct detection experiments through both dark matter scattering and enhanced neutrino interactions. The interplay between dark matter and neutrino sectors in anomaly-free gauge extensions creates multiple experimental handles: electron recoils for ultralight mediators, nuclear recoils for massive mediators (50-500 MeV), and coherent scattering of solar neutrinos. These signals provide complementary avenues to probe the underlying gauge structure and distinguish between different theoretical scenarios.]

[研究表明，低再加热温度下冻结机制产生的MeV尺度费米子暗物质为未来直接探测实验提供了有前景的发现前景，通过暗物质散射和增强的中微子相互作用。异常规范扩展中暗物质与中微子部门的相互作用创造了多个实验切入点：超轻介质的电子反冲，大质量介质（50-500 MeV）的核反冲，以及太阳中微子的相干散射。这些信号提供了探测底层规范结构并区分不同理论情景的互补途径。]

Abstract: We investigate the freeze-in of MeV-scale fermionic dark matter (DM) that couples to the Standard Model via a new vector mediator to assess the potential that future direct detection experiments have to observe new physics in either the DM or neutrino sectors. We study the minimal kinetic mixing dark photon of a secluded $U(1)_D$ as well as gauge bosons of the anomaly-free $U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$, with $i,j=e,μ,τ$, and $U(1)_{B-L}$ gauge extensions, exploring the impact of low reheating temperatures on the DM production rates. For the ultralight dark photon scenario, we show that current experimental constraints from electron recoil data in DAMIC-M and PandaX-4T can be avoided if the DM fermion is only a subcomponent (smaller than 40%) of the total cold DM and that future detectors can be sensitive to a DM fraction below 1% for masses above 1 MeV. For a massive dark photon, there are allowed regions of the parameter space with masses in the range 50 MeV $\lesssim m_{\rm DM}\lesssim$ 500 MeV that can be within the reach of direct detection experiments through nuclear recoils if freeze-in occurred at a low reheating temperature. Finally, the case of $U(1)_{L_i-L_j}$ and $U(1)_{B-L}$ is particularly interesting since the discovery of new physics can come from either the DM or the neutrino sector, which features new interactions. We find that freeze-in at low reheating temperatures can reproduce the observed abundance in large parts of the parameter space up to gauge couplings of $g_X\sim10^{-2}$ for MeV DM. Most notably, direct detection experiments will be sensitive to considerable parts of this parameter space in nuclear recoils for 50 MeV $\lesssim m_{\rm DM}\lesssim$ 500 MeV. Additionally, the enhanced signal from solar neutrino coherent scattering is observable in these scenarios, which can serve as a further handle to identify the underlying particle physics model.

</details>


### [57] [Prospects for precision CE$ν$NS measurements with electron-capture neutrinos and lithium-based bolometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16740)
*Giovanni Benato,Francesca M. Pofi,Andrei Puiu,Christoph A. Ternes*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Proposal for high-precision CEνNS measurements using mono-energetic neutrinos from electron-capture decays with compact lithium fluoride bolometric detector arrays, aiming for ~3% flux determination precision to resolve the gallium anomaly.

利用电子俘获衰变产生的单能中微子进行高精度相干弹性中微子-原子核散射测量的方案，采用紧凑型氟化锂量热探测器阵列，目标达到约3%的中微子通量测定精度以解决镓异常问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The gallium anomaly in neutrino physics requires precise measurements of electron-capture neutrino flux to disentangle nuclear effects from source activity miscalibrations or short-baseline oscillations. Current limitations in flux determination precision hinder resolution of this discrepancy.

中微子物理中的镓异常问题需要精确测量电子俘获中微子通量，以区分核效应与源活度校准误差或短基线振荡。当前通量测定精度的限制阻碍了这一差异的解决。

Method: Uses intense radioactive electron-capture sources ($^{51}$Cr or $^{37}$Ar) providing mono-energetic neutrinos. Employs compact arrays of bolometric detectors with light-element absorbers (LiF, Li, O, F) optimized for low-energy detection. Assumes 1 kg LiF detector mass, source activities of $\sim10^{17}$ Bq, and energy threshold of 20 eV, with 90-day measurement duration.

使用强放射性电子俘获源（$^{51}$Cr或$^{37}$Ar）提供单能中微子。采用轻元素吸收体（LiF、Li、O、F）的紧凑型量热探测器阵列，针对低能探测优化。假设1 kg LiF探测器质量，$\sim10^{17}$ Bq源活度，20 eV能量阈值，测量持续90天。

Result: With the proposed setup, a $\sim 3\%$ precision on neutrino flux determination is achievable. This precision enables tests of the gallium anomaly by separating nuclear effects in gallium detectors from potential source activity miscalibrations or short-baseline neutrino oscillation contributions.

采用所提方案，可实现约3%的中微子通量测定精度。该精度能够通过区分镓探测器中的核效应与潜在源活度校准误差或短基线中微子振荡贡献，从而检验镓异常。

Conclusion: Electron-capture sources combined with compact bolometric arrays using light-element absorbers represent a viable path to high-precision coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering measurements. The achievable precision offers a clean method to resolve the gallium anomaly's origin.

电子俘获源结合轻元素吸收体的紧凑型量热探测器阵列，为高精度相干弹性中微子-原子核散射测量提供了可行路径。可达到的精度为解析镓异常根源提供了清晰方法。

Abstract: We evaluate the feasibility of high-precision coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering measurements exploiting mono-energetic neutrinos produced by electron-capture (EC) decays of intense radioactive sources, such as $^{51}$Cr or $^{37}$Ar. To fully exploit the high neutrino flux achievable with EC sources, and accounting for the low energy of EC neutrinos, we evaluate the sensitivity of a compact array of bolometric detectors with absorbers based on light elements, such as lithium, oxygen and fluorine. With 1 kg of LiF detectors, source activities of $\sim10^{17}$ Bq, and assuming an energy threshold of 20 eV, we expect to achieve a $\sim 3\%$ precision on the determination of the neutrino flux with 90 days of measurement. Such a measurement would represent a test of the gallium neutrino anomaly, and could disentangle nuclear effects on gallium from the misevaluation of the EC source activity or short-baseline neutrino oscillations.

### [58] [Exact Path Integral Methods in Supersymmetric $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15730)
*Alberto Castellano,Carmine Montella,Matteo Zatti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We compute exact 1-loop determinants for charged spin-0 and spin-1/2 fields in AdS₂×S² with background electromagnetic fields, revealing their functional form via Schwinger proper-time methods. Specializing to supersymmetric BPS backgrounds yields quantum corrections to black hole partition functions, connecting to Gopakumar-Vafa invariants.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The partition function of supersymmetric black holes in N=2 supergravity receives quantum corrections from matter fluctuations around BPS backgrounds. Computing these requires precise knowledge of 1-loop determinants in curved spacetime with electromagnetic fluxes, particularly near black hole horizons where geometry becomes AdS₂×S². Establishing exact results for functional determinants enables systematic evaluation of quantum black hole entropy.

Method: Using Schwinger proper-time formalism in constant background field approximation, we derive exact non-perturbative expressions for functional determinants of charged massive scalars and fermions in AdS₂×S² with electromagnetic fields. We implement zeta-function regularization and heat kernel techniques to handle curved spacetime effects, then specialize to supersymmetric BPS backgrounds satisfying attractor equations in 4d N=2 supergravity.

Result: Obtained closed-form expressions for functional determinants $\\det(-D^2 + m^2)$ and $\\det(i\\slashed{D} + m)$ in AdS₂×S² with constant electromagnetic fluxes. Derived the complete 1-loop effective action for N=2 BPS hypermultiplet in near-horizon black hole geometry, providing exact quantum corrections to black hole partition function. Established connection between these determinants and Gopakumar-Vafa integral representation through analytic continuation.

Conclusion: Exact functional determinants for matter fields in AdS₂×S² backgrounds provide crucial ingredients for computing quantum-corrected black hole partition functions in N=2 supergravity. The Schwinger proper-time approach yields non-perturbative results valid beyond perturbation theory, enabling systematic study of black hole microstate counting beyond semi-classical approximations and connecting to topological string invariants.

Abstract: We determine the exact functional determinants of charged, massive spin-0 and spin-$\frac12$ particles in $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ backgrounds threaded by constant electric and magnetic fields. This is achieved using Schwinger proper-time formalism, which allows us to derive the full non-perturbative effective action in the 1-loop and constant background field approximations. We then specialize the computation to supersymmetric settings and we obtain the effective action for a 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ BPS massive hypermultiplet in a supersymmetric $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ spacetime. This setup can be seen to be equivalent to the near-horizon geometry of a BPS black hole which solves the attractor equations of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ supergravity. Our results provide a necessary intermediate step for the evaluation of the quantum-corrected black hole partition function. We also comment on the relation with the celebrated Gopakumar-Vafa integral representation.

### [59] [Zooming out of AdS$_4 \times$S$^2 \times$S$^2$: The Branes behind the CFT's](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15731)
*Iosif Bena,Antoine Bourget,Raphaël Dulac,Dimitrios Toulikas,Nicholas P. Warner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This work reveals supersymmetric brane configurations giving AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$ solutions, dual to 3D $N=4$ CFTs or 4D $N=4$ SYM interfaces/domain walls. They show these preserve same Killing spinors as orthogonal D3-D5-NS5 systems and track from weak coupling to supergravity, explaining how AdS$_4$ emerges from self-similar bending regions. The geometric construction clarifies Gaiotto-Witten's "good-bad-ugly" classification.

这项工作揭示了产生AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$解的超对称膜构型，这些解对偶于三维$N=4$ CFT或四维$N=4$ SYM的共形边界和畴壁。他们证明这些解与平坦时空中的正交D3-D5-NS5膜系统保持相同的Killing旋子，并从弱耦合追踪到超引力，解释AdS$_4$如何从自相似弯曲区域涌现。几何构造阐明了Gaiotto-Witten的"好-坏-丑"分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To provide explicit holographic duals for three-dimensional $N=4$ conformal field theories and interfaces/domain walls in four-dimensional $N=4$ super Yang-Mills theory. The AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$ supergravity solutions serve as these duals, but their precise brane engineering origins needed clarification. Understanding how these geometries emerge from string theory brane configurations is crucial for connecting weak-coupling gauge theory descriptions to strongly coupled gravitational duals.

为三维$N=4$共形场论和四维$N=4$超杨-米尔斯理论中的界面/畴壁提供显式的全息对偶。AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S^2$超引力解充当这些对偶，但它们的精确膜工程起源需要澄清。理解这些几何如何从弦理论的膜构型中涌现对于连接弱耦合规范理论描述和强耦合引力对偶至关重要。

Method: The authors identify supersymmetric brane configurations in flat space that preserve the same Killing spinors as the target AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$ solutions. These involve orthogonal D3, D5, and NS5 branes. They track the solutions from the weak-coupling regime (where branes don't backreact) to the supergravity regime, showing how the geometry emerges. Key innovations include: 1) Demonstrating that singular sources correspond to semi-infinite D3-D5 and D3-NS5 spikes; 2) Proving the AdS$_4$ factor arises from universal self-similar bending regions of the five-branes, with steepness matching weak-coupling linking numbers; 3) Providing a brane configuration for Janus interface solutions.

作者识别了平坦时空中的超对称膜构型，这些构型保持与目标AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$解相同的Killing旋子。这些涉及正交的D3、D5和NS5膜。他们从弱耦合区域（膜不产生反作用）追踪到超引力区域，展示几何如何涌现。关键创新包括：1)证明奇异源对应于半无限D3-D5和D3-NS5尖峰；2)证明AdS$_4$因子源于五维膜的普适自相似弯曲区域，其陡峭度匹配弱耦合linking数；3)为Janus界面解提供膜构型。

Result: 1) Identified explicit brane configurations yielding AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$ solutions with holographic duals to 3D $N=4$ CFTs and 4D $N=4$ SYM interfaces/domain walls. 2) Showed these preserve identical Killing spinors to orthogonal D3-D5-NS5 systems in flat space. 3) Demonstrated singular sources correspond to semi-infinite D3-D5 and D3-NS5 spikes. 4) Traced the geometric transition from weak coupling to supergravity, proving the AdS$_4$ emerges from self-similar bending regions of five-branes where bending steepness equals weak-coupling linking numbers. 5) Proposed brane engineering for Janus interfaces. 6) Provided geometric interpretation of Gaiotto-Witten classification: only "good" theories have five-branes that avoid crossing when back-reacting, sourcing AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$.

1) 识别了产生AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$解的显式膜构型，这些解全息对偶于三维$N=4$ CFT和四维$N=4$ SYM界面/畴壁。2) 证明这些解保持与平坦时空中正交D3-D5-NS5系统相同的Killing旋子。3) 证明奇异源对应于半无限D3-D5和D3-NS5尖峰。4) 追踪了从弱耦合到超引力的几何转变，证明AdS$_4$从五维膜的自相似弯曲区域涌现，其中弯曲陡峭度等于弱耦合linking数。5) 提出了Janus界面的膜工程。6) 为Gaiotto-Witten分类提供了几何解释：只有"好"理论在反作用时不发生五维膜交叉，从而产生AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a comprehensive brane engineering framework for AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$ supergravity solutions and their holographic duals. The geometric construction naturally explains the emergence of AdS factor from self-similar bending of five-branes, connecting linking numbers (weak-coupling gauge theory parameters) to geometric properties in the strongly coupled regime. Most significantly, it provides a clear geometric criterion distinguishing Gaiotto-Witten's "good," "bad," and "ugly" $N=4$ theories: only "good" theories avoid five-brane crossing during back-reaction and successfully generate the desired holographic geometry. This bridges string theory brane constructions with supergravity solutions and gauge theory classifications.

本文为AdS$_4\times$S^2\times$S^2$超引力解及其全息对偶建立了一个全面的膜工程框架。几何构造自然地解释了AdS因子如何从五维膜的自相似弯曲中涌现，将linking数（弱耦合规范理论参数）与强耦合区域的几何性质联系起来。最重要的是，它提供了区分Gaiotto-Witten"好"、"坏"和"丑"$N=4$理论的清晰几何判据：只有"好"理论在反作用时避免五维膜交叉，成功产生所需的全息几何。这连接了弦理论的膜构造、超引力解和规范理论分类。

Abstract: We reveal the supersymmetric brane configurations that give rise to AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$ supergravity solutions, which are holographic duals to three-dimensional $N=4$ CFTs or to conformal boundaries and domain walls of four-dimensional $N=4$ SYM. We show that these solutions preserve the same Killing spinors as orthogonal D3, D5 and NS5 branes in flat space, and that the singular sources of these solutions correspond to semi-infinite D3-D5 and D3-NS5 spikes.
  We track these solutions all the way from the weak-coupling regime of parameters, where the branes do not backreact, to the supergravity regime. We explain how the AdS$_4$ factor arises from certain universal self-similar bending regions of the five-branes, whose steepness is the same as the weak-coupling linking numbers. We also propose a brane configuration that gives rise to the Janus interface solutions.
  Our construction gives a clear geometric explanation of the Gaiotto-Witten "good-bad-ugly" classification of eight-supercharge theories: only good theories have five-branes that do not cross when back-reacting, and end up sourcing an AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$ solution.

*Yoav Zigdon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Worldsheet CFT approach constructs string-scale wormholes beyond supergravity, showing strongly coupled CFTs describe Euclidean wormholes/double cones/ER bridges, with conformal manifold mediating closed Universe-wormhole transitions.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To extend beyond supergravity limitations by constructing wormhole solutions with throat sizes comparable to string scale, requiring worldsheet CFT framework for proper string-theoretic description of wormhole geometries including Euclidean wormholes, double cones, and Einstein-Rosen bridges.
