Abstract: I provide multiple examples of conformal field theories (CFTs) on the worldsheet that describe string propagation in target space wormholes connecting two disjoint asymptotic manifolds. The worldsheet approach goes beyond the framework of supergravity by incorporating wormholes for which the size of the throat is comparable to the string scale. Typically, strongly coupled CFTs describe these stringy wormholes, which include Euclidean wormholes, double cones, and Einstein-Rosen bridges. Finally, I interpret a conformal manifold that contains $\text{SU}(2)_k$ and $\big(\text{SU}(2)_k \times \text{U}(1)_{k'}\big)/\text{U}(1)$ CFTs as mediating a transition between a closed Universe and a wormhole.

### [61] [Negative running of gravitational positivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15755)
*J. Fernandez,M. Ruhdorfer,J. Serra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We demonstrate that one-loop renormalization group evolution in 4D effective field theories of shift-symmetric scalars, photons, and gravitons reveals negative running of Wilson coefficients for certain non-minimal three-point interactions, with beta-functions suppressed by the Planck scale. This negative infrared behavior, combined with positive contributions from graviton loops (when smeared over momentum transfer), leads to constraints on the number of non-minimally coupled particles via the species bound.

我们证明了在4维有效场论中，对于具有平移对称性的标量、光子和引力子，特定非最小三点相互作用会导致Wilson系数的负跑动，其β函数受到普朗克尺度的抑制。这种负的红外行为与引力子圈的正贡献（在动量传递上平均后）相结合，通过物种界限对非最小耦合粒子数量产生了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding quantum corrections in effective field theories (EFTs) of massless particles with shift symmetries, which naturally appear in the infrared description of various physical systems. Specifically, we aim to analyze how non-minimal interactions in these theories (scalars, photons, gravitons) evolve under the renormalization group (RG) and to determine the implications for positivity bounds derived from dispersion relations. The interplay between negative running from non-minimal couplings and positive contributions from graviton loops is crucial for establishing consistency conditions of the EFT.

研究动机源于理解具有平移对称性的无质量粒子有效场论（EFT）中的量子修正，这些理论自然出现在各种物理系统的红外描述中。具体来说，我们旨在分析这些理论（标量、光子、引力子）中的非最小相互作用如何在重整化群（RG）下演化，并确定其对色散关系导出的正定性界限的影响。非最小耦合引起的负跑动与引力子圈正贡献之间的相互作用对于建立EFT的一致性条件至关重要。

Method: We employ one-loop renormalization group techniques in four-dimensional effective field theories. The analysis focuses on the leading operators in the EFTs of shift-symmetric scalars, photons, and gravitons. We compute the beta-functions for Wilson coefficients of non-minimal three-point interactions. The gravitational contributions are systematically included via graviton loops. To properly compare the negative running with positive infrared contributions, we employ momentum transfer smearing techniques. The final constraints are derived by imposing consistency with the species bound, which limits the number of non-minimally coupled particles.

我们采用四维有效场论中的单圈重整化群技术。分析重点集中在具有平移对称性的标量、光子和引力子EFT中的主导算符上。我们计算了非最小三点相互作用的Wilson系数的β函数。通过引力子圈系统地包含了引力贡献。为了正确比较负跑动与正的红外贡献，我们采用了动量传递平均技术。最终约束是通过施加与物种界限的一致性导出的，该界限限制了非最小耦合粒子的数量。

Result: 1. Negative running of Wilson coefficients: Certain non-minimal three-point interactions in shift-symmetric scalar, photon, and graviton EFTs induce negative running of the corresponding Wilson coefficients under RG flow toward the infrared. The beta-functions are suppressed by the Planck scale $M_{Pl}$, scaling as $\\beta \\sim g^2 / M_{Pl}^2$ where $g$ is the coupling constant.

2. Graviton loop contributions: Gravitational interactions generate positive infrared contributions that compete with the negative running. After smearing over momentum transfer, these positive contributions dominate provided the number of non-minimally coupled particles $N$ satisfies $N \\lesssim M_{Pl}/\\Lambda$, where $\\Lambda$ is the EFT cutoff.

3. Species bound constraint: The analysis yields a constraint on the number of non-minimally coupled particles consistent with the species bound: $N \\leq M_{Pl}/\\Lambda$. This ensures that the positive gravitational contributions overcome the negative running, maintaining consistency with positivity bounds from dispersion relations.

1. Wilson系数的负跑动：在具有平移对称性的标量、光子和引力子EFT中，特定非最小三点相互作用会导致相应Wilson系数在朝向红外方向的重整化群流下产生负跑动。β函数受到普朗克尺度$M_{Pl}$的抑制，按$\\beta \\sim g^2 / M_{Pl}^2$的比例缩放，其中$g$是耦合常数。

2. 引力子圈贡献：引力相互作用产生正的红外贡献，与负跑动竞争。在动量传递上平均后，只要非最小耦合粒子数$N$满足$N \\lesssim M_{Pl}/\\Lambda$（其中$\\Lambda$是EFT截断），这些正贡献就会占主导。

3. 物种界限约束：分析得出了与非最小耦合粒子数量相关的约束，与物种界限一致：$N \\leq M_{Pl}/\\Lambda$。这确保了正的引力贡献克服负跑动，保持了与色散关系正定性界限的一致性。

Conclusion: The one-loop renormalization group analysis reveals a non-trivial interplay between non-minimal interactions and gravitational loops in shift-symmetric effective field theories. The negative running of Wilson coefficients for certain three-point interactions, suppressed by the Planck scale, must be balanced against positive infrared contributions from graviton loops. After momentum smearing, gravitational positivity dominates only when the number of non-minimally coupled particles respects the species bound. This work demonstrates how gravitational quantum corrections can impose constraints on particle content in EFTs and highlights the importance of including gravitational effects even when suppressed by $M_{Pl}$, as they can qualitatively alter the RG flow and positivity bounds.

单圈重整化群分析揭示了在具有平移对称性的有效场论中，非最小相互作用与引力子圈之间存在非平凡的相互作用。特定三点相互作用的Wilson系数的负跑动（受到普朗克尺度的抑制）必须与引力子圈的正红外贡献相平衡。经过动量平均后，只有当非最小耦合粒子数量遵守物种界限时，引力的正定性才会占主导。这项工作展示了引力量子修正如何对EFT中的粒子内容施加约束，并强调了即使受到$M_{Pl}$抑制，包含引力效应的重要性，因为它们可以定性地改变重整化群流和正定性界限。

Abstract: We investigate the one-loop renormalization group evolution in four dimensions of the leading operators in the effective field theories of shift-symmetric scalars, photons, and gravitons. We show that certain non-minimal three-point interactions induce a negative running of the corresponding Wilson coefficients, with beta-functions suppressed by the Planck scale. The decrease of the coefficients toward the infrared prompts us to revisit their dispersive bounds, in particular accounting for graviton loops. Gravitational interactions generate positive infrared contributions which, after smearing over the momentum transfer, are argued to dominated over the negative running, provided the number of non-minimally coupled particles is bounded from above according to the species bound.

</details>


### [62] [Formalization of QFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15770)
*Michael R. Douglas,Sarah Hoback,Anna Mei,Ron Nissim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Formalization in Lean 4 of the free bosonic quantum field theory in 4D Euclidean spacetime with proof of Glimm-Jaffe/Osterwalder-Schrader axioms, demonstrating AI-assisted mathematical physics formalization with community contributions resolving initial assumptions.

在Lean 4中对4维欧氏时空中的自由玻色量子场论进行形式化，并证明了Glimm-Jaffe/Osterwalder-Schrader公理，展示了AI辅助的数学物理形式化方法，并通过社区贡献解决了最初的假设依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To demonstrate that extended arguments in mathematical physics, specifically constructive quantum field theory results, can be translated into machine-checked proofs using AI tools and interactive theorem provers. The work serves as a proof of concept for formalizing complex physics theories while establishing a community-driven approach to resolving dependencies.

证明数学物理中的扩展论证，特别是构造性量子场论的结果，可以使用AI工具和交互式定理证明器转化为机器验证的证明。这项工作作为形式化复杂物理理论的概念验证，同时建立了解决依赖关系的社区驱动方法。

Method: Used Lean 4 interactive theorem prover with Mathlib library. Initially assumed three key mathematical results: Minlos' theorem (Gaussian measures on infinite-dimensional spaces), nuclear property of Schwartz space (topological properties of function spaces), and Goursat's theorem (complex analysis). Later releases incorporated community contributions proving or avoiding these assumptions through formalizations in Lean.

使用Lean 4交互式定理证明器和Mathlib库。最初假设了三个关键的数学结果：Minlos定理（无限维空间上的高斯测度）、Schwartz空间的核性质（函数空间的拓扑性质）和Goursat定理（复分析）。后续版本通过社区贡献，在Lean中证明或避免了这些假设。

Result: Successfully formalized the free bosonic quantum field theory in four-dimensional Euclidean spacetime and proved it satisfies the Glimm-Jaffe axioms (variant of Osterwalder-Schrader axioms). The formalization now stands complete without external assumptions, relying solely on Lean and Mathlib. The project demonstrates the feasibility of AI-assisted formalization for complex physics theories.

成功形式化了四维欧氏时空中的自由玻色量子场论，并证明了其满足Glimm-Jaffe公理（Osterwalder-Schrader公理的变体）。该形式化现在完全独立于外部假设，仅依赖于Lean和Mathlib。该项目证明了AI辅助形式化复杂物理理论的可行性。

Conclusion: The formalization establishes a significant precedent for using interactive theorem provers and AI tools in theoretical physics. The community-driven resolution of initial assumptions demonstrates the scalability of such approaches. This work suggests a potential future where AI-assisted formalization becomes integral to theoretical physics verification and development.

该形式化建立了在理论物理中使用交互式定理证明器和AI工具的重要先例。对初始假设的社区驱动解决方案展示了这种方法的可扩展性。这项工作预示着AI辅助形式化可能成为理论物理验证和发展的组成部分的未来前景。

Abstract: A foundational result in constructive quantum field theory is the construction of the free bosonic quantum field theory in four-dimensional Euclidean spacetime and the proof that it satisfies the Glimm-Jaffe axioms, a variant of the Osterwalder-Schrader axioms. We present a formalization of this result in the Lean 4 interactive theorem prover. The project is intended as a proof of concept that extended arguments in mathematical physics can be translated into machine-checked proofs using existing AI tools. We begin by introducing interactive theorem proving and constructive quantum field theory, then describe our formalization and the design decisions that shaped it. We also explain the methods we used, including coding assistants, and conclude by considering how AI assisted formalization may influence the future of theoretical physics.
  Our original release assumed three results, Minlos' theorem, the nuclear property of Schwartz space, and Goursat's theorem. In subsequent releases from our group and from contributors from the Lean community, these assumptions have been proven (or avoided), so that the OS/GJ axioms are now proven using only Lean and its library Mathlib.

Conclusion: Conclusion: Successfully extends amplitude-based methods to Einstein-Maxwell theory for binary dynamics, providing complete 2PM results for charged systems. Abstract: We employ one-loop scattering amplitudes in Einstein-Maxwell theory to compute the classical Hamiltonian of a binary system of two charged, non-spinning compact objects. The Hamiltonian is valid to all orders in velocity and up to second post-Minkowskian order (2PM), i.e. $\mathcal{O}(G^2)$. The classical interaction potential is extracted via matching to a non-relativistic classical effective field theory. We also provide the scattering angle at 2PM order. ### [64] [Two-time physics, Carroll symmetry and Jordan algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16276)
*Alexander Kamenshchik,Alessio Marrani,Federica Muscolino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper develops a novel description of Carroll particles (relativistic particles with zero velocity but nonzero energy) using two-time (2T) physics framework, establishing connections between extended phase space symmetries and Freudenthal triple systems over cubic Jordan algebras.

\n\n
本文利用双时间（2T）物理框架开发了一种新颖的卡罗尔粒子（具有零速度但非零能量的相对论粒子）描述方法，建立了扩展相空间对称性与基于立方乔丹代数的Freudenthal三重系统之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Carroll particles represent a fascinating corner of relativistic mechanics where particles have nonzero energy but remain stationary, emerging as a limit where the speed of light goes to zero. The motivation is to provide a unified geometric framework for these unusual relativistic systems using Bars' 2T physics formalism, which offers a higher-dimensional approach that naturally incorporates Carroll symmetries through dimensional reduction and gauge symmetries. Additionally, exploring connections between 2T physics and Freudenthal triple systems reveals deep mathematical structures linking exceptional geometries to relativistic particle dynamics.

\n\n
卡罗尔粒子代表了相对论力学中一个迷人的角落，其中粒子具有非零能量但保持静止，出现在光速趋于零的极限情况下。动机是利用Bars的2T物理形式体系为这些不寻常的相对论系统提供一个统一的几何框架，该框架通过维度约化和规范对称性自然地包含了卡罗尔对称性。此外，探索2T物理与Freudenthal三重系统之间的联系揭示了将例外几何与相对论粒子动力学联系起来的深层数学结构。

Method: The paper employs Bars' 2T physics framework which extends spacetime with one additional time and one additional space dimension. The key methodological innovation is gauging the phase-space symmetry that exchanges generalized coordinates with their conjugate momenta, implementing a Sp(2,R) gauge symmetry in the extended phase space. Both classical and quantum descriptions are developed: classical analysis uses constrained Hamiltonian mechanics with first-class constraints, while quantum treatment involves implementing constraints as operator conditions on wavefunctions. The connection to Freudenthal triple systems is established by constructing these systems over semisimple cubic Jordan algebras, specifically the Lorentzian spin factor, and showing their correspondence with 2T physics phase space structures.

\n\n
本文采用Bars的2T物理框架，该框架通过增加一个额外的时间维度和一个额外的空间维度来扩展时空。关键的方法创新是规范相空间对称性，该对称性交换广义坐标与其共轭动量，在扩展相空间中实现Sp(2,R)规范对称性。开发了经典和量子描述：经典分析使用具有第一类约束的约束哈密顿力学，而量子处理涉及将约束实现为波函数的算子条件。通过在半单立方乔丹代数（特别是洛伦兹旋量因子）上构造这些系统，并展示它们与2T物理相空间结构的对应关系，建立了与Freudenthal三重系统的联系。

Result: The main results include: (1) Derivation of Carroll particle dynamics from 2T physics through dimensional reduction, showing how the Sp(2,R) gauge symmetry in extended phase space produces Carroll symmetries in ordinary spacetime; (2) Complete classical and quantum descriptions of Carroll particles within the 2T framework, including constraint algebras and quantization procedures; (3) Establishment of a precise mathematical correspondence between the extended phase space of 2T physics and Freudenthal triple systems constructed over the Lorentzian spin factor cubic Jordan algebra; (4) Demonstration that these exceptional geometric structures naturally encode Carroll symmetries, providing new insights into the origin of Carroll invariance from higher-dimensional frameworks.

\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 通过维度约化从2T物理推导出卡罗尔粒子动力学，展示了扩展相空间中的Sp(2,R)规范对称性如何在普通时空中产生卡罗尔对称性；(2) 在2T框架内完整的卡罗尔粒子经典和量子描述，包括约束代数量子化程序；(3) 建立了2T物理扩展相空间与基于洛伦兹旋量因子立方乔丹代数构造的Freudenthal三重系统之间的精确数学对应关系；(4) 证明了这些例外几何结构自然地编码了卡罗尔对称性，为从高维框架理解卡罗尔不变性的起源提供了新的见解。

Conclusion: The paper successfully demonstrates that two-time physics provides a natural and unified framework for describing Carroll particles, revealing deep connections between relativistic particle dynamics, exceptional geometries, and extended phase space symmetries. The gauge symmetries in 2T physics naturally give rise to Carroll invariance through dimensional reduction, while the correspondence with Freudenthal triple systems suggests a broader mathematical unification of particle physics with exceptional Jordan algebraic structures. This work opens new directions for understanding constrained relativistic systems and their connections to exceptional geometry and higher-dimensional physics frameworks.

\n\n
本文成功证明双时间物理为描述卡罗尔粒子提供了一个自然而统一的框架，揭示了相对论粒子动力学、例外几何和扩展相空间对称性之间的深层联系。2T物理中的规范对称性通过维度约化自然地产生了卡罗尔不变性，而与Freudenthal三重系统的对应关系表明粒子物理与例外乔丹代数结构之间存在更广泛的数学统一。这项工作为理解约束相对论系统及其与例外几何和高维物理框架的联系开辟了新的方向。

Abstract: We describe Carroll particles with nonzero energy (i.e., particles that remain at rest) within the framework of two-time (2T) physics developed by Bars and collaborators. In a spacetime with one additional time and one additional space dimension, one can gauge the phase-space symmetry that exchanges generalized coordinates with their conjugate momenta, thereby unifying the description of apparently different one-time systems. We develop both classical and quantum descriptions of the Carroll particle arising from 2T physics, and explore links between the extended phase space of 2T physics and Freudenthal triple systems constructed over a semisimple cubic Jordan algebra (the Lorentzian spin factor).

### [65] [Krylov Complexity in Supersymmetric Large-$N$ Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16291)
*Eleonora Alfinito,Matteo Beccaria*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates Krylov complexity in the Veneziano-Wosiek model, revealing oscillatory behavior for λ≠1 and quadratic growth K(t)∼t² at the critical coupling λ=1, with a companion rank-1 modified model providing exact analytical solutions showing polynomial growth ∼t²ᴹ for degree-M Krylov complexities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Krylov complexity has become a valuable diagnostic tool for operator growth in quantum many-body systems and holographic contexts. Understanding its behavior in non-trivial quantum mechanical models with supersymmetry, large-N limits, and critical transitions is crucial for developing a more comprehensive framework for quantum complexity.

Method: The study analyzes Krylov complexity $K(t)$ in the Veneziano-Wosiek model, a supersymmetric matrix quantum mechanical model with large-$N$ planar limit and weak-strong duality. Numerical computations are performed starting from selected states in fermion number 0 and 1 sectors related by supersymmetry. A companion model with rank-1 modification of the Hamiltonian is introduced, admitting explicit supercharges, which enables exact analytical computation of Krylov complexity to corroborate numerical findings.

Result: For λ≠1, Krylov complexity $K(t)$ exhibits oscillatory behavior. At the critical coupling λ=1, $K(t)$ grows quadratically: $K(t)∼t^2$ with amplitudes depending on the fermion sector. Higher degree-$M$ Krylov complexities grow polynomially: $K_M(t)∼t^{2M}$ at λ=1. The companion model's exact solutions confirm this behavior. The critical dynamics are analogous to the spreading of a localized squeezed state in a 1D quantum harmonic oscillator with frequency ω, where the free limit ω→0 corresponds to λ→1.

Conclusion: The work demonstrates that Krylov complexity serves as a sensitive probe of critical behavior in supersymmetric matrix quantum mechanics. The quadratic growth at λ=1 indicates ballistic operator spreading at the critical point, contrasting with oscillatory behavior away from criticality. The exact solvability of the rank-1 modified model provides a controlled testing ground for complexity diagnostics in strongly coupled systems. The analogy to quantum harmonic oscillator dynamics suggests deeper connections between Krylov complexity and squeezed state physics.

Abstract: Krylov complexity has recently emerged as a useful probe of operator growth and quantum dynamics in many-body systems and holographic dualities. In this paper we study its behavior in the Veneziano--Wosiek model, a supersymmetric matrix quantum mechanical model admitting a large-$N$ planar limit with manifest weak-strong duality and a critical transition at the 't Hooft coupling $λ=1$. Starting from selected states in the sectors with fermion number 0 and 1, related by supersymmetry, we analyze the time dependence of the numerical complexity. For $λ\neq1$ the Krylov complexity $K(t)$ exhibits oscillatory behavior, while at the critical coupling $λ=1$ it grows quadratically in time, $K(t)\sim t^2$, with sector-dependent amplitudes. To obtain analytical insight, we study a companion model defined by a rank-1 modification of the Veneziano--Wosiek Hamiltonian, which admits explicit supercharges. In this model the Krylov complexity can be computed exactly and reproduces the behavior observed in the original model. Higher degree-$M$ Krylov complexities, defined as expectation values of powers of Lanczos index, are also computed and grow polynomially in time $\sim t^{2M}$ at the critical point in both models. This behavior is closely analogous to the spreading of a localized squeezed state in a one-dimensional quantum harmonic oscillator of frequency $ω$, with the free limit $ω\to 0$ corresponding to the critical $λ\to 1$ limit.

</details>


### [66] [Gravitational Metric of a Star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16493)
*Poul H. Damgaard,Hojin Lee,Kanghoon Lee,Tabasum Rahnuma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop a systematic perturbative framework for stationary vacuum spacetime solutions in general relativity, employing multipole expansions and post-Minkowskian perturbation theory. Using de Donder gauge, we derive the metric outside matter sources to second post-Minkowskian order, expressed via tensor bubble integrals. The formalism recovers Kerr black hole solutions and enables construction of Kerr-like stellar metrics through multipole tuning, while addressing gauge ambiguities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to systematically construct stationary vacuum spacetime solutions in general relativity for localized matter sources, particularly stars. Traditional approaches often rely on specific symmetry assumptions or numerical methods. This work develops a perturbative framework combining multipole expansions and post-Minkowskian perturbation theory to obtain explicit analytic expressions for the metric outside arbitrary stationary sources, bridging the gap between exact black hole solutions and realistic stellar models.

论文旨在为广义相对论中局域化物质源（特别是恒星）的系统性构建稳态真空时空解。传统方法通常依赖于特定的对称性假设或数值方法。这项工作开发了一个结合多极展开和后闵可夫斯基扰动理论的微扰框架，以获得任意稳态源外部度规的显式解析表达式，架起精确黑洞解与真实恒星模型之间的桥梁。

Method: The methodology employs a double expansion: post-Minkowskian expansion in Newton's constant $G$ (perturbation around Minkowski spacetime) and multipole expansion of the source. The metric ansatz is $g_{\mu\nu} = \eta_{\mu\nu} + h_{\mu\nu}^{(1)} + h_{\mu\nu}^{(2)} + \cdots$, with $h_{\mu\nu}^{(n)} \sim G^n$. The source is characterized by its infinite set of mass multipoles $M_{L}$ and current multipoles $S_{L}$, where $L$ represents multi-index notation. Using de Donder gauge condition $\partial^{\mu}\bar{h}_{\mu\nu}=0$ (with $\bar{h}_{\mu\nu}=h_{\mu\nu}-\frac{1}{2}\eta_{\mu\nu}h$), the Einstein equations are solved recursively. At second post-Minkowskian order, the solution is expressed in terms of generalized tensor bubble integrals in momentum space, facilitating analytic continuation to any multipole order. The inverse-distance expansion yields explicit coordinate-space expressions.

该方法采用双重展开：牛顿常数$G$的后闵可夫斯基展开（围绕闵可夫斯基时空的微扰）和源的多极展开。度规设定为$g_{\mu\nu} = \eta_{\mu\nu} + h_{\mu\nu}^{(1)} + h_{\mu\nu}^{(2)} + \cdots$，其中$h_{\mu\nu}^{(n)} \sim G^n$。源通过其无限质量多极矩$M_{L}$和电流多极矩$S_{L}$表征，其中$L$表示多重指标符号。利用de Donder规范条件$\partial^{\mu}\bar{h}_{\mu\nu}=0$（其中$\bar{h}_{\mu\nu}=h_{\mu\nu}-\frac{1}{2}\eta_{\mu\nu}h$），递归求解爱因斯坦场方程。在二阶后闵可夫斯基阶，解以动量空间中的广义张量气泡积分表示，便于解析延拓至任意多极阶。逆距离展开产生显式的坐标空间表达式。

Result: The main result is an explicit perturbative metric solution valid to $O(G^2)$ for arbitrary stationary sources: $h_{\mu\nu} = h_{\mu\nu}^{(1)} + h_{\mu\nu}^{(2)} + \cdots$, where $h_{\mu\nu}^{(1)}$ contains linearized multipole contributions and $h_{\mu\nu}^{(2)}$ involves nonlinear interactions. The solution is expressed through generalized bubble integrals: $I_{L}^{\mu\nu}(r) = \int \frac{d^3k}{(2\pi)^3} e^{i\vec{k}\cdot\vec{r}} \frac{k_{L}}{|\vec{k}|^4} \mathcal{T}^{\mu\nu}(\vec{k})$, where $\mathcal{T}^{\mu\nu}$ encodes source multipole structure. In the special limit where multipoles satisfy the Kerr relations $M_{l} = M(ia)^{l}$ and $S_{l} = M(ia)^{l}$ (with $a$ representing spin parameter), the metric reduces to the Kerr solution up to $O(G^2)$. By slightly deviating from these specific multipole relations, one obtains Kerr-like metrics describing stars rather than black holes. The work also identifies a subtle gauge ambiguity in de Donder gauge related to residual coordinate freedom at second order.

主要结果是针对任意稳态源、有效至$O(G^2)$的显式微扰度规解：$h_{\mu\nu} = h_{\mu\nu}^{(1)} + h_{\mu\nu}^{(2)} + \cdots$，其中$h_{\mu\nu}^{(1)}$包含线性化多极贡献，$h_{\mu\nu}^{(2)}$涉及非线性相互作用。解通过广义气泡积分表示：$I_{L}^{\mu\nu}(r) = \int \frac{d^3k}{(2\pi)^3} e^{i\vec{k}\cdot\vec{r}} \frac{k_{L}}{|\vec{k}|^4} \mathcal{T}^{\mu\nu}(\vec{k})$，其中$\mathcal{T}^{\mu\nu}$编码源多极结构。在多极矩满足克尔关系$M_{l} = M(ia)^{l}$和$S_{l} = M(ia)^{l}$（$a$表示自旋参数）的特殊极限下，度规简化为直至$O(G^2)$的克尔解。通过略微偏离这些特定多极关系，获得描述恒星而非黑洞的类克尔度规。该工作还识别了de Donder规范中与二阶残余坐标自由度相关的微妙规范模糊性。

Conclusion: This work establishes a systematic perturbative framework for constructing stationary vacuum spacetimes in general relativity, providing explicit analytic control over multipole structure and nonlinear gravitational interactions. The formalism bridges exact black hole solutions with realistic stellar models through controlled multipole deviations. The identification of gauge ambiguities in de Donder gauge highlights subtleties in perturbation theory at higher orders. This approach offers powerful tools for precision gravitational physics, including tests of general relativity, gravitational wave modeling for neutron stars, and investigations of exotic compact objects beyond black holes.

这项工作建立了在广义相对论中构建稳态真空时空的系统微扰框架，提供了对多极结构和非线性引力相互作用的显式解析控制。该形式体系通过受控的多极偏离，架起了精确黑洞解与真实恒星模型之间的桥梁。de Donder规范中规范模糊性的识别凸显了高阶扰动理论中的微妙之处。该方法为精密引力物理学提供了强大工具，包括广义相对论检验、中子星引力波建模以及对黑洞之外奇异致密天体的研究。

Abstract: Solving the classical equations of motion in general relativity recursively, we consider the metric of a spatially localized and stationary source of matter. Having in mind a star of general composition, we characterize it by means of its infinite set of mass and current multipoles. Specializing to de Donder gauge we set up the recursive equations that produce the metric outside the star to any desired order in perturbation theory, expanded both in Newton's constant and in the order of multipoles. Up to second post-Minkowskian order we express the result to any order in the multipole expansion in terms of generalized (tensor) bubble integrals in momentum space and a corresponding simple expansion in inverse distances. In a special corner of the space of multipoles we recover the Kerr black hole solution to the given order. By tweaking just slightly the multipoles away from the Kerr limit the metric will describe stars that are Kerr-like and yet are not black holes. A subtlety with respect to the gauge ambiguity of de Donder gauge is also pointed out.

</details>

*Mark Raugas*

TL;DR: We explore connections between non-commutative Hodge structures, quiver gauge theories on cubic fourfolds, and semiorthogonal decompositions, proposing that K3 Hodge atoms represent protected quantum phases invariant under non-perturbative tunneling.

Method: Comparative analysis of algebraic and analytic frameworks for birational invariants. Application of non-commutative Hodge theory to quiver gauge field theory on cubic fourfolds. Interpretation of semiorthogonal property as dynamical selection rule.

Result: The K3 Hodge atom of cubic fourfold emerges as central object. Conjecture: this Hodge atom represents protected quantum phase whose spectra remain invariant under non-perturbative tunneling processes, connecting algebraic geometry to quantum field theory.

Abstract: We compare algebraic and analytic pictures relevant to the study of birational invariants. Motivated by recent advances in the development of non-commutative Hodge structures, we examine their implication for quiver gauge field theory on the cubic fourfold. ### [68] [Novel cluster-algebraic letters for 5- and 6-point QCD processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16743)
*Rigers Aliaj,Garbriele Dian,Georgios Papathanasiou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: [The paper demonstrates how breaking dual conformal invariance allows translation of cluster-algebraic predictions from 9-point amplitudes in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM to 5- and 6-point QCD processes, revealing nested square roots in massive kinematics and identifying novel letters that may appear at higher loops.]

\n\n
[本文展示了如何通过打破对偶共形不变性，将$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中9点振幅的簇代数预测转换到5点和6点QCD过程，揭示了质量运动学中的嵌套平方根，并识别了可能在更高圈数中出现的新字母。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation stems from leveraging the rich mathematical structure of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory—particularly its amplituhedron and cluster-algebraic descriptions—to gain insights into the more complex algebraic structures of QCD amplitudes. By breaking the dual conformal invariance inherent to planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM, one can systematically relate predictions for symbol alphabets to those for QCD processes with fewer external legs but potentially massive kinematics.]

\n\n
[动机源于利用$\mathcal{N}=4$超杨-米尔斯理论的丰富数学结构——特别是其amplituhedron和簇代数描述——来深入理解更复杂的QCD振幅代数结构。通过打破平面$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM固有的对偶共形不变性，可以系统地将符号字母表的预测与具有较少外腿但可能包含质量运动学的QCD过程联系起来。]

Method: [The core method involves breaking the dual conformal invariance of cluster-algebraic predictions derived for 9-point amplitudes in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM. This breaking procedure transforms these predictions into analogous candidate symbol alphabets for QCD processes with fewer external points (5- and 6-point). For the 6-point case with one massive external leg, this yields the first systematic prediction of candidate letters, which are then compared against known structures: (1) all 1-loop integrals with the same kinematics, (2) the recently computed alphabet of finite, planar 2-loop amplitudes for massless 6-point QCD processes, and (3) identification of additional letters that may appear at higher loops. A similar procedure is applied to 5-point 2-mass processes, with cross-checking against existing literature.]

\n\n
[核心方法涉及打破针对平面$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中9点振幅导出的簇代数预测的对偶共形不变性。这一打破过程将这些预测转换为具有较少外点（5点和6点）的QCD过程的类似候选符号字母表。对于具有一个质量外腿的6点情况，这产生了第一个系统性的候选字母预测，随后与已知结构进行比较：(1)具有相同运动学的所有单圈积分，(2)最近计算的无质量6点QCD过程的有限平面双圈振幅字母表，以及(3)识别可能在更高圈数中出现的额外字母。类似的方法也应用于5点双质量过程，并与现有文献进行交叉验证。]

Result: [1. For 6-point QCD processes with one massive external leg: first systematic prediction of candidate letters, which surprisingly contain nested square roots—a feature not typically expected for such amplitudes. These candidate letters essentially contain the alphabet of all 1-loop integrals with these kinematics.

2. In the massless limit: the predicted alphabet contains the recently computed alphabet of finite, planar 2-loop amplitudes for 6-point massless QCD processes, plus an additional 162 letters that may appear at higher loops.

3. For 5-point 2-mass processes: production of candidate letters via the same method, revealing nontrivial overlap with existing literature that includes new letters not previously identified.

4. The breaking of dual conformal invariance provides a systematic map from the cluster algebra of planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM to the more complicated algebraic structures of QCD amplitudes with massive legs.]

\n\n
[1. 对于具有一个质量外腿的6点QCD过程：首次系统预测候选字母，这些字母令人惊讶地包含嵌套平方根——这种特征通常不为此类振幅所预期。这些候选字母基本上包含了具有这些运动学的所有单圈积分的字母表。

2. 在无质量极限下：预测的字母表包含了最近计算的无质量6点QCD过程的有限平面双圈振幅字母表，外加162个可能在更高圈数中出现的额外字母。

3. 对于5点双质量过程：通过相同方法生成候选字母，揭示了与现有文献的非平凡重叠，其中包括先前未识别的新字母。

4. 对偶共形不变性的打破提供了一个系统映射，从平面$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM的簇代数到具有质量外腿的QCD振幅的更复杂代数结构。]

Conclusion: [The work establishes a powerful connection between the mathematical structures of maximally supersymmetric gauge theory and realistic QCD amplitudes through controlled breaking of dual conformal symmetry. The appearance of nested square roots in massive 6-point kinematics suggests richer algebraic structures than previously anticipated for such processes. The identification of 162 additional letters in the massless 6-point case indicates that higher-loop amplitudes in QCD may involve significantly more complicated symbol alphabets than those currently known. The methodology provides a systematic framework for predicting symbol alphabets for QCD amplitudes by leveraging the well-understood cluster-algebraic structure of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM.]

\n\n
[这项工作通过对偶共形对称性的受控打破，在最大超对称规范理论的数学结构与现实QCD振幅之间建立了强有力的联系。质量6点运动学中嵌套平方根的出现表明，此类过程的代数结构比先前预期的更为丰富。在无质量6点情况下识别出的162个额外字母表明，QCD中的更高圈振幅可能涉及比目前已知的显著更复杂的符号字母表。该方法通过利用$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM的充分理解的簇代数结构，为预测QCD振幅的符号字母表提供了一个系统框架。]

Abstract: By breaking dual conformal invariance, we transform cluster-algebraic predictions for the alphabet of 9-point amplitudes in $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory to analogous predictions for 5- and 6-point processes in QCD. We start by obtaining, for the first time, candidate letters for 6-point processes with one massive external leg, and discover that they surprisingly also contain nested square roots. We confirm that our results essentially contain the alphabet of all 1-loop integrals with these kinematics, and in their massless limit also the recently computed alphabet of finite, planar 2-loop amplitudes for 6-point massless QCD processes. In the latter case, we additionally find 162 letters that may appear at higher loops. We similarly produce candidate letters for 5-point 2-mass processes, whose comparison with the literature reveals a nontrivial overlap that also includes new letters.

</details>
